// ── Framer-Motion mock (renders without animations) ──
const *forwardRef = (tag) => {
return function MotionComp({ children, style, animate, initial, exit, transition, whileTap, whileHover, drag, dragConstraints, dragElastic, onDragEnd, layout, layoutId, variants, …props }) {
return React.createElement(tag, { style, …props }, children);
};
};
const motion = new Proxy({}, { get: (*, tag) => _forwardRef(tag) });
const AnimatePresence = ({ children }) => <>{children}</>;
const useMotionValue = (init) => { const [v] = useState(init); return { get: () => v, set: () => {} }; };
const useTransform = (mv, inp, out) => ({ get: () => out[0] });

const s = document.createElement(“style”);
s.id = “m3-spin”;
s.textContent = “@keyframes spin{to{transform:rotate(360deg)}} .m3-spin{animation:spin 0.7s linear infinite}”;
document.head.appendChild(s);
}

/* ── iOS / Android viewport & overscroll fix ── */
if (typeof document !== “undefined” && !document.getElementById(“m3-viewport”)) {
const s = document.createElement(“style”);
s.id = “m3-viewport”;
s.textContent = [
“*, *::before, *::after { box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; }”,
“html, body { height: 100%; overflow: hidden; overscroll-behavior: none; }”,
“body { margin: 0; padding: 0; }”,
“input, textarea, select { font-size: 16px !important; }”,
“button { -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; }”,
].join(” “);
document.head.appendChild(s);
}

const GA = (id) => AREAS.find((a) => a.id === id);

// Bridge: AREAS uses slightly different IDs than ITEM_AREAS
// (e.g. “finances” vs “finance”). This maps wheel IDs to item IDs.
const AREA_BRIDGE = { finances:“finance”, personal:“learning”, environment:“home” };
function normalizeAreaId(id) { return AREA_BRIDGE[id] || id; }
// Resolve color/name from either system
function resolveArea(id) {
const normalized = normalizeAreaId(id);
const ia = ITEM_AREAS[normalized];
const la = GA(id);
return { c: ia?.c || la?.c || T.brand, n: ia?.n || la?.n || id, e: ia?.e || “” };
}

function AreaIcon({ area, size = 20, color }) {
const c = color || area.c;
return (
<svg width={size} height={size} viewBox=“0 0 24 24” fill=“none”
stroke={c} strokeWidth={1.7} strokeLinecap=“round” strokeLinejoin=“round”
style={{ color: c }}>
{AREA_ICONS[area.icon]}
</svg>
);
}

function getCommitted(progId) { return COMMITTED.find(c => c.id === progId); }
function getAreaPrograms(areaId) {
// Include journeys where this area is primary OR secondary
return COMMITTED.filter(c => {
const p = PRG.find(x => x.id === c.id);
return p && (p.a === areaId || (p.sa || []).includes(areaId));
}).map(c => ({ …c, …PRG.find(x => x.id === c.id) }));
}
function getAvailablePrograms(areaId) {
const committed = COMMITTED.map(c => c.id);
// Available = not committed AND primary area matches (secondary-only journeys show in their primary area)
return PRG.filter(p => p.a === areaId && !committed.includes(p.id));
}

/* ═══ DAILY ACTIONS (enriched) ═══ */
/* ═══ DYNAMIC TODAY ACTIONS — unified pipeline from all sources ═══ */
const TIME_ORDER = { morning: 0, afternoon: 1, evening: 2, anytime: 3 };

function inferTimeOfDay(action) {
// If explicitly set, use it
if (action.timeOfDay && action.timeOfDay !== “anytime”) return action.timeOfDay;
// Heuristic: exercise/meditation → morning, reflection/journal → evening
const t = (action.title || “”).toLowerCase();
if (/meditat|stretch|wake|morning|sunlight|exercise|workout/i.test(t)) return “morning”;
if (/journal|reflect|review|wind|bed|sleep|evening|night/i.test(t)) return “evening”;
return “afternoon”;
}

function getTodayActions() {
const actions = [];
const today = new Date();
const activePrograms = COMMITTED.filter(c => c.status === “active”);

// ── SOURCE 1: Journey actions from COMMITTED ──
activePrograms.forEach(committed => {
const prg = PRG.find(p => p.id === committed.id);
if (!prg) return;
const area = GA(prg.a);
const weekIdx = (committed.week || 1) - 1;
const dayIdx = (committed.day || 1) - 1;
const weekTitle = prg.wp?.[weekIdx] || `Week ${committed.week}`;

```
// Source 1a: COMMITTED weeks data
if (committed.weeks?.length > 0) {
  const weekData = committed.weeks[weekIdx];
  if (weekData) {
    const dayData = weekData.days?.[dayIdx % weekData.days.length];
    if (dayData) {
      dayData.actions.forEach((actionText, i) => {
        actions.push({
          id: `${committed.id}-w${committed.week}-d${committed.day}-${i}`,
          title: actionText, description: "", duration: 15,
          timeOfDay: inferTimeOfDay({ title: actionText }),
          category: weekTitle, icon: "check", type: "journey",
          program: committed.id, area: prg.a,
          weekTitle, dayTitle: dayData.title,
          weekNum: committed.week, dayNum: committed.day, totalWeeks: prg.w,
          sourceEmoji: ICONS[committed.id] || "📘", sourceTitle: prg.t,
        });
      });
      return;
    }
  }
}

// Source 1b: WA data (weekly action sets)
const waData = WA[committed.id];
if (waData && waData[weekIdx]) {
  const weekActions = waData[weekIdx];
  weekActions.forEach((wa, i) => {
    const durMins = parseDurationMins(wa.dur);
    actions.push({
      id: `${committed.id}-w${committed.week}-wa-${i}`,
      title: wa.t, description: wa.desc, duration: durMins || 15,
      timeOfDay: inferTimeOfDay({ title: wa.t }),
      category: weekTitle, icon: "check", type: "journey",
      program: committed.id, area: prg.a,
      weekTitle, dayTitle: prg.wp?.[weekIdx] || `Day ${committed.day}`,
      weekNum: committed.week, dayNum: committed.day, totalWeeks: prg.w,
      sourceEmoji: ICONS[committed.id] || "📘", sourceTitle: prg.t,
    });
  });
}
```

});

// ── SOURCE 2: Project steps scheduled for today (items with steps) ──
ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && i.steps?.length > 0).forEach(item => {
item.steps.filter(s => s.today && !s.done).forEach(step => {
const subDone = step.subtasks?.filter(st => st.done).length || 0;
const subTotal = step.subtasks?.length || 0;
actions.push({
id: step.id, title: step.title, description: step.description || “”,
duration: step.duration || 15,
timeOfDay: step.timeOfDay || inferTimeOfDay({ title: step.title }),
category: item.title, icon: “check”, type: “project”,
projectId: item.id, projectTitle: item.title,
projectEmoji: item.emoji, projectColor: ITEM_AREAS[item.area]?.c || item.color,
projectDeadline: item.deadline,
sourceEmoji: item.emoji, sourceTitle: item.title,
subtasksDone: subDone, subtasksTotal: subTotal,
assignees: step.assignees || [],
assignee: step.assignee,
priority: step.priority || “normal”,
effort:   step.effort   || “medium”,
status:   step.status   || “todo”,
blockedBy: step.blockedBy || [],
});
});
});

// ── SOURCE 3: Recurring items (habits) matching today’s schedule ──
ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && i.recurrence).forEach(item => {
if (matchesRecurrence(item.recurrence, today)) {
actions.push({
id: `habit-${item.id}-${today.toISOString().slice(0,10)}`,
title: item.title, description: formatRecurrence(item.recurrence),
duration: item.habitDuration || 15,
timeOfDay: item.habitTimeOfDay || “morning”,
category: “Habits”, icon: “check”, type: “habit”,
habitId: item.id,
sourceEmoji: item.emoji, sourceTitle: item.title,
isHabit: true,
});
}
});

// ── SOURCE 4: Standalone actions (no steps, no recurrence) ──
ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && !i.steps?.length && !i.recurrence).forEach(item => {
actions.push({
id: `task-${item.id}`,
title: item.title, description: “”,
duration: item.taskDuration || 15,
timeOfDay: item.taskTimeOfDay || “anytime”,
category: “To-Do”, icon: “check”, type: “action”,
taskId: item.id,
sourceEmoji: item.emoji, sourceTitle: item.title,
});
});

// Sort by time of day
actions.sort((a, b) => (TIME_ORDER[a.timeOfDay] || 3) - (TIME_ORDER[b.timeOfDay] || 3));
return actions;
}

/* Group today’s actions by source (program or project) for dashboard */
function groupActionsBySource(actions) {
const groups = [];
const programGroups = {};
const projectGroups = {};

actions.forEach(a => {
if (a.type === “project”) {
if (!projectGroups[a.projectId]) {
const proj = getUserProjects().find(p => p.id === a.projectId);
const totalTasks = proj?.steps.length || 0;
const doneTasks = proj?.steps.filter(t => t.done).length || 0;
projectGroups[a.projectId] = {
type: “project”, sourceId: a.projectId,
title: a.projectTitle, emoji: a.projectEmoji,
color: a.projectColor, deadline: a.projectDeadline,
totalTasks, doneTasks, actions: [],
};
}
projectGroups[a.projectId].actions.push(a);
} else {
if (!programGroups[a.program]) {
const prg = PRG.find(p => p.id === a.program);
const area = GA(a.area);
programGroups[a.program] = {
type: “journey”, sourceId: a.program,
program: prg, area,
title: prg?.t, emoji: ICONS[a.program] || “\u2728”,
color: area?.c || T.brand,
weekTitle: a.weekTitle, dayTitle: a.dayTitle,
weekNum: a.weekNum, dayNum: a.dayNum, totalWeeks: a.totalWeeks,
actions: [],
};
}
programGroups[a.program].actions.push(a);
}
});

// Journeys first, then projects
groups.push(…Object.values(programGroups));
groups.push(…Object.values(projectGroups));
return groups;
}

/* Parse duration string to minutes (e.g. “5 min” → 5, “1 hr” → 60, “2 hrs” → 120) */
function parseDurationMins(dur) {
if (!dur) return 0;
const s = dur.toLowerCase().trim();
const numMatch = s.match(/(\d+)/);
if (!numMatch) return 0;
const n = parseInt(numMatch[1]);
if (s.includes(“hr”)) return n * 60;
if (s.includes(“min”)) return n;
return n; // assume minutes
}

/* Is this action a “quick win” (under 5 minutes)? */
function isQuickWin(action) {
const dur = action.duration;
if (!dur) return false;
if (typeof dur === “number”) return dur > 0 && dur <= 5;
const mins = parseDurationMins(dur);
return mins > 0 && mins <= 5;
}

/* Group today’s actions by time of day for the new timeline view */
function groupByTimeOfDay(actions) {
const groups = {
morning: { id: “morning”, label: “Morning”, icon: “sun”, actions: [], totalMins: 0 },
afternoon: { id: “afternoon”, label: “Afternoon”, icon: “sunCloud”, actions: [], totalMins: 0 },
evening: { id: “evening”, label: “Evening”, icon: “moon”, actions: [], totalMins: 0 },
anytime: { id: “anytime”, label: “Anytime”, icon: “inbox”, actions: [], totalMins: 0 },
};
actions.forEach(a => {
const tod = a.timeOfDay || “anytime”;
const g = groups[tod] || groups.anytime;
g.actions.push(a);
g.totalMins += (typeof a.duration === “number” ? a.duration : parseDurationMins(a.duration)) || 0;
});
return Object.values(groups).filter(g => g.actions.length > 0);
}

/* Smart session picker: selects priority items for guided swipe session */
function pickSessionActions(allActions, statuses, starred) {
const MAX_SESSION = 5;
const starSet = starred || new Set();
const pending = allActions.filter(a => !statuses[a.id]);
const deferred = allActions.filter(a => statuses[a.id] === “deferred”);
const pool = […deferred, …pending.filter(a => !deferred.find(d => d.id === a.id))];

// Priority tiers:
// 1. User-starred items (always first)
// 2. Deferred/snoozed (user saw these, bring back)
// 3. Quick wins (<= 5 min) for momentum
// 4. Interleave remaining across sources

const starredItems = pool.filter(a => starSet.has(a.id));
const rest = pool.filter(a => !starSet.has(a.id));

const deferredRest = rest.filter(a => statuses[a.id] === “deferred”);
const pendingRest = rest.filter(a => !statuses[a.id]);

const quickWins = pendingRest.filter(a => isQuickWin(a)).slice(0, 2);
const remaining = pendingRest.filter(a => !quickWins.includes(a));

// Interleave remaining across different sources
const sourceMap = {};
[…deferredRest, …remaining].forEach(a => {
const key = a.type === “project” ? `proj-${a.projectId}` : `prog-${a.program}`;
if (!sourceMap[key]) sourceMap[key] = [];
sourceMap[key].push(a);
});
const interleaved = [];
const sources = Object.values(sourceMap);
let idx = 0;
const needed = MAX_SESSION - starredItems.length - quickWins.length;
while (interleaved.length < needed && sources.some(s => s.length > 0)) {
const src = sources[idx % sources.length];
if (src.length > 0) interleaved.push(src.shift());
idx++;
}

return […starredItems, …quickWins, …interleaved].slice(0, MAX_SESSION);
}

{ value:4, label:“Good”, emoji:“smile”, color:”#34C759” },
{ value:5, label:“Great”, emoji:“smile”, color:”#30D158” },
];

/* ═══ UNIFIED ITEMS MODEL ═══ */
/* Everything is an Item. No user-facing types. AI classifies by setting properties.
Behavior is determined by properties, not categories:

┌─────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ Has steps?   → It’s a PROJECT (multi-step goal with progress)     │
│ Has recurring?→ It’s a HABIT (repeats, tracks streaks/consistency)│
│ Neither?     → It’s an ACTION (one-off thing to do)               │
│ status=someday → It’s a GOAL (aspirational, links to projects/journeys)         │
│ source=journey → It came from an expert-designed Journey          │
└─────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

Item {
id, title, emoji, area, color, status, source
steps: […] | undefined        // → project behavior
recurring: { type, days } | undefined  // → habit behavior
duration, timeOfDay, deadline   // scheduling
graduatedFrom: journeyId | undefined  // journey→habit graduation
pausedAt: ISO date | undefined  // when item was paused (for nudge logic)
createdAt, completedAt          // lifecycle timestamps
}

STATUS LIFECYCLE (4 statuses):
┌─────────┐     ┌────────┐     ┌──────┐
│ someday │────→│ active │────→│ done │
└─────────┘     └───┬────┘     └──────┘
│  ↑
┌───↓──┴───┐
│  paused  │
└──────────┘

someday  = Goal — aspirational, can link projects/journeys → Goals tab
active   = Committed, generating Today actions → Active tab + Today view
paused   = Was active, temporarily on hold (streak frozen, hidden from Today) → Active tab (dimmed)
done     = Completed → Profile/archive

source: “self” | “journey”
area: health | home | career | finance | learning | relationships | fun
*/

/* Derive display kind from properties (never stored, always computed) */
/* Note: paused items retain their kind (habit/project/action) — paused is a status, not a kind */
function itemKind(item) {
if (item.status === “someday”) return “goal”;
if (item.recurring || item.recurrence) return “habit”;
if (item.steps?.length > 0) return “project”;
return “action”;
}

/* Is the item currently generating Today actions? */
function isItemActive(item) {
return item.status === “active”;
}

/* Is the item on hold? */
function isItemPaused(item) {
return item.status === “paused”;
}

/* ═══ RECURRENCE ENGINE ═══ */
function matchesRecurrence(recurrence, date) {
if (!recurrence) return false;
const dow = date.getDay(); // 0=Sun, 1=Mon…
const dayNames = [“sun”,“mon”,“tue”,“wed”,“thu”,“fri”,“sat”];
switch (recurrence.type) {
case “daily”: return true;
case “weekdays”: return dow >= 1 && dow <= 5;
case “specific_days”: return (recurrence.days || []).includes(dayNames[dow]);
case “interval”:
if (!recurrence.startDate) return true;
const start = new Date(recurrence.startDate);
const diff = Math.floor((date - start) / 86400000);
return diff >= 0 && diff % (recurrence.interval || 7) === 0;
case “monthly”:
return date.getDate() === (recurrence.monthDay || 1);
default: return false;
}
}

function formatRecurrence(recurrence) {
if (!recurrence) return “”;
switch (recurrence.type) {
case “daily”: return “Every day”;
case “weekdays”: return “Weekdays”;
case “specific_days”: return (recurrence.days || []).map(d => d.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + d.slice(1, 3)).join(”, “);
case “interval”: return `Every ${recurrence.interval} days`;
case “monthly”: return `Monthly on the ${recurrence.monthDay || 1}${["st","nd","rd"][((recurrence.monthDay||1)-1)%10]||"th"}`;
default: return “”;
}
}

function formatDuration(mins) {
if (!mins) return “”;
if (mins < 60) return `${mins}m`;
const h = Math.floor(mins / 60);
const m = mins % 60;
return m > 0 ? `${h}h ${m}m` : `${h}h`;
}

/* Helper: get items by status/kind (property-driven, no type field) */
function getActiveItems() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active”); }
function getPausedItems() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “paused”); }
function getSomedayItems() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “someday”); }
function getDoneItems() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “done”); }
function getItemsByArea(area) {
return ITEMS.filter(i => (i.status === “active” || i.status === “paused”) &&
(i.area === area || (i.secondaryAreas || []).includes(area)));
}
function getProjectItems() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && i.steps?.length > 0); }
function getHabitItems() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && i.recurrence); }
function getActionItems() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && !i.steps?.length && !i.recurrence); }

/* Area definitions with expanded set */
const ITEM_AREAS = {

function getUserProjects() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.source === “self” && i.status === “active” && i.steps?.length > 0); }
function getUserDreams() { return ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “someday”); }

/* ═══ FRACTIONAL PROGRESS ENGINE ═══
Task progress = subtask completion ratio (fractional)
Task done status = all subtasks complete (binary)
Project progress = average of all task progress
Goal progress = average of linked item progress
*/
function taskProgress(step) {
if (step.done) return 1;
if (!step.subtasks || step.subtasks.length === 0) return 0;
return step.subtasks.filter(st => st.done).length / step.subtasks.length;
}

function projectProgress(item) {
const steps = item.steps;
if (!steps || steps.length === 0) return 0;
return steps.reduce((sum, s) => sum + taskProgress(s), 0) / steps.length;
}

function journeyProgress(committed) {
if (!committed) return 0;
const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === committed.id);
if (!prog) return 0;
return Math.min(1, committed.week / prog.w);
}

/* ═══ APP SCORE ENGINE ═══
Computes an objective activity-based score (1–10) for a life area.

MULTI-CATEGORY WEIGHTED FORMULA:
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Each item/journey can contribute to multiple areas with
diminishing weights per area role:
Primary area   → 1.0× contribution  (full)
Secondary (1st)→ 0.5× contribution  (meaningful spillover)
Secondary (2nd)→ 0.25× contribution (minor spillover)

This prevents score inflation from cross-category items while
still crediting real multi-area benefit.

Item contribution values (before area weighting):
Journey (active)   → 1.5 base + up to 2.5 for progress
Journey (completed)→ 1.0 (lasting benefit)
Habit (active)     → 0.8 (consistency signal)
Project (active)   → 0.4 base + up to 1.2 for completion
*/

// Returns area weight for an item: 1.0 / 0.5 / 0.25 / 0 (not applicable)
function areaWeight(item, areaId) {
const normId = normalizeAreaId(areaId);
const primary = normalizeAreaId(item.area);
const secondary = (item.secondaryAreas || []).map(normalizeAreaId);
if (primary === normId) return 1.0;
const secIdx = secondary.indexOf(normId);
if (secIdx === 0) return 0.5;
if (secIdx === 1) return 0.25;
return 0;
}

// Same for journeys (stored in PRG as p.a + p.sa)
function journeyAreaWeight(prog, areaId) {
if (!prog) return 0;
if (prog.a === areaId) return 1.0;
const sa = prog.sa || [];
const secIdx = sa.indexOf(areaId);
if (secIdx === 0) return 0.5;
if (secIdx === 1) return 0.25;
return 0;
}

function computeAppScore(areaId) {
let points = 0;

// ── Journeys ──
COMMITTED.forEach(c => {
const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === c.id);
if (!prog) return;
const w = journeyAreaWeight(prog, areaId);
if (w === 0) return;
let contribution = 0;
if (c.status === “active”) {
const progress = Math.min(1, c.week / prog.w);
contribution = 1.5 + progress * 2.5;
} else if (c.status === “completed”) {
contribution = 1.0;
}
points += contribution * w;
});

// ── Habits ──
ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && i.recurrence).forEach(item => {
const w = areaWeight(item, areaId);
if (w === 0) return;
points += 0.8 * w;
});

// ── Projects ──
ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “active” && i.steps?.length > 0).forEach(item => {
const w = areaWeight(item, areaId);
if (w === 0) return;
const pp = projectProgress(item);
const contribution = 0.4 + pp * 1.2;
points += contribution * w;
});

// Clamp to 1–10
return Math.max(1, Math.min(10, Math.round((1 + points) * 10) / 10));
}

function appScoreInsight(selfScore, appScore) {
const gap = selfScore - appScore;
if (Math.abs(gap) <= 1) return { type: “aligned”, msg: “Your effort and self-rating are well aligned.” };
if (gap > 1) return { type: “overconfident”, msg: `You rate this ${gap.toFixed(1)} higher than your activity suggests. Are you coasting?` };
return { type: “undervalued”, msg: `You're putting in more work than you give yourself credit for — ${Math.abs(gap).toFixed(1)} points of hidden effort.` };
}

function goalProgress(goal) {
const linkedProjects = (goal.linkedItems || []).map(id => ITEMS.find(i => i.id === id)).filter(Boolean);
const linkedJourneys = (goal.linkedJourneys || []).map(id => {
const c = COMMITTED.find(cc => cc.id === id);
return c ? { type: “journey”, progress: journeyProgress(c) } : null;
}).filter(Boolean);
const allProgress = [
…linkedProjects.map(p => projectProgress(p)),
…linkedJourneys.map(j => j.progress),
];
if (allProgress.length === 0) return 0;
return allProgress.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / allProgress.length;
}

function getGoalLinkedItems(goal) {
const projects = (goal.linkedItems || []).map(id => {
const item = ITEMS.find(i => i.id === id);
return item ? { …item, kind: itemKind(item), progress: projectProgress(item) } : null;
}).filter(Boolean);
const journeys = (goal.linkedJourneys || []).map(id => {
const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === id);
const c = COMMITTED.find(cc => cc.id === id);
return prog ? { id, title: prog.t, area: prog.a, kind: “journey”, progress: c ? journeyProgress(c) : 0, prog, committed: c } : null;
}).filter(Boolean);
return […projects, …journeys];
}

function getUnlinkedItems() {
const linkedIds = new Set();
ITEMS.filter(i => i.status === “someday”).forEach(g => {
(g.linkedItems || []).forEach(id => linkedIds.add(id));
});
return ITEMS.filter(i =>
i.status !== “someday” && !linkedIds.has(i.id) && i.status !== “done”
);
}

/* ═══ SHARED COMPONENTS ═══ */
const IC_IDS = new Set([“check”,“skip”,“flame”,“sun”,“moon”,“book”,“clock”,“target”,“list”,“sparkle”,“smile”,“meh”,“frown”,“chevLeft”,“chevRight”,“undo”,“plus”,“edit”,“zap”,“calendar”,“trash”,“pause”,“play”,“repeat”,“folder”,“skipFwd”,“sunCloud”,“compass”,“inbox”,“timer”,“house”,“award”,“trendUp”,“bolt”,“layers”,“eye”]);
function SmartIcon({ icon, size = 16, color }) {
if (IC_IDS.has(icon)) return <Ic id={icon} size={size} color={color} />;
return <span style={{ fontSize: size * 0.9, lineHeight: 1 }}>{icon}</span>;
}
function Dots({ d }) {
const v = DIFF[d];
return (
<div style={{ display: “inline-flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 4 }}>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, gap: 2 }}>
{[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
<div key={i} style={{ width: 5, height: 5, borderRadius: 3, background: i <= v.n ? v.c : `${v.c}20` }} />
))}
</div>
<span style={{ fontSize: 10.5, fontWeight: 600, color: v.c }}>{v.l}</span>
</div>
);
}

function ProgIcon({ id, area, size = 40 }) {
const ar = GA(area);
return (
<div style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size * 0.32,
background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${ar.c}14, ${ar.c}08)`,
border: `0.5px solid ${ar.c}20`,
boxShadow: `inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.5), 0 1px 3px ${ar.c}08`,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, flexShrink: 0 }}>
<span style={{ fontSize: size * 0.46, lineHeight: 1 }}>{ICONS[id] || “\u2728”}</span>
</div>
);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
APP STATE CONTEXT — reactive state management
═══════════════════════════════════ */
const INITIAL_ITEMS = […ITEMS];
const INITIAL_COMMITTED = […COMMITTED];

const AppStateCtx = createContext(null);
function useAppState() { return useContext(AppStateCtx); }

function AppStateProvider({ children }) {
const [items, setItems] = useState(INITIAL_ITEMS);
const [committed, setCommitted] = useState(INITIAL_COMMITTED);
const [moodLog, setMoodLog] = useState([]); // [{ date, mood }]
const [completionLog, setCompletionLog] = useState(() => {
// Seed with fake history for streak demo
const log = {};
for (let d = 1; d <= 4; d++) {
const dt = new Date(); dt.setDate(dt.getDate() - d);
log[dt.toISOString().slice(0, 10)] = { done: 5, total: 8 };
}
return log;
});

// Sync module-level vars SYNCHRONOUSLY so legacy helper functions
// (getTodayActions, getUnlinkedItems, goalProgress, etc.) see current data
// during the same render cycle. useEffect is too late (runs after paint).
ITEMS = items;
COMMITTED = committed;

// Streak calculation
const streak = useMemo(() => {
let count = 0;
const today = new Date();
// Check if today has completions — if so start from today, else from yesterday
const todayKey = today.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
const startOffset = completionLog[todayKey]?.done > 0 ? 0 : 1;
for (let d = startOffset; d < 365; d++) {
const dt = new Date(); dt.setDate(dt.getDate() - d);
const key = dt.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
if (completionLog[key]?.done > 0) count++;
else break;
}
return count;
}, [completionLog]);

// Weekly completion data for charts (last 7 days)
const weeklyData = useMemo(() => {
const days = [];
for (let d = 6; d >= 0; d–) {
const dt = new Date(); dt.setDate(dt.getDate() - d);
const key = dt.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
const entry = completionLog[key];
days.push({
label: dt.toLocaleDateString(“en-AU”, { weekday: “short” }).slice(0, 2),
date: key,
done: entry?.done || 0,
total: entry?.total || 0,
isToday: d === 0,
});
}
return days;
}, [completionLog]);

// Mutations
const addItem = useCallback((item) => {
setItems(prev => [item, …prev]);
}, []);

const updateItem = useCallback((id, updates) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => i.id === id ? { …i, …updates } : i));
}, []);

const removeItem = useCallback((id) => {
setItems(prev => prev.filter(i => i.id !== id));
}, []);

const pauseItem = useCallback((id) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => i.id === id ? { …i, status: “paused”, pausedAt: new Date().toISOString() } : i));
}, []);

const resumeItem = useCallback((id) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => i.id === id ? { …i, status: “active”, pausedAt: null } : i));
}, []);

const completeItem = useCallback((id) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => i.id === id ? { …i, status: “done” } : i));
}, []);

const toggleStep = useCallback((itemId, stepId) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId || !i.steps) return i;
const newSteps = i.steps.map(s => {
if (s.id !== stepId) return s;
const newDone = !s.done;
// If marking done, also mark all subtasks done; if undoing, leave subtasks as-is
const newSubtasks = newDone && s.subtasks ? s.subtasks.map(st => ({ …st, done: true })) : s.subtasks;
return { …s, done: newDone, status: newDone ? “done” : (s.status === “done” ? “todo” : s.status), subtasks: newSubtasks };
});
return { …i, steps: newSteps };
}));
}, []);

const toggleSubtask = useCallback((itemId, stepId, subtaskId) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId || !i.steps) return i;
const newSteps = i.steps.map(s => {
if (s.id !== stepId || !s.subtasks) return s;
const newSubtasks = s.subtasks.map(st => st.id === subtaskId ? { …st, done: !st.done } : st);
// Auto-complete parent task if all subtasks done
const allDone = newSubtasks.every(st => st.done);
return { …s, subtasks: newSubtasks, done: allDone, status: allDone ? “done” : (s.status === “done” ? “doing” : s.status) };
});
return { …i, steps: newSteps };
}));
}, []);

const updateStepStatus = useCallback((itemId, stepId, newStatus) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId || !i.steps) return i;
return { …i, steps: i.steps.map(s => s.id === stepId ? { …s, status: newStatus } : s) };
}));
}, []);

const addStep = useCallback((itemId, step) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId) return i;
return { …i, steps: […(i.steps || []), step] };
}));
}, []);

const removeStep = useCallback((itemId, stepId) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId || !i.steps) return i;
return { …i, steps: i.steps.filter(s => s.id !== stepId) };
}));
}, []);

const updateStep = useCallback((itemId, stepId, updates) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId || !i.steps) return i;
return { …i, steps: i.steps.map(s => s.id === stepId ? { …s, …updates } : s) };
}));
}, []);

const addSubtask = useCallback((itemId, stepId, subtask) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId || !i.steps) return i;
return { …i, steps: i.steps.map(s => {
if (s.id !== stepId) return s;
return { …s, subtasks: […(s.subtasks || []), subtask] };
})};
}));
}, []);

const removeSubtask = useCallback((itemId, stepId, subtaskId) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== itemId || !i.steps) return i;
return { …i, steps: i.steps.map(s => {
if (s.id !== stepId || !s.subtasks) return s;
return { …s, subtasks: s.subtasks.filter(st => st.id !== subtaskId) };
})};
}));
}, []);

const activateDream = useCallback((id, asType) => {
setItems(prev => prev.map(i => {
if (i.id !== id) return i;
if (asType === “habit”) return { …i, status: “active”, recurrence: { type: “daily” }, habitDuration: 15, habitTimeOfDay: “morning” };
if (asType === “project”) return { …i, status: “active”, steps: [{ id: “s1”, title: “Plan first step”, done: false }, { id: “s2”, title: “Get started”, done: false }, { id: “s3”, title: “Complete”, done: false }] };
return { …i, status: “active” }; // generic activate
}));
}, []);

const enrollProgram = useCallback((progId, weekData) => {
setCommitted(prev => {
if (prev.find(c => c.id === progId)) return prev; // already enrolled
return […prev, { id: progId, status: “active”, week: 1, day: 1, pct: 0, weeks: weekData || [] }];
});
}, []);

const recordMood = useCallback((mood) => {
setMoodLog(prev => […prev, { date: new Date().toISOString(), …mood }]);
}, []);

const recordCompletion = useCallback((actionId, status) => {
const todayKey = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
setCompletionLog(prev => {
const entry = prev[todayKey] || { done: 0, total: 0, skipped: 0 };
return {
…prev,
[todayKey]: {
done: entry.done + (status === “done” ? 1 : 0),
skipped: entry.skipped + (status === “skipped” ? 1 : 0),
total: entry.total + 1,
},
};
});
}, []);

const value = useMemo(() => ({
items, committed, moodLog, completionLog, streak, weeklyData,
addItem, updateItem, removeItem, pauseItem, resumeItem, completeItem,
toggleStep, toggleSubtask, updateStepStatus,
addStep, removeStep, updateStep, addSubtask, removeSubtask,
activateDream, enrollProgram, recordMood, recordCompletion,
}), [items, committed, moodLog, completionLog, streak, weeklyData,
addItem, updateItem, removeItem, pauseItem, resumeItem, completeItem,
toggleStep, toggleSubtask, updateStepStatus,
addStep, removeStep, updateStep, addSubtask, removeSubtask,
activateDream, enrollProgram, recordMood, recordCompletion]);

return <AppStateCtx.Provider value={value}>{children}</AppStateCtx.Provider>;
}

function ProgressRing({ progress, size = 48, sw = 3.5, color = T.brand }) {
const r = (size - sw) / 2;
const c = 2 * Math.PI * r;
return (
<svg width={size} height={size} style={{ transform: “rotate(-90deg)” }}>
<circle cx={size / 2} cy={size / 2} r={r} fill=“none” stroke={T.fill} strokeWidth={sw} />
<motion.circle cx={size / 2} cy={size / 2} r={r} fill=“none” stroke={color} strokeWidth={sw}
strokeLinecap=“round” strokeDasharray={c}
animate={{ strokeDashoffset: c - (progress * c) }}
transition={{ duration: 0.6, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }} />
</svg>
);
}

/* ═══ TAB ICONS ═══ */
function TabIcon({ name, active }) {
const c = active ? T.brand : T.t3;
const w = active ? 2 : 1.6;
const s = 22;
if (name === “home”) return (
<svg width={s} height={s} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={c} strokeWidth={w} strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
<path d=“M3 10.5L12 3l9 7.5V21a2 2 0 01-2 2H5a2 2 0 01-2-2V10.5z” fill={active ? `${c}15` : “none”} />
<polyline points="9 22 9 14 15 14 15 22" />
</svg>
);
if (name === “mylife”) return (
<svg width={s} height={s} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={c} strokeWidth={w} strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
<path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2" />
<path d="M12 6v6l4.5 2.5" />
<circle cx=“12” cy=“12” r=“1.5” fill={active ? c : “none”} />
</svg>
);
if (name === “discover”) return (
<svg width={s} height={s} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={c} strokeWidth={w} strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
<circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10" />
<polygon points=“16.24,7.76 13.5,13.5 7.76,16.24 10.5,10.5” fill={active ? c : “none”} stroke={c} strokeWidth={w * 0.8} />
</svg>
);
if (name === “plan”) return (
<svg width={s} height={s} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={c} strokeWidth={w} strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
<polygon points=“12 2 2 7 12 12 22 7 12 2” fill={active ? `${c}15` : “none”} />
<polyline points="2 17 12 22 22 17" />
<polyline points="2 12 12 17 22 12" />
</svg>
);
if (name === “add”) return (
<svg width={s} height={s} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="white" strokeWidth={2.6} strokeLinecap="round">
<line x1="12" y1="5" x2="12" y2="19"/><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12"/>
</svg>
);
return null;
}

/* — Swipe Card — */
/* — Swipe Card (with DONE/SKIP/DEFER labels) — */
function SwipeCard({ action, onComplete, onSkip, onDefer, isTop }) {
const x = useMotionValue(0);
const y = useMotionValue(0);
const rotate = useTransform(x, [-200, 200], [-15, 15]);
const doneOpacity = useTransform(x, [0, 80], [0, 1]);
const skipOpacity = useTransform(x, [-80, 0], [1, 0]);
const deferOpacity = useTransform(y, [0, 60], [0, 1]);
const prg = action.program ? PRG.find(p => p.id === action.program) : null;
const ar = action.area ? GA(action.area) : null;
const proj = action.type === “project” ? getUserProjects().find(p => p.id === action.projectId) : null;
const accent = ar ? ar.c : proj ? proj.color : T.brand;
return (
<motion.div
style={{ x, y, rotate, position: “absolute”, width: “100%”, cursor: “grab”, touchAction: “none” }}
drag={isTop ? true : false} dragConstraints={{ left: 0, right: 0, top: 0, bottom: 0 }} dragElastic={0.8}
onDragEnd={(_, info) => {
if (info.offset.x > 100) onComplete();
else if (info.offset.x < -100) onSkip();
else if (info.offset.y > 80) onDefer();
}}
initial={{ scale: isTop ? 1 : 0.95, y: isTop ? 0 : 8, opacity: isTop ? 1 : 0.6 }}
animate={{ scale: isTop ? 1 : 0.95, y: isTop ? 0 : 8, opacity: isTop ? 1 : 0.6 }}
exit={{ x: x.get() > 50 ? 300 : x.get() < -50 ? -300 : 0, y: y.get() > 50 ? 200 : 0, opacity: 0, transition: { duration: 0.3 } }}>
<div style={{ background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: “blur(24px) saturate(180%)”, WebkitBackdropFilter: “blur(24px) saturate(180%)”, borderRadius: 24, overflow: “hidden”,
border: T.cardBorder, minHeight: 290,
display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, position: “relative”,
boxShadow: isTop ? “0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.08)” : “0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.04)” }}>

```
    {/* Area color accent bar */}
    <div style={{ height: 3, background: `linear-gradient(90deg, ${accent}, ${accent}90)`, flexShrink: 0 }} />

    {/* Swipe feedback — overlaid on content, only visible during drag */}
    <motion.div style={{ opacity: doneOpacity, position: "absolute", left: 20, top: 18, zIndex: 2,
      padding: "5px 14px", borderRadius: 8, background: `${T.green}08`, border: `2px solid ${T.green}`, color: T.green,
      fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 800, letterSpacing: 1, transform: "rotate(-12deg)" }}>DONE</motion.div>
    <motion.div style={{ opacity: skipOpacity, position: "absolute", right: 20, top: 18, zIndex: 2,
      padding: "5px 14px", borderRadius: 8, background: `${T.red}08`, border: `2px solid ${T.red}`, color: T.red,
      fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 800, letterSpacing: 1, transform: "rotate(12deg)" }}>SKIP</motion.div>
    <motion.div style={{ opacity: deferOpacity, position: "absolute", left: "50%", top: 18, zIndex: 2,
      transform: "translateX(-50%)",
      padding: "5px 14px", borderRadius: 8, background: `${T.orange}08`, border: `2px solid ${T.orange}`, color: T.orange,
      fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 800, letterSpacing: 1 }}>LATER</motion.div>

    {/* Card content */}
    <div style={{ padding: "18px 22px 22px", flex: 1, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column" }}>

      {/* Source line — program/project + area + context */}
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: 4, marginBottom: 12 }}>
        {prg && ar ? (<>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 14, lineHeight: 1 }}>{ICONS[prg.id] || "\u2728"}</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 12.5, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t2 }}>{prg.t}</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, margin: "0 2px" }}>{"\u00B7"}</span>
          <div style={{ width: 6, height: 6, borderRadius: 3, background: ar.c }} />
          <span style={{ fontSize: 12.5, fontWeight: 600, color: ar.c }}>{ar.n}</span>
          {action.duration ? (<>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, margin: "0 2px" }}>{"\u00B7"}</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{formatDuration(action.duration)}</span>
          </>) : null}
        </>) : proj ? (<>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 14, lineHeight: 1 }}>{proj.emoji}</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 12.5, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t2 }}>{proj.title}</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: proj.color, fontWeight: 600, background: `${proj.color}10`,
            padding: "1px 6px", borderRadius: 4, marginLeft: 2 }}>Project</span>
          {action.duration ? (<>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, margin: "0 2px" }}>{"\u00B7"}</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{formatDuration(action.duration)}</span>
          </>) : null}
        </>) : (<>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 12.5, fontWeight: 600, color: T.brand }}>{action.category}</span>
          {action.duration ? (<>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, margin: "0 2px" }}>{"\u00B7"}</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{formatDuration(action.duration)}</span>
          </>) : null}
        </>)}
      </div>

      {/* Daily goal context */}
      {action.dayTitle && (
        <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginBottom: 12,
          padding: "6px 10px", borderRadius: 9, background: ar ? `${ar.c}06` : T.fill, alignSelf: "flex-start" }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 650, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase", letterSpacing: 0.3 }}>Today:</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t2 }}>{action.dayTitle}</span>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Title */}
      <h3 style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, margin: "0 0 12px", letterSpacing: -0.3, lineHeight: 1.28 }}>{action.title}</h3>

      {/* Description */}
      <p style={{ fontSize: 14.5, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.65, margin: 0, flex: 1 }}>{action.description}</p>

    </div>
  </div>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* — Action Tap Buttons — */
function ActionButtons({ onSkip, onDefer, onDone }) {

style={{ flex: 1, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, gap: 6,
padding: “14px 8px”, borderRadius: 16, border: `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
background: “#FFFFFF”, cursor: “pointer”, fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.t2 }}>
<Ic id="skip" size={16} color={T.red} /> Skip
</motion.button>
<motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.88 }} onClick={onDefer}
style={{ flex: 1, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, gap: 6,
padding: “14px 8px”, borderRadius: 16, border: `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
background: “#FFFFFF”, cursor: “pointer”, fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.t2 }}>
<Ic id="clock" size={16} color={T.orange} /> Later
</motion.button>
<motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.88 }} onClick={onDone}
style={{ flex: 1, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, gap: 6,
padding: “14px 8px”, borderRadius: 16, border: `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
background: “#FFFFFF”, cursor: “pointer”, fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.t2 }}>
<Ic id="check" size={16} color={T.green} /> Done
</motion.button>
</div>
);
}

</motion.div>
);

/* — Completion Screen (handles deferred) — */
function CompletionScreen({ completed, skipped, deferred, total, mood, streak, onUndo, canUndo, onSummary }) {
const pct = completed / total;
const headline = deferred > 0
? (completed > 0 ? “Good progress!” : “Actions deferred”)
: (pct === 1 ? “Perfect day!” : pct >= 0.5 ? “Good progress!” : “Every step counts”);
const subline = deferred > 0
? `${completed} done, ${deferred} for later. You can complete them anytime from the Today tab.`
: (pct === 1
? `All ${total} actions completed. Your consistency is building real momentum.`
: `${completed} of ${total} actions done today.`);
return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 200, damping: 22 }}
style={{ padding: “0 20px”, textAlign: “center” }}>
<div style={{ background: “#FFFFFF”, borderRadius: 24, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: 32 }}>
<div style={{ position: “relative”, width: 100, height: 100, margin: “0 auto 20px” }}>
<ProgressRing progress={pct} size={100} sw={6} color={pct === 1 ? T.green : T.brand} />
<div style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center” }}>
<span style={{ fontSize: 28, fontWeight: 800, color: T.text }}>{completed}</span>
<span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>of {total}</span>
</div>
</div>
<h3 style={{ fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, margin: “0 0 6px” }}>{headline}</h3>
<p style={{ fontSize: 15, color: T.t3, margin: “0 0 20px” }}>{subline}</p>

```
    {/* Stats row */}
    <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, marginBottom: 20 }}>
      {[
        { label: "Done", value: completed, color: T.green, icon: "check" },
        { label: "Skipped", value: skipped, color: T.t3, icon: "skip" },
        { label: "Later", value: deferred, color: T.orange, icon: "clock" },
        { label: "Streak", value: `${streak + (completed > 0 ? 1 : 0)}d`, color: T.orange, icon: "flame" },
      ].map((s) => (
        <div key={s.label} style={{ flex: 1, padding: "10px 4px", borderRadius: 12, background: `${s.color}08`, textAlign: "center" }}>
          <Ic id={s.icon} size={14} color={s.color} />
          <div style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 800, color: T.text, marginTop: 2 }}>{s.value}</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3 }}>{s.label}</div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>

    {mood && (
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", gap: 8,
        padding: "10px 16px", borderRadius: 12, background: `${mood.color}10`, marginBottom: 20 }}>
        <Ic id={mood.emoji} size={20} color={mood.color} />
        <span style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t2 }}>Feeling {mood.label.toLowerCase()} today</span>
      </div>
    )}

    {canUndo && (
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }} onClick={onUndo}
        style={{ width: "100%", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", gap: 6,
          padding: "12px", borderRadius: 14, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
          background: "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.brand, marginBottom: 10 }}>
        <Ic id="undo" size={15} color={T.brand} /> Undo last action
      </motion.button>
    )}
    <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={onSummary}
      style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
        background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
        boxShadow: "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2), 0 2px 6px rgba(108,92,231,0.1), inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.25)" }}>
      View Today's Summary
    </motion.button>
  </div>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* — Daily Summary Screen — */
function DailySummaryScreen({ actions, statuses, mood, streak, onDone }) {
const completed = Object.values(statuses).filter(s => s === “done”).length;
const skipped = Object.values(statuses).filter(s => s === “skipped”).length;
const deferred = Object.values(statuses).filter(s => s === “deferred”).length;
const total = actions.length;
const [aiInsight, setAiInsight] = useState(””);
const [insightLoading, setInsightLoading] = useState(true);

useEffect(() => {
(async () => {
setInsightLoading(true);
try {
const actionSummary = actions.map(a => `${a.title}: ${statuses[a.id] || "not done"}`).join(”. “);
const response = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”, {
method: “POST”, headers: { “Content-Type”: “application/json” },
body: JSON.stringify({
model: “claude-sonnet-4-20250514”, max_tokens: 200,
system: `You are the Stevo AI coach. Write a 2-3 sentence evening reflection for ${USER.name}. Week ${USER.programWeek} of their program. Mood: ${mood ? mood.label : "not logged"}. Actions: ${actionSummary}. Streak: ${streak} days. ${deferred > 0 ? `${deferred} actions deferred for later today. Gently encourage completing them.` : ""} Be specific. Never use em dashes. No exclamation marks at start. Warm and direct.`,
messages: [{ role: “user”, content: “Generate my daily summary.” }],
}),
});
const data = await response.json();
let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || “”).join(””) || “”;
text = text.replace(/\u2014/g, “. “).replace(/–/g, “. “).replace(/.\s./g, “.”).replace(/\s{2,}/g, “ “);
setAiInsight(text);
} catch (e) {
setAiInsight(completed === total
? `You nailed every action today, ${USER.name}. That kind of consistency is what actually rewires your habits.`
: deferred > 0
? `${completed} actions done so far, with ${deferred} waiting for later. Come back when you are ready.`
: `${completed} of ${total} actions completed today. Even partial days build the pathways that make these habits stick.`);
} finally { setInsightLoading(false); }
})();
}, []);

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 16 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 260, damping: 24 }}
style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: “auto”, padding: “4px 20px 40px” }}>
{/* Stats cards */}
<div style={{ display: “flex”, gap: 8, marginBottom: 14 }}>
{[
{ label: “Done”, value: completed, color: T.green, icon: “check” },
{ label: “Skipped”, value: skipped, color: T.t3, icon: “skip” },
{ label: “Later”, value: deferred, color: T.orange, icon: “clock” },
{ label: “Streak”, value: `${streak + (completed > 0 ? 1 : 0)}d`, color: T.orange, icon: “flame” },
].map((s, i) => (
<motion.div key={s.label} initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
transition={{ delay: 0.15 + i * 0.08 }}
style={{ flex: 1, background: “#FFFFFF”, borderRadius: 16, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: “12px 8px”, textAlign: “center” }}>
<Ic id={s.icon} size={14} color={s.color} />
<div style={{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 800, color: T.text, marginTop: 2 }}>{s.value}</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 500, color: T.t3 }}>{s.label}</div>
</motion.div>
))}
</div>
{mood && (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.35 }}
style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 10, padding: “12px 14px”,
borderRadius: 14, background: `${mood.color}08`, border: `0.5px solid ${mood.color}15`, marginBottom: 14 }}>
<Ic id={mood.emoji} size={22} color={mood.color} />
<div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>Feeling {mood.label.toLowerCase()}</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>Logged this morning</div>
</div>
</motion.div>
)}
{/* Actions list */}
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.4 }}
style={{ background: “#FFFFFF”, borderRadius: 18, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, overflow: “hidden”, marginBottom: 14 }}>
<div style={{ padding: “12px 16px 8px”, fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, textTransform: “uppercase”, letterSpacing: 0.5 }}>Actions</div>
{actions.map((a) => {
const s = statuses[a.id] || “pending”; const isDone = s === “done”; const isSkipped = s === “skipped”; const isDeferred = s === “deferred”;
return (
<div key={a.id} style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 12, padding: “12px 16px”,
borderTop: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, opacity: isSkipped ? 0.5 : 1 }}>
<div style={{ width: 24, height: 24, borderRadius: 12, background: isDone ? T.green : isDeferred ? `${T.orange}15` : “transparent”,
border: `1.5px solid ${isDone ? T.green : isDeferred ? T.orange : isSkipped ? T.t3 : T.fill}`,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, flexShrink: 0 }}>
{isDone && <svg width={12} height={12} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="white" strokeWidth={3} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg>}
{isSkipped && <Ic id="skip" size={10} color={T.t3} />}
{isDeferred && <Ic id="clock" size={10} color={T.orange} />}
</div>
<div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
<div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text, textDecoration: isSkipped ? “line-through” : “none” }}>{a.title}</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{formatDuration(a.duration)}</div>
</div>
<span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600, borderRadius: 6, padding: “3px 8px”,
color: isDone ? T.green : isDeferred ? T.orange : isSkipped ? T.t3 : T.brand,
background: isDone ? `${T.green}10` : isDeferred ? `${T.orange}10` : isSkipped ? T.fill : `${T.brand}08` }}>
{isDone ? “Done” : isDeferred ? “Later” : isSkipped ? “Skipped” : “Pending”}
</span>
</div>
);
})}
</motion.div>
{/* AI Coach */}
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.55 }}
style={{ background: “#FFFFFF”, borderRadius: 18, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: 18 }}>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 8, marginBottom: 10 }}>
<div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 8, background: T.grad,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center” }}>
<span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 800, color: “white” }}>M3</span>
</div>
<span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Coach’s Take</span>
</div>
{insightLoading ? (
<div style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 8, padding: “8px 0” }}>
<motion.div animate={{ rotate: 360 }} transition={{ duration: 1.5, repeat: Infinity, ease: “linear” }}
style={{ width: 16, height: 16, borderRadius: 8, border: “1.5px solid rgba(108,92,231,0.2)”, borderTopColor: T.brand }} />
<span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3 }}>Reflecting on your day…</span>
</div>
) : (
<p style={{ fontSize: 14.5, lineHeight: 1.6, color: T.t2, margin: 0 }}>{aiInsight}</p>
)}
</motion.div>
<motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
transition={{ delay: 0.65 }} onClick={onDone}
style={{ width: “100%”, padding: “15px”, borderRadius: 14, border: “none”, cursor: “pointer”,
background: T.grad, color: “white”, fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650, marginTop: 14,
boxShadow: “0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2), 0 2px 6px rgba(108,92,231,0.1), inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.25)” }}>
Done for Today
</motion.button>
</motion.div>
);
}

/* — Today Dashboard (compact flat checklist, Things 3 inspired) — */
/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
TODAY DASHBOARD  — checklist-first, ritual cards on top
───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

function WeeklyReviewScreen({ weekNum, totalWeeks, actions, statuses, mood, streak, onContinue }) {
const completed = Object.values(statuses).filter(s => s === “done”).length;
const total = actions.length;
const pct = Math.round((completed / total) * 100);
const [aiReview, setAiReview] = useState(””);
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

useEffect(() => {
(async () => {
try {
const response = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”, {
method: “POST”, headers: { “Content-Type”: “application/json” },
body: JSON.stringify({
model: “claude-sonnet-4-20250514”, max_tokens: 250,
system: `You are the Stevo AI coach writing a weekly review for ${USER.name}. They just completed week ${weekNum} of ${totalWeeks}. Completion rate: ${pct}%. Streak: ${streak} days. Write 3 sentences: celebrate what went well, identify one area to improve, preview what is coming next week. Never use em dashes. Warm and direct.`,
messages: [{ role: “user”, content: “Generate my weekly review.” }],
}),
});
const data = await response.json();
let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || “”).join(””) || “”;
text = text.replace(/\u2014/g, “. “).replace(/–/g, “. “).replace(/.\s./g, “.”).replace(/\s{2,}/g, “ “);
setAiReview(text);
} catch (e) {
setAiReview(`Week ${weekNum} is in the books, ${USER.name}. You completed ${pct}% of your actions this week, and that consistency is building real change. Next week brings new challenges and deeper habits.`);
} finally { setLoading(false); }
})();
}, []);

const isLastWeek = weekNum >= totalWeeks;

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: “auto”, padding: “20px 20px 40px”, textAlign: “center” }}>
<motion.div initial={{ scale: 0 }} animate={{ scale: 1 }} transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 300, damping: 20 }}
style={{ width: 72, height: 72, borderRadius: 36, background: `${T.brand}10`,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, margin: “0 auto 16px” }}>
<span style={{ fontSize: 28, fontWeight: 800, color: T.brand }}>W{weekNum}</span>
</motion.div>
<h2 style={{ fontSize: 26, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, margin: “0 0 4px” }}>Week {weekNum} Complete</h2>
<p style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t3, margin: “0 0 24px” }}>{isLastWeek ? “Final week done!” : `${totalWeeks - weekNum} weeks remaining`}</p>

```
  <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginBottom: 20 }}>
    {[
      { label: "Completion", value: `${pct}%`, color: T.green },
      { label: "Streak", value: `${streak}d`, color: T.orange },
      { label: "Actions done", value: completed, color: T.brand },
    ].map((s) => (
      <div key={s.label} style={{ flex: 1, background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 16, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: "14px 8px" }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 800, color: s.color }}>{s.value}</div>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{s.label}</div>
      </div>
    ))}
  </div>

  {/* AI weekly reflection */}
  <div style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 18, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: 18, marginBottom: 20, textAlign: "left" }}>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, marginBottom: 10 }}>
      <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 8, background: T.grad,
        display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
        <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>M3</span>
      </div>
      <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Weekly Reflection</span>
    </div>
    {loading ? (
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, padding: "8px 0" }}>
        <motion.div animate={{ rotate: 360 }} transition={{ duration: 1.5, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
          style={{ width: 16, height: 16, borderRadius: 8, border: "1.5px solid rgba(108,92,231,0.2)", borderTopColor: T.brand }} />
        <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3 }}>Writing your weekly review...</span>
      </div>
    ) : (
      <p style={{ fontSize: 14.5, lineHeight: 1.6, color: T.t2, margin: 0 }}>{aiReview}</p>
    )}
  </div>

  <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={onContinue}
    style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
      background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
      boxShadow: "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2), 0 2px 6px rgba(108,92,231,0.1), inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.25)" }}>
    {isLastWeek ? "See Final Results" : `Start Week ${weekNum + 1}`}
  </motion.button>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* — Graduation Screen — */
function GraduationScreen({ programName, totalWeeks, streak, totalActions, onBrowse }) {
const [aiReflection, setAiReflection] = useState(””);
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
const [recPrograms, setRecPrograms] = useState([]);

useEffect(() => {
(async () => {
try {
const response = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”, {
method: “POST”, headers: { “Content-Type”: “application/json” },
body: JSON.stringify({
model: “claude-sonnet-4-20250514”, max_tokens: 250,
system: `You are the Stevo AI coach. ${USER.name} just completed the entire "${programName}" program (${totalWeeks} weeks, ${totalActions} actions). Write a 3-sentence congratulatory reflection. Acknowledge the commitment, highlight what they have built, and encourage what comes next. Never use em dashes. Warm, specific, and celebratory.`,
messages: [{ role: “user”, content: “Generate my graduation reflection.” }],
}),
});
const data = await response.json();
let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || “”).join(””) || “”;
text = text.replace(/\u2014/g, “. “).replace(/–/g, “. “).replace(/.\s./g, “.”).replace(/\s{2,}/g, “ “);
setAiReflection(text);
} catch (e) {
setAiReflection(`${totalWeeks} weeks, ${totalActions} actions, and a ${streak}-day streak. You did not just complete a program, ${USER.name}. You built a foundation that will keep working long after today.`);
} finally { setLoading(false); }
})();
// Recommend 2 programs from different areas
const currentProg = PRG.find(p => p.t === programName);
const recs = PRG.filter(p => p.id !== currentProg?.id).sort((a, b) => b.rt - a.rt).slice(0, 2);
setRecPrograms(recs);
}, []);

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: “auto”, padding: “20px 20px 40px”, textAlign: “center” }}>
<motion.div initial={{ scale: 0, rotate: -180 }} animate={{ scale: 1, rotate: 0 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 200, damping: 15, delay: 0.2 }}
style={{ width: 88, height: 88, borderRadius: 44, background: T.grad,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, margin: “0 auto 20px”,
boxShadow: “0 8px 32px rgba(108,92,231,0.3)” }}>
<Ic id="sparkle" size={40} color="white" />
</motion.div>
<motion.h2 initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.4 }}
style={{ fontSize: 28, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, margin: “0 0 4px” }}>
Journey Complete
</motion.h2>
<motion.p initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.5 }}
style={{ fontSize: 15, color: T.t3, margin: “0 0 24px” }}>{programName}</motion.p>

```
  <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.6 }}
    style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginBottom: 20 }}>
    {[
      { label: "Weeks", value: totalWeeks, color: T.brand },
      { label: "Actions", value: totalActions, color: T.green },
      { label: "Streak", value: `${streak}d`, color: T.orange },
    ].map((s) => (
      <div key={s.label} style={{ flex: 1, background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 16, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: "14px 8px" }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 26, fontWeight: 800, color: s.color }}>{s.value}</div>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{s.label}</div>
      </div>
    ))}
  </motion.div>

  {/* AI reflection */}
  <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.7 }}
    style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 18, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: 18, marginBottom: 20, textAlign: "left" }}>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, marginBottom: 10 }}>
      <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 8, background: T.grad,
        display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
        <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>M3</span>
      </div>
      <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Your Journey</span>
    </div>
    {loading ? (
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, padding: "8px 0" }}>
        <motion.div animate={{ rotate: 360 }} transition={{ duration: 1.5, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
          style={{ width: 16, height: 16, borderRadius: 8, border: "1.5px solid rgba(108,92,231,0.2)", borderTopColor: T.brand }} />
        <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3 }}>Reflecting on your journey...</span>
      </div>
    ) : (
      <p style={{ fontSize: 14.5, lineHeight: 1.6, color: T.t2, margin: 0 }}>{aiReflection}</p>
    )}
  </motion.div>

  {/* Recommended next */}
  {recPrograms.length > 0 && (
    <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.85 }}
      style={{ textAlign: "left", marginBottom: 20 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase", letterSpacing: 0.5, marginBottom: 8 }}>
        Recommended next
      </div>
      {recPrograms.map((p) => {
        const ar = GA(p.a);
        return (
          <div key={p.id} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "14px 16px",
            background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 16, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, marginBottom: 8 }}>
            <ProgIcon id={p.id} area={p.a} size={40} />
            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>{p.t}</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{p.e} {"\u00B7"} {p.w} weeks</div>
            </div>
            <Dots d={p.d} />
          </div>
        );
      })}
    </motion.div>
  )}

  <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
    transition={{ delay: 0.95 }} onClick={onBrowse}
    style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
      background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
      boxShadow: "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2), 0 2px 6px rgba(108,92,231,0.1), inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.25)" }}>
    Browse Journeys
  </motion.button>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* — Today’s List View (with defer support) — */

/* — Main Today Screen (full state machine) — */
function GoalFinder({ onSelectProgram, onClose }) {
const [input, setInput] = useState(””);
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
const [results, setResults] = useState(null); // { intro, programs: [{ id, reason }] }
const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
const [filterArea, setFilterArea] = useState(null);
const scrollRef = useRef(null);

const programCatalog = PRG.map(p => `${p.id}: "${p.t}" (${GA(p.a).n}) - ${p.ds}`).join(”\n”);

// When user taps an area filter, show programs in that area directly
function handleFilterArea(areaId) {
if (filterArea === areaId) {
setFilterArea(null);
setResults(null);
setMessages([]);
return;
}
setFilterArea(areaId);
const areaName = GA(areaId)?.n || areaId;
const matched = PRG.filter(p => p.a === areaId);
setResults({
intro: `Here are the ${areaName.toLowerCase()} journeys available.`,
programs: matched.map(p => ({ id: p.id, reason: p.ds })),
});
setMessages([
{ role: “user”, text: `Show me ${areaName.toLowerCase()} journeys` },
{ role: “assistant”, text: `Here are the ${areaName.toLowerCase()} journeys available.` },
]);
}

async function handleSend() {
if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
const userMsg = input.trim();
setInput(””);
setFilterArea(null);
setMessages(prev => […prev, { role: “user”, text: userMsg }]);
setLoading(true);
setResults(null);

```
try {
  const response = await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", {
    method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: "claude-sonnet-4-20250514", max_tokens: 500,
      system: `You are the Stevo AI helping users find the right self-improvement journeys. Here is the full journey catalog:\n\n${programCatalog}\n\nThe user will describe a goal, problem, or aspiration. Respond with:\n1. A brief 1-2 sentence empathetic acknowledgement of their goal\n2. 2-4 recommended journey IDs from the catalog that best match, with a short reason for each\n\nRespond ONLY with valid JSON, no markdown backticks:\n{"intro":"your acknowledgement","programs":[{"id":"program_id","reason":"why this helps"}]}`,
      messages: [{ role: "user", content: userMsg }],
    }),
  });
  const data = await response.json();
  let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || "").join("") || "";
  text = text.replace(/```json|```/g, "").trim();
  const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
  setResults(parsed);
  setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "assistant", text: parsed.intro }]);
} catch (e) {
  // Fallback: keyword match
  const lower = userMsg.toLowerCase();
  const matched = PRG.filter(p =>
    p.t.toLowerCase().includes(lower) || p.ds.toLowerCase().includes(lower) ||
    GA(p.a).n.toLowerCase().includes(lower)
  ).slice(0, 3);
  const fallback = {
    intro: matched.length > 0
      ? `Here are some journeys that could help with what you're looking for.`
      : `I couldn't find an exact match, but here are some popular journeys to explore.`,
    programs: (matched.length > 0 ? matched : PRG.filter(p => p.f)).map(p => ({
      id: p.id, reason: p.ds
    })),
  };
  setResults(fallback);
  setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "assistant", text: fallback.intro }]);
} finally { setLoading(false); }
```

}

useEffect(() => {
if (scrollRef.current) scrollRef.current.scrollTop = scrollRef.current.scrollHeight;
}, [messages, results, loading]);

const suggestions = [
“I want to find a new job”,
“Help me sleep better”,
“I want to build better habits”,
“How do I manage my money”,
];

// Only show areas that have programs
const areasWithPrograms = AREAS.filter(a => PRG.some(p => p.a === a.id));

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 320, damping: 30 }}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, background: T.meshBg, zIndex: 30, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column” }}>

```
  {/* Header */}
  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "14px 20px 10px", flexShrink: 0 }}>
    <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={onClose}
      style={{ width: 34, height: 34, borderRadius: 17, background: T.fill, border: "none",
        cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
      <Ic id="chevLeft" size={18} color={T.text} />
    </motion.button>
    <div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>Find Your Journey</div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>Tell me what you want to work on</div>
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Area filter chips */}
  <div style={{ padding: "0 20px 8px", flexShrink: 0 }}>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, overflowX: "auto", scrollbarWidth: "none", padding: "2px 0" }}>
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
        onClick={() => { setFilterArea(null); if (messages.length > 0 && filterArea) { setMessages([]); setResults(null); } }}
        style={{ padding: "6px 12px", borderRadius: 10, border: "none", cursor: "pointer", whiteSpace: "nowrap", flexShrink: 0,
          fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, background: !filterArea ? T.brand : T.fill, color: !filterArea ? "white" : T.t2 }}>
        All
      </motion.button>
      {areasWithPrograms.map(a => {
        const count = PRG.filter(p => p.a === a.id).length;
        return (
          <motion.button key={a.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
            onClick={() => handleFilterArea(a.id)}
            style={{ padding: "6px 12px", borderRadius: 10, border: "none", cursor: "pointer", whiteSpace: "nowrap", flexShrink: 0,
              fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 4,
              background: filterArea === a.id ? a.c : T.fill, color: filterArea === a.id ? "white" : T.t2 }}>
            {a.n.split(" ")[0]}
            <span style={{ fontSize: 10, opacity: 0.7 }}>({count})</span>
          </motion.button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Chat area */}
  <div ref={scrollRef} style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: "auto", padding: "8px 20px 16px" }}>

    {/* Empty state with suggestions */}
    {messages.length === 0 && (
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}>
        <div style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 20, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
          padding: 20, marginBottom: 16 }}>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, marginBottom: 12 }}>
            <div style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, background: T.grad,
              display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>M3</span>
            </div>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Stevo</span>
          </div>
          <p style={{ fontSize: 15, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.6, margin: "0 0 16px" }}>
            Describe a goal, challenge, or something you want to improve. I'll recommend the best journeys for you.
          </p>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase",
            letterSpacing: 0.5, marginBottom: 8 }}>Try something like</div>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
            {suggestions.map((s, i) => (
              <motion.button key={i} whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }}
                onClick={() => { setInput(s); }}
                style={{ textAlign: "left", padding: "10px 14px", borderRadius: 12,
                  background: `${T.brand}06`, border: `0.5px solid ${T.brand}15`,
                  cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 14, color: T.brand, fontWeight: 500 }}>
                {s}
              </motion.button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    )}

    {/* Message thread */}
    {messages.map((m, i) => (
      <motion.div key={i} initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: m.role === "user" ? "flex-end" : "flex-start",
          marginBottom: 10 }}>
        <div style={{
          maxWidth: "85%", padding: "12px 16px", borderRadius: 18,
          ...(m.role === "user"
            ? { background: T.brand, color: "white",
                borderBottomRightRadius: 6 }
            : { background: "#FFFFFF", color: T.text, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                borderBottomLeftRadius: 6 }),
          fontSize: 15, lineHeight: 1.55,
        }}>
          {m.text}
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    ))}

    {/* Loading */}
    {loading && (
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
        style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, alignItems: "center", padding: "8px 0" }}>
        <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 8, background: T.grad,
          display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>M3</span>
        </div>
        <motion.div animate={{ opacity: [0.4, 1, 0.4] }} transition={{ duration: 1.5, repeat: Infinity }}
          style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t3 }}>Finding the best journeys for you...</motion.div>
      </motion.div>
    )}

    {/* Program recommendations */}
    {results && results.programs && (
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        style={{ marginTop: 4 }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase",
          letterSpacing: 0.5, marginBottom: 8, paddingLeft: 4 }}>Recommended journeys</div>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 8 }}>
          {results.programs.map((rec, i) => {
            const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === rec.id);
            if (!prog) return null;
            const ar = GA(prog.a);
            return (
              <motion.div key={rec.id}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                transition={{ delay: i * 0.1 }}
                whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }}
                onClick={() => onSelectProgram(prog)}
                style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 16, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                  overflow: "hidden", cursor: "pointer" }}>
                <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "14px 16px" }}>
                  <ProgIcon id={prog.id} area={prog.a} size={44} />
                  <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text, lineHeight: 1.25 }}>{prog.t}</div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 11.5, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>{prog.e} · {prog.w} weeks</div>
                    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginTop: 4 }}>
                      <Dots d={prog.d} />
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3 }}>{prog.u >= 1000 ? (prog.u/1000).toFixed(1)+"k" : prog.u} enrolled</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <Ic id="chevLeft" size={16} color={T.t3} style={{ transform: "rotate(180deg)" }} />
                </div>
                {/* AI reason */}
                <div style={{ padding: "0 16px 12px", display: "flex", gap: 8, alignItems: "flex-start" }}>
                  <div style={{ width: 18, height: 18, borderRadius: 5, background: T.grad, flexShrink: 0, marginTop: 1,
                    display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                    <Ic id="sparkle" size={10} color="white" />
                  </div>
                  <p style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.45, margin: 0 }}>{rec.reason}</p>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Ask again */}
        <div style={{ textAlign: "center", marginTop: 16 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3 }}>Not quite right? Try describing your goal differently below.</span>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    )}
  </div>

  {/* Input bar */}
  <div style={{ padding: "8px 20px 20px", flexShrink: 0,
    background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.55)", backdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)",
    WebkitBackdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)", borderTop: "0.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.5)" }}>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8 }}>
      <input value={input} onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)}
        onKeyDown={e => e.key === "Enter" && handleSend()}
        placeholder="What do you want to work on?"
        style={{ flex: 1, padding: "12px 16px", borderRadius: 14, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
          background: "#FFFFFF", fontSize: 15, color: T.text, outline: "none", fontFamily: "inherit" }} />
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={handleSend}
        disabled={!input.trim() || loading}
        style={{ width: 42, height: 42, borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
          background: input.trim() ? T.grad : T.fill,
          display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0,
          opacity: input.trim() ? 1 : 0.5 }}>
        <svg width={18} height={18} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
          stroke={input.trim() ? "white" : T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round">
          <line x1="22" y1="2" x2="11" y2="13" /><polygon points="22 2 15 22 11 13 2 9 22 2" />
        </svg>
      </motion.button>
    </div>
  </div>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* — Program Builder (AI-powered custom program creation) — */
function ProgramBuilder({ onClose, onSave }) {
const [step, setStep] = useState(“goal”); // goal | details | generating | review | saved
const [goal, setGoal] = useState(””);
const [area, setArea] = useState(null);
const [weeks, setWeeks] = useState(4);
const [minsPerDay, setMinsPerDay] = useState(15);
const [program, setProgram] = useState(null); // AI-generated result
const [editingTitle, setEditingTitle] = useState(false);
const [editTitle, setEditTitle] = useState(””);
const scrollRef = useRef(null);

const areasCatalog = AREAS.map(a => `${a.id}: ${a.n}`).join(”, “);

async function handleGenerate() {
if (!goal.trim()) return;
setStep(“generating”);
try {
const response = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”, {
method: “POST”, headers: { “Content-Type”: “application/json” },
body: JSON.stringify({
model: “claude-sonnet-4-20250514”, max_tokens: 1000,
system: `You are the Stevo AI journey designer. Create a structured self-improvement journey based on the user's goal.\n\nAvailable life areas: ${areasCatalog}\n\nUser preferences: ${area ? `Area: ${area}` : "Auto-detect best area"}, Duration: ${weeks} weeks, Time commitment: ${minsPerDay} min/day.\n\nRespond ONLY with valid JSON, no markdown backticks:\n{\n  "title": "Journey title (concise, action-oriented)",\n  "area": "area_id from list above",\n  "description": "1-2 sentence description",\n  "weeks": ${weeks},\n  "minutesPerDay": ${minsPerDay},\n  "weekPlan": [\n    {\n      "week": 1,\n      "focus": "Week theme (2-3 words)",\n      "actions": [\n        {"title": "Action name", "duration": "X minutes", "description": "Brief how-to"}\n      ]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n\nEach week should have 3-4 daily actions. Make actions specific, actionable, and progressive. Never use em dashes.`,
messages: [{ role: “user”, content: `My goal: ${goal}` }],
}),
});
const data = await response.json();
let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || “”).join(””) || “”;
text = text.replace(/`json|`/g, “”).trim();
const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
setProgram(parsed);
setEditTitle(parsed.title);
setStep(“review”);
} catch (e) {
// Fallback program
const fallback = {
title: `Custom: ${goal.slice(0, 30)}`,
area: area || “personal”,
description: `A personalized journey to help you ${goal.toLowerCase()}.`,
weeks,
minutesPerDay: minsPerDay,
weekPlan: Array.from({ length: weeks }, (_, i) => ({
week: i + 1,
focus: i === 0 ? “Foundation” : i === weeks - 1 ? “Integration” : `Week ${i + 1} Focus`,
actions: [
{ title: “Morning intention setting”, duration: “5 minutes”, description: “Start each day by writing your specific intention for this week’s focus.” },
{ title: “Core practice”, duration: `${Math.max(5, minsPerDay - 10)} minutes`, description: “Dedicated time for your main activity this week.” },
{ title: “Evening reflection”, duration: “5 minutes”, description: “Review what worked, what didn’t, and what to adjust tomorrow.” },
],
})),
};
setProgram(fallback);
setEditTitle(fallback.title);
setStep(“review”);
}
}

function handleRemoveAction(weekIdx, actionIdx) {
setProgram(prev => {
const next = { …prev, weekPlan: prev.weekPlan.map((w, wi) =>
wi === weekIdx ? { …w, actions: w.actions.filter((_, ai) => ai !== actionIdx) } : w
)};
return next;
});
}

function handleSave() {
if (program) {
program.title = editTitle || program.title;
setStep(“saved”);
if (onSave) onSave(program);
}
}

const totalActions = program ? program.weekPlan.reduce((sum, w) => sum + w.actions.length, 0) : 0;

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 320, damping: 30 }}
