```
                    return (
                      <div key={a.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, opacity:d?0.38:1, transition:"opacity 0.2s" }}>
                        <div style={{ width:18, height:18, borderRadius:9, flexShrink:0,
                          border: d ? `2px solid ${T.green}` : `1.5px solid ${jg.ac}35`,
                          background: d ? T.green : "transparent",
                          display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center" }}>
                          {d && <svg width={9} height={9} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="white" strokeWidth={3.5} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg>}
                        </div>
                        <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:d?T.t3:T.t2, fontWeight:d?400:500,
                          textDecoration:d?"line-through":"none", lineHeight:1.35 }}>{a.title}</span>
                      </div>
                    );
                  })}
                  {jg.actions.length > 3 && <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.t3, paddingLeft:28 }}>+{jg.actions.length-3} more</div>}
                </div>
                {/* Footer */}
                <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8,
                  paddingTop:12, borderTop:`1px solid ${jg.ac}10` }}>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.t3 }}>~{formatDuration(jg.totalMins)}</span>
                  <div style={{ flex:1, height:3, borderRadius:2, background:`${jg.ac}10`, overflow:"hidden" }}>
                    <div style={{ width:`${Math.round((doneCount2/jg.actions.length)*100)}%`, height:"100%",
                      background:`linear-gradient(90deg,${jg.ac},${jg.ac}80)` }}/>
                  </div>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:11, fontWeight:600, color:jg.ac }}>
                    {doneCount2}/{jg.actions.length} done
                  </span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ═══ TODAY'S TASKS ═══ */}
  {checklistGroups.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ padding:"0 16px" }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:T.t2, marginBottom:10, paddingLeft:2, letterSpacing:-0.2 }}>
        {journeyGroups.length > 0 ? "Tasks & habits" : "Today"}
      </div>
      {checklistGroups.map(g => <ChecklistGroup key={g.id} group={g} />)}
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ═══ DREAM NUDGE ═══ */}
  {allChecklistDone && getSomedayItems().length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ padding: "8px 16px 0" }}>
      <div style={{ padding: "14px 16px", borderRadius: 16, background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.5)", border: "0.5px solid rgba(155,89,182,0.12)" }}>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
          <div style={{ width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: 10, background: "linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(155,89,182,0.08), rgba(108,92,231,0.08))", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 17 }}>{getSomedayItems()[0].emoji}</span>
          </div>
          <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>"{getSomedayItems()[0].title}"</div>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>A dream waiting. Ready when you are.</div>
          </div>
          <svg width={13} height={13} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.brand} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="9 18 15 12 9 6"/></svg>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ═══ EMPTY STATE ═══ */}
  {totalToday === 0 && (
    <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "64px 24px 40px" }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 48, marginBottom: 12 }}>☀️</div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.3, marginBottom: 8 }}>Nothing scheduled today</div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t3, lineHeight: 1.55, maxWidth: 260, margin: "0 auto" }}>
        Mark tasks as "Today" in a project, start a Journey from Discover, or add a new habit.
      </div>
    </div>
  )}
</div>
```

);
}

/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
TODAY SCREEN  — state machine: dashboard | journey session
───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function TodayScreen({ onDiscovery }) {
const { items, streak, toggleStep, recordCompletion } = useAppState();

// Recomputes whenever items change — fixes the empty-deps bug
const todayActions = useMemo(() => getTodayActions(), [items]);

// Session state
const [todayView, setTodayView]           = useState(“dashboard”);
const [sessionStep, setSessionStep]       = useState(“briefing”);
const [sessionJourneyId, setSessionJourneyId] = useState(null);
const [briefing, setBriefing]             = useState(””);
const [briefingLoading, setBriefingLoading] = useState(false);
const [mood, setMood]                     = useState(null);
const [statuses, setStatuses]             = useState({});
const [undoStack, setUndoStack]           = useState([]);
const [showUndo, setShowUndo]             = useState(false);
const undoTimer                           = useRef(null);

// Week/program state (kept for WeeklyReview + GraduationScreen)
const [weekStatus, setWeekStatus]   = useState(“active”);
const [programWeek, setProgramWeek] = useState(USER.programWeek);
const [weekDay, setWeekDay]         = useState(USER.weekDay);
const currentProg = PRG.find(p => p.id === “sleep”);
const totalWeeks  = currentProg?.w || 6;

// Session deck: only the chosen journey’s actions, not project tasks
const sessionJourneyActions = useMemo(() =>
sessionJourneyId
? todayActions.filter(a => a.type === “journey” && a.program === sessionJourneyId)
: [],
[todayActions, sessionJourneyId]);

const actionDeck = useMemo(
() => pickSessionActions(sessionJourneyActions, statuses, new Set()),
[sessionJourneyActions, statuses]);

const completed   = Object.values(statuses).filter(s => s === “done”).length;
const skipped     = Object.values(statuses).filter(s => s === “skipped”).length;
const deferred    = Object.values(statuses).filter(s => s === “deferred”).length;

// Briefing — generated per-journey when session starts
async function loadBriefing(journeyId) {
setBriefingLoading(true);
const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === journeyId);
const jActions = todayActions.filter(a => a.type === “journey” && a.program === journeyId);
try {
const res = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”, {
method: “POST”, headers: { “Content-Type”: “application/json” },
body: JSON.stringify({
model: “claude-sonnet-4-20250514”, max_tokens: 200,
system: `You are the Stevo AI. Generate a brief morning briefing (2 sentences) for ${USER.name} starting their "${prog?.t}" journey session. Today is Day ${jActions[0]?.dayNum || 1} of Week ${jActions[0]?.weekNum || 1}: "${jActions[0]?.dayTitle || ""}". ${jActions.length} actions today. ${USER.streak}-day streak. Be specific to today's focus. Never use em dashes. Direct and warm.`,
messages: [{ role: “user”, content: “Generate briefing.” }],
}),
});
const data = await res.json();
let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || “”).join(””) || “”;
text = text.replace(/\u2014/g, “. “).replace(/–/g, “. “).replace(/.\s./g, “.”).replace(/\s{2,}/g, “ “);
setBriefing(text);
} catch {
const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === journeyId);
setBriefing(`${jActions.length} actions for your ${prog?.t} session today. Each one builds on the last — let's make Day ${jActions[0]?.dayNum || 1} count.`);
} finally { setBriefingLoading(false); }
}

function startJourneySession(journeyId) {
setSessionJourneyId(journeyId);
setSessionStep(“briefing”);
setTodayView(“session”);
loadBriefing(journeyId);
}

function exitSession() { setTodayView(“dashboard”); }

function flashUndo() {
setShowUndo(true);
if (undoTimer.current) clearTimeout(undoTimer.current);
undoTimer.current = setTimeout(() => setShowUndo(false), 4000);
}

function processAction(status) {
const action = actionDeck[0];
if (!action) return;
setUndoStack(prev => […prev, { actionId: action.id, prevStatus: statuses[action.id] }]);
setStatuses(prev => ({ …prev, [action.id]: status }));
recordCompletion(action.id, status);
flashUndo();
const newStatuses = { …statuses, [action.id]: status };
if (pickSessionActions(sessionJourneyActions, newStatuses, new Set()).length === 0) {
setTimeout(() => setSessionStep(“complete”), 300);
}
}

function handleUndo() {
if (!undoStack.length) return;
const last = undoStack[undoStack.length - 1];
setUndoStack(p => p.slice(0, -1));
setStatuses(prev => {
const n = { …prev };
if (last.prevStatus === undefined) delete n[last.actionId];
else n[last.actionId] = last.prevStatus;
return n;
});
if (sessionStep === “complete”) setSessionStep(“actions”);
setShowUndo(false);
}

function handleDoneForToday() {
setTodayView(“dashboard”);
if (weekDay >= 7) setTimeout(() => setWeekStatus(“review”), 500);
}

function handleWeeklyReviewContinue() {
if (programWeek >= totalWeeks) {
setWeekStatus(“graduated”);
} else {
setProgramWeek(p => p + 1);
setWeekDay(1);
setWeekStatus(“active”);
setSessionStep(“briefing”);
setStatuses({});
setUndoStack([]);
setMood(null);
setTodayView(“dashboard”);
}
}

// Session header labels
const sessionHandled = Object.keys(statuses).filter(k => sessionJourneyActions.some(a => a.id === k)).length;
const currentAction  = actionDeck[0];
const currentProg2   = currentAction ? PRG.find(p => p.id === currentAction.program) : null;
const sessionTitle   = sessionStep === “briefing” ? “Today’s Briefing”
: sessionStep === “mood” ? “Check-in”
: sessionStep === “actions” ? `Action ${sessionHandled + 1} of ${sessionJourneyActions.length}`
: sessionStep === “complete” ? “Session Complete”
: sessionStep === “summary” ? “Today’s Summary” : “Session”;
const sessionSubtitle = currentProg2 ? `${ICONS[currentProg2.id] || ""} ${currentProg2.t}` : “”;
const canBack = [“mood”, “actions”, “complete”, “summary”].includes(sessionStep);
const backLabel = sessionStep === “mood” ? “Briefing” : sessionStep === “actions” ? “Dashboard” : sessionStep === “summary” ? “Complete” : “”;

function handleSessionBack() {
if (sessionStep === “mood”) setSessionStep(“briefing”);
else if (sessionStep === “actions”) exitSession();
else if (sessionStep === “complete”) { if (undoStack.length) handleUndo(); }
else if (sessionStep === “summary”) setSessionStep(“complete”);
}

if (weekStatus === “review”) return (
<div style={{ flex: 1, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, overflow: “hidden” }}>
<WeeklyReviewScreen weekNum={programWeek} totalWeeks={totalWeeks}
actions={sessionJourneyActions} statuses={statuses} mood={mood} streak={streak}
onContinue={handleWeeklyReviewContinue} />
</div>
);
if (weekStatus === “graduated”) return (
<div style={{ flex: 1, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, overflow: “hidden” }}>
<GraduationScreen programName={currentProg?.t || “Journey”} totalWeeks={totalWeeks}
streak={streak} totalActions={totalWeeks * sessionJourneyActions.length} onBrowse={onDiscovery} />
</div>
);

return (
<div style={{ flex: 1, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, overflow: “hidden” }}>

```
  {/* Session sub-header */}
  {todayView === "session" && (
    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10, padding: "6px 20px 8px", flexShrink: 0 }}>
      {canBack && (
        <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.9 }} onClick={handleSessionBack}
          style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 2, background: "none", border: "none", cursor: "pointer", padding: 0, color: T.brand, fontSize: 13.5, fontWeight: 600, flexShrink: 0 }}>
          <Ic id="chevLeft" size={18} color={T.brand} />
          <span>{backLabel}</span>
        </motion.button>
      )}
      <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.2 }}>{sessionTitle}</div>
        {sessionSubtitle && <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{sessionSubtitle}</div>}
      </div>
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.9 }} onClick={exitSession}
        style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 4, padding: "6px 12px", borderRadius: 10, background: T.fill, border: "none", cursor: "pointer" }}>
        <Ic id="list" size={14} color={T.t2} />
        <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t2 }}>Dashboard</span>
      </motion.button>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* Content */}
  <div style={{ flex: 1, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", minHeight: 0 }}>
    <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
      {todayView === "dashboard" ? (
        <motion.div key="dash" initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
          style={{ flex: 1, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", minHeight: 0, overflow: "auto" }}>
          <TodayDashboard
            actions={todayActions}
            statuses={statuses} setStatuses={setStatuses}
            streak={streak}
            onStartJourney={startJourneySession}
          />
        </motion.div>
      ) : (
        <motion.div key="session" initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }}
          style={{ flex: 1, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column",
            justifyContent: sessionStep === "summary" ? "flex-start" : "center",
            overflow: sessionStep === "summary" ? "auto" : "hidden" }}>

          {sessionStep === "briefing" && (
            <BriefingCard briefing={briefing} loading={briefingLoading}
              onContinue={() => setSessionStep("mood")} onSkip={() => setSessionStep("mood")} />
          )}
          {sessionStep === "mood" && (
            <MoodCheck onSelect={m => { setMood(m); setSessionStep("actions"); }} />
          )}
          {sessionStep === "actions" && (
            <>
              <div style={{ position: "relative", height: 340, margin: "0 20px" }}>
                <AnimatePresence>
                  {actionDeck.slice(0, 2).reverse().map((action, i, arr) => (
                    <SwipeCard key={action.id} action={action} isTop={i === arr.length - 1}
                      onComplete={() => processAction("done")}
                      onSkip={() => processAction("skipped")}
                      onDefer={() => processAction("deferred")} />
                  ))}
                </AnimatePresence>
                {/* Progress dots */}
                <div style={{ position: "absolute", bottom: -28, left: 0, right: 0, display: "flex", justifyContent: "center", gap: 4 }}>
                  {sessionJourneyActions.map(a => {
                    const s = statuses[a.id];
                    const isCurrent = actionDeck[0]?.id === a.id;
                    const ac = GA(a.area)?.c || T.brand;
                    const dot = s === "done" ? T.green : s === "skipped" ? T.t3 : s === "deferred" ? T.orange : isCurrent ? ac : `${ac}18`;
                    return <div key={a.id} style={{ width: isCurrent ? 18 : 7, height: 7, borderRadius: 4, background: dot, transition: "all 0.25s" }} />;
                  })}
                </div>
                {/* Undo */}
                <AnimatePresence>
                  {showUndo && undoStack.length > 0 && (
                    <motion.button initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 4 }}
                      whileTap={{ scale: 0.92 }} onClick={handleUndo}
                      style={{ position: "absolute", bottom: -58, left: "50%", transform: "translateX(-50%)", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, padding: "8px 16px", borderRadius: 12, background: "#FFFFFF", border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, boxShadow: "0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.06)", cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: T.brand, whiteSpace: "nowrap" }}>
                      <Ic id="undo" size={14} color={T.brand} />
                      Undo {statuses[undoStack[undoStack.length - 1]?.actionId]}
                    </motion.button>
                  )}
                </AnimatePresence>
              </div>
              <div style={{ marginTop: 52, flexShrink: 0 }}>
                <ActionButtons onSkip={() => processAction("skipped")} onDefer={() => processAction("deferred")} onDone={() => processAction("done")} />
              </div>
            </>
          )}
          {sessionStep === "complete" && (
            <CompletionScreen completed={completed} skipped={skipped} deferred={deferred}
              total={sessionJourneyActions.length} mood={mood} streak={streak}
              onUndo={handleUndo} canUndo={undoStack.length > 0}
              onSummary={() => setSessionStep("summary")} />
          )}
          {sessionStep === "summary" && (
            <DailySummaryScreen actions={sessionJourneyActions} statuses={statuses}
              mood={mood} streak={streak} onDone={handleDoneForToday} />
          )}
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  </div>
</div>
```

);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
TAB 2: PROGRAMS
═══════════════════════════════════ */
/* — Goal Finder (AI-powered program recommendations) — */
function GoalFinder({ onSelectProgram, onClose }) {
const [input, setInput] = useState(””);
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
const [results, setResults] = useState(null); // { intro, programs: [{ id, reason }] }
const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
const [filterArea, setFilterArea] = useState(null);
const scrollRef = useRef(null);

const programCatalog = PRG.map(p => `${p.id}: "${p.t}" (${GA(p.a).n}) - ${p.ds}`).join(”\n”);

// When user taps an area filter, show programs in that area directly
function handleFilterArea(areaId) {
if (filterArea === areaId) {
setFilterArea(null);
setResults(null);
setMessages([]);
return;
}
setFilterArea(areaId);
const areaName = GA(areaId)?.n || areaId;
const matched = PRG.filter(p => p.a === areaId);
setResults({
intro: `Here are the ${areaName.toLowerCase()} journeys available.`,
programs: matched.map(p => ({ id: p.id, reason: p.ds })),
});
setMessages([
{ role: “user”, text: `Show me ${areaName.toLowerCase()} journeys` },
{ role: “assistant”, text: `Here are the ${areaName.toLowerCase()} journeys available.` },
]);
}

async function handleSend() {
if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
const userMsg = input.trim();
setInput(””);
setFilterArea(null);
setMessages(prev => […prev, { role: “user”, text: userMsg }]);
setLoading(true);
setResults(null);

```
try {
  const response = await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", {
    method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: "claude-sonnet-4-20250514", max_tokens: 500,
      system: `You are the Stevo AI helping users find the right self-improvement journeys. Here is the full journey catalog:\n\n${programCatalog}\n\nThe user will describe a goal, problem, or aspiration. Respond with:\n1. A brief 1-2 sentence empathetic acknowledgement of their goal\n2. 2-4 recommended journey IDs from the catalog that best match, with a short reason for each\n\nRespond ONLY with valid JSON, no markdown backticks:\n{"intro":"your acknowledgement","programs":[{"id":"program_id","reason":"why this helps"}]}`,
      messages: [{ role: "user", content: userMsg }],
    }),
  });
  const data = await response.json();
  let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || "").join("") || "";
  text = text.replace(/```json|```/g, "").trim();
  const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
  setResults(parsed);
  setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "assistant", text: parsed.intro }]);
} catch (e) {
  // Fallback: keyword match
  const lower = userMsg.toLowerCase();
  const matched = PRG.filter(p =>
    p.t.toLowerCase().includes(lower) || p.ds.toLowerCase().includes(lower) ||
    GA(p.a).n.toLowerCase().includes(lower)
  ).slice(0, 3);
  const fallback = {
    intro: matched.length > 0
      ? `Here are some journeys that could help with what you're looking for.`
      : `I couldn't find an exact match, but here are some popular journeys to explore.`,
    programs: (matched.length > 0 ? matched : PRG.filter(p => p.f)).map(p => ({
      id: p.id, reason: p.ds
    })),
  };
  setResults(fallback);
  setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "assistant", text: fallback.intro }]);
} finally { setLoading(false); }
```

}

useEffect(() => {
if (scrollRef.current) scrollRef.current.scrollTop = scrollRef.current.scrollHeight;
}, [messages, results, loading]);

const suggestions = [
“I want to find a new job”,
“Help me sleep better”,
“I want to build better habits”,
“How do I manage my money”,
];

// Only show areas that have programs
const areasWithPrograms = AREAS.filter(a => PRG.some(p => p.a === a.id));

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 320, damping: 30 }}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, background: T.meshBg, zIndex: 30, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column” }}>

```
  {/* Header */}
  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "14px 20px 10px", flexShrink: 0 }}>
    <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={onClose}
      style={{ width: 34, height: 34, borderRadius: 17, background: T.fill, border: "none",
        cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
      <Ic id="chevLeft" size={18} color={T.text} />
    </motion.button>
    <div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>Find Your Journey</div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>Tell me what you want to work on</div>
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Area filter chips */}
  <div style={{ padding: "0 20px 8px", flexShrink: 0 }}>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, overflowX: "auto", scrollbarWidth: "none", padding: "2px 0" }}>
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
        onClick={() => { setFilterArea(null); if (messages.length > 0 && filterArea) { setMessages([]); setResults(null); } }}
        style={{ padding: "6px 12px", borderRadius: 10, border: "none", cursor: "pointer", whiteSpace: "nowrap", flexShrink: 0,
          fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, background: !filterArea ? T.brand : T.fill, color: !filterArea ? "white" : T.t2 }}>
        All
      </motion.button>
      {areasWithPrograms.map(a => {
        const count = PRG.filter(p => p.a === a.id).length;
        return (
          <motion.button key={a.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
            onClick={() => handleFilterArea(a.id)}
            style={{ padding: "6px 12px", borderRadius: 10, border: "none", cursor: "pointer", whiteSpace: "nowrap", flexShrink: 0,
              fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 4,
              background: filterArea === a.id ? a.c : T.fill, color: filterArea === a.id ? "white" : T.t2 }}>
            {a.n.split(" ")[0]}
            <span style={{ fontSize: 10, opacity: 0.7 }}>({count})</span>
          </motion.button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Chat area */}
  <div ref={scrollRef} style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: "auto", padding: "8px 20px 16px" }}>

    {/* Empty state with suggestions */}
    {messages.length === 0 && (
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}>
        <div style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 20, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
          padding: 20, marginBottom: 16 }}>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, marginBottom: 12 }}>
            <div style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, background: T.grad,
              display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>M3</span>
            </div>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Stevo</span>
          </div>
          <p style={{ fontSize: 15, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.6, margin: "0 0 16px" }}>
            Describe a goal, challenge, or something you want to improve. I'll recommend the best journeys for you.
          </p>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase",
            letterSpacing: 0.5, marginBottom: 8 }}>Try something like</div>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
            {suggestions.map((s, i) => (
              <motion.button key={i} whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }}
                onClick={() => { setInput(s); }}
                style={{ textAlign: "left", padding: "10px 14px", borderRadius: 12,
                  background: `${T.brand}06`, border: `0.5px solid ${T.brand}15`,
                  cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 14, color: T.brand, fontWeight: 500 }}>
                {s}
              </motion.button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    )}

    {/* Message thread */}
    {messages.map((m, i) => (
      <motion.div key={i} initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: m.role === "user" ? "flex-end" : "flex-start",
          marginBottom: 10 }}>
        <div style={{
          maxWidth: "85%", padding: "12px 16px", borderRadius: 18,
          ...(m.role === "user"
            ? { background: T.brand, color: "white",
                borderBottomRightRadius: 6 }
            : { background: "#FFFFFF", color: T.text, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                borderBottomLeftRadius: 6 }),
          fontSize: 15, lineHeight: 1.55,
        }}>
          {m.text}
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    ))}

    {/* Loading */}
    {loading && (
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
        style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, alignItems: "center", padding: "8px 0" }}>
        <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 8, background: T.grad,
          display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>M3</span>
        </div>
        <motion.div animate={{ opacity: [0.4, 1, 0.4] }} transition={{ duration: 1.5, repeat: Infinity }}
          style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t3 }}>Finding the best journeys for you...</motion.div>
      </motion.div>
    )}

    {/* Program recommendations */}
    {results && results.programs && (
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        style={{ marginTop: 4 }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase",
          letterSpacing: 0.5, marginBottom: 8, paddingLeft: 4 }}>Recommended journeys</div>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 8 }}>
          {results.programs.map((rec, i) => {
            const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === rec.id);
            if (!prog) return null;
            const ar = GA(prog.a);
            return (
              <motion.div key={rec.id}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                transition={{ delay: i * 0.1 }}
                whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }}
                onClick={() => onSelectProgram(prog)}
                style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 16, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                  overflow: "hidden", cursor: "pointer" }}>
                <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "14px 16px" }}>
                  <ProgIcon id={prog.id} area={prog.a} size={44} />
                  <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text, lineHeight: 1.25 }}>{prog.t}</div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 11.5, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>{prog.e} · {prog.w} weeks</div>
                    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginTop: 4 }}>
                      <Dots d={prog.d} />
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3 }}>{prog.u >= 1000 ? (prog.u/1000).toFixed(1)+"k" : prog.u} enrolled</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <Ic id="chevLeft" size={16} color={T.t3} style={{ transform: "rotate(180deg)" }} />
                </div>
                {/* AI reason */}
                <div style={{ padding: "0 16px 12px", display: "flex", gap: 8, alignItems: "flex-start" }}>
                  <div style={{ width: 18, height: 18, borderRadius: 5, background: T.grad, flexShrink: 0, marginTop: 1,
                    display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                    <Ic id="sparkle" size={10} color="white" />
                  </div>
                  <p style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.45, margin: 0 }}>{rec.reason}</p>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Ask again */}
        <div style={{ textAlign: "center", marginTop: 16 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3 }}>Not quite right? Try describing your goal differently below.</span>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    )}
  </div>

  {/* Input bar */}
  <div style={{ padding: "8px 20px 20px", flexShrink: 0,
    background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.55)", backdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)",
    WebkitBackdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)", borderTop: "0.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.5)" }}>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8 }}>
      <input value={input} onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)}
        onKeyDown={e => e.key === "Enter" && handleSend()}
        placeholder="What do you want to work on?"
        style={{ flex: 1, padding: "12px 16px", borderRadius: 14, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
          background: "#FFFFFF", fontSize: 15, color: T.text, outline: "none", fontFamily: "inherit" }} />
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={handleSend}
        disabled={!input.trim() || loading}
        style={{ width: 42, height: 42, borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
          background: input.trim() ? T.grad : T.fill,
          display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0,
          opacity: input.trim() ? 1 : 0.5 }}>
        <svg width={18} height={18} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
          stroke={input.trim() ? "white" : T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round">
          <line x1="22" y1="2" x2="11" y2="13" /><polygon points="22 2 15 22 11 13 2 9 22 2" />
        </svg>
      </motion.button>
    </div>
  </div>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* — Program Builder (AI-powered custom program creation) — */
function ProgramBuilder({ onClose, onSave }) {
const [step, setStep] = useState(“goal”); // goal | details | generating | review | saved
const [goal, setGoal] = useState(””);
const [area, setArea] = useState(null);
const [weeks, setWeeks] = useState(4);
const [minsPerDay, setMinsPerDay] = useState(15);
const [program, setProgram] = useState(null); // AI-generated result
const [editingTitle, setEditingTitle] = useState(false);
const [editTitle, setEditTitle] = useState(””);
const scrollRef = useRef(null);

const areasCatalog = AREAS.map(a => `${a.id}: ${a.n}`).join(”, “);

async function handleGenerate() {
if (!goal.trim()) return;
setStep(“generating”);
try {
const response = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”, {
method: “POST”, headers: { “Content-Type”: “application/json” },
body: JSON.stringify({
model: “claude-sonnet-4-20250514”, max_tokens: 1000,
system: `You are the Stevo AI journey designer. Create a structured self-improvement journey based on the user's goal.\n\nAvailable life areas: ${areasCatalog}\n\nUser preferences: ${area ? `Area: ${area}` : "Auto-detect best area"}, Duration: ${weeks} weeks, Time commitment: ${minsPerDay} min/day.\n\nRespond ONLY with valid JSON, no markdown backticks:\n{\n  "title": "Journey title (concise, action-oriented)",\n  "area": "area_id from list above",\n  "description": "1-2 sentence description",\n  "weeks": ${weeks},\n  "minutesPerDay": ${minsPerDay},\n  "weekPlan": [\n    {\n      "week": 1,\n      "focus": "Week theme (2-3 words)",\n      "actions": [\n        {"title": "Action name", "duration": "X minutes", "description": "Brief how-to"}\n      ]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n\nEach week should have 3-4 daily actions. Make actions specific, actionable, and progressive. Never use em dashes.`,
messages: [{ role: “user”, content: `My goal: ${goal}` }],
}),
});
const data = await response.json();
let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || “”).join(””) || “”;
text = text.replace(/`json|`/g, “”).trim();
const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
setProgram(parsed);
setEditTitle(parsed.title);
setStep(“review”);
} catch (e) {
// Fallback program
const fallback = {
title: `Custom: ${goal.slice(0, 30)}`,
area: area || “personal”,
description: `A personalized journey to help you ${goal.toLowerCase()}.`,
weeks,
minutesPerDay: minsPerDay,
weekPlan: Array.from({ length: weeks }, (_, i) => ({
week: i + 1,
focus: i === 0 ? “Foundation” : i === weeks - 1 ? “Integration” : `Week ${i + 1} Focus`,
actions: [
{ title: “Morning intention setting”, duration: “5 minutes”, description: “Start each day by writing your specific intention for this week’s focus.” },
{ title: “Core practice”, duration: `${Math.max(5, minsPerDay - 10)} minutes`, description: “Dedicated time for your main activity this week.” },
{ title: “Evening reflection”, duration: “5 minutes”, description: “Review what worked, what didn’t, and what to adjust tomorrow.” },
],
})),
};
setProgram(fallback);
setEditTitle(fallback.title);
setStep(“review”);
}
}

function handleRemoveAction(weekIdx, actionIdx) {
setProgram(prev => {
const next = { …prev, weekPlan: prev.weekPlan.map((w, wi) =>
wi === weekIdx ? { …w, actions: w.actions.filter((_, ai) => ai !== actionIdx) } : w
)};
return next;
});
}

function handleSave() {
if (program) {
program.title = editTitle || program.title;
setStep(“saved”);
if (onSave) onSave(program);
}
}

const totalActions = program ? program.weekPlan.reduce((sum, w) => sum + w.actions.length, 0) : 0;

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 320, damping: 30 }}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, background: T.meshBg, zIndex: 35, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column” }}>

```
  {/* Header */}
  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "14px 20px 10px", flexShrink: 0 }}>
    <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={step === "saved" ? onClose : step === "review" ? () => setStep("details") : onClose}
      style={{ width: 34, height: 34, borderRadius: 17, background: T.fill, border: "none",
        cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
      <Ic id={step === "saved" ? "skip" : "chevLeft"} size={18} color={T.text} />
    </motion.button>
    <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>
        {step === "goal" ? "Build Your Journey" : step === "details" ? "Customize" : step === "generating" ? "Creating..." : step === "review" ? "Review Journey" : "Journey Created"}
      </div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>
        {step === "goal" ? "Describe your goal" : step === "details" ? "Set your preferences" : step === "generating" ? "AI is designing your journey" : step === "review" ? "Edit anything before saving" : "Ready to start"}
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* ── Step: Goal ── */}
  {step === "goal" && (
    <div style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: "auto", padding: "8px 20px 20px" }}>
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}>
        <div style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 20, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: 20, marginBottom: 16 }}>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, marginBottom: 14 }}>
            <div style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, background: T.grad,
              display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
              <Ic id="zap" size={16} color="white" />
            </div>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>What's your goal?</span>
          </div>
          <textarea value={goal} onChange={e => setGoal(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="e.g. I want to transition into a product management role, I want to run a half marathon, I want to get my finances under control..."
            rows={4}
            style={{ width: "100%", padding: "14px 16px", borderRadius: 14, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
              background: T.fill, fontSize: 15, color: T.text, outline: "none", fontFamily: "inherit",
              resize: "none", lineHeight: 1.5, boxSizing: "border-box" }} />
        </div>

        {/* Quick suggestions */}
        <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase",
          letterSpacing: 0.5, marginBottom: 8, paddingLeft: 4 }}>Or start from an idea</div>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: 6, marginBottom: 20 }}>
          {[
            "Get promoted at work", "Learn to meditate daily", "Build a side income",
            "Improve my relationship", "Get fit without a gym", "Read more books",
            "Overcome social anxiety", "Start journaling", "Fix my sleep schedule",
          ].map((s, i) => (
            <motion.button key={i} whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
              onClick={() => setGoal(s)}
              style={{ padding: "8px 12px", borderRadius: 10, border: `0.5px solid ${goal === s ? T.brand : T.sep}`,
                background: goal === s ? `${T.brand}08` : "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer",
                fontSize: 13, color: goal === s ? T.brand : T.t2, fontWeight: 500 }}>
              {s}
            </motion.button>
          ))}
        </div>

        <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={() => goal.trim() && setStep("details")}
          disabled={!goal.trim()}
          style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
            background: goal.trim() ? T.grad : T.fill, color: goal.trim() ? "white" : T.t3,
            fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650, opacity: goal.trim() ? 1 : 0.6,
            boxShadow: goal.trim() ? "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2)" : "none" }}>
          Continue
        </motion.button>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Step: Details ── */}
  {step === "details" && (
    <div style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: "auto", padding: "8px 20px 20px" }}>
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}>
        {/* Goal preview */}
        <div style={{ background: `${T.brand}06`, borderRadius: 14, padding: "12px 16px",
          border: `0.5px solid ${T.brand}15`, marginBottom: 20, display: "flex", alignItems: "flex-start", gap: 10 }}>
          <Ic id="target" size={18} color={T.brand} />
          <div>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.brand, marginBottom: 2 }}>Your goal</div>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.text, lineHeight: 1.45 }}>{goal}</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Life area */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 20 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text, marginBottom: 8 }}>Life area</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 10 }}>Pick one, or leave it for AI to decide</div>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: 6 }}>
            <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }} onClick={() => setArea(null)}
              style={{ padding: "7px 12px", borderRadius: 10, border: `0.5px solid ${!area ? T.brand : T.sep}`,
                background: !area ? `${T.brand}08` : "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer",
                fontSize: 12.5, fontWeight: 600, color: !area ? T.brand : T.t2 }}>
              <Ic id="sparkle" size={12} color={!area ? T.brand : T.t3} /> Auto-detect
            </motion.button>
            {AREAS.map(a => (
              <motion.button key={a.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }} onClick={() => setArea(a.id)}
                style={{ padding: "7px 12px", borderRadius: 10, border: `0.5px solid ${area === a.id ? a.c : T.sep}`,
                  background: area === a.id ? `${a.c}10` : "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer",
                  fontSize: 12.5, fontWeight: 600, color: area === a.id ? a.c : T.t2 }}>
                {a.n}
              </motion.button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Duration */}
        <div style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 16, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: 18, marginBottom: 16 }}>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between", marginBottom: 14 }}>
            <div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Duration</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>How many weeks?</div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
              <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={() => setWeeks(w => Math.max(1, w - 1))}
                style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                  background: "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center",
                  fontSize: 18, color: T.text, fontWeight: 500 }}>-</motion.button>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, minWidth: 36, textAlign: "center" }}>{weeks}</span>
              <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={() => setWeeks(w => Math.min(12, w + 1))}
                style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                  background: "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center",
                  fontSize: 18, color: T.text, fontWeight: 500 }}>+</motion.button>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between" }}>
            <div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Time per day</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>Minutes of daily commitment</div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
              <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={() => setMinsPerDay(m => Math.max(5, m - 5))}
                style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                  background: "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center",
                  fontSize: 18, color: T.text, fontWeight: 500 }}>-</motion.button>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, minWidth: 48, textAlign: "center" }}>{minsPerDay}m</span>
              <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={() => setMinsPerDay(m => Math.min(60, m + 5))}
                style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                  background: "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center",
                  fontSize: 18, color: T.text, fontWeight: 500 }}>+</motion.button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={handleGenerate}
          style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
            background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
            display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", gap: 8,
            boxShadow: "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2), 0 2px 6px rgba(108,92,231,0.1), inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.25)" }}>
          <Ic id="sparkle" size={18} color="white" /> Generate My Journey
        </motion.button>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Step: Generating ── */}
  {step === "generating" && (
    <div style={{ flex: 1, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", padding: 40 }}>
      <motion.div
        animate={{ rotate: 360 }}
        transition={{ duration: 2, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
        style={{ width: 56, height: 56, borderRadius: 28, border: `3px solid ${T.fill}`,
          borderTopColor: T.brand, marginBottom: 24 }} />
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} transition={{ delay: 0.3 }}
        style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 8, textAlign: "center" }}>
        Designing your journey
      </motion.div>
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} transition={{ delay: 0.6 }}
        style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t3, textAlign: "center", lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
        Building a {weeks}-week plan with daily actions
        {area ? ` focused on ${GA(area)?.n}` : ""}...
      </motion.div>
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: [0.3, 0.8, 0.3] }}
        transition={{ duration: 2, repeat: Infinity, delay: 1 }}
        style={{ marginTop: 20, fontSize: 13, color: T.t3 }}>
        This usually takes a few seconds
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Step: Review ── */}
  {step === "review" && program && (
    <div ref={scrollRef} style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: "auto", padding: "8px 20px 20px" }}>
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}>
        {/* Title card */}
        <div style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 20, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, padding: 20, marginBottom: 14 }}>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "flex-start", gap: 12 }}>
            <div style={{ width: 48, height: 48, borderRadius: 14, flexShrink: 0,
              background: `linear-gradient(135deg,${GA(program.area)?.c || T.brand}12,${GA(program.area)?.c || T.brand}04)`,
              display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
              <Ic id="zap" size={22} color={GA(program.area)?.c || T.brand} />
            </div>
            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
              {editingTitle ? (
                <input value={editTitle} onChange={e => setEditTitle(e.target.value)}
                  onBlur={() => setEditingTitle(false)} onKeyDown={e => e.key === "Enter" && setEditingTitle(false)}
                  autoFocus
                  style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, border: "none", borderBottom: `2px solid ${T.brand}`,
                    outline: "none", width: "100%", padding: "2px 0", fontFamily: "inherit", background: "transparent" }} />
              ) : (
                <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, lineHeight: 1.3 }}>{editTitle}</div>
                  <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={() => setEditingTitle(true)}
                    style={{ background: "none", border: "none", cursor: "pointer", padding: 2, flexShrink: 0 }}>
                    <Ic id="edit" size={14} color={T.t3} />
                  </motion.button>
                </div>
              )}
              <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3, marginTop: 4 }}>{program.description}</div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Stats */}
          <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginTop: 16 }}>
            {[
              { icon: "calendar", label: `${program.weeks} weeks`, color: T.brand },
              { icon: "clock", label: `${program.minutesPerDay}m/day`, color: T.orange },
              { icon: "list", label: `${totalActions} actions`, color: T.green },
            ].map((s, i) => (
              <div key={i} style={{ flex: 1, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6,
                padding: "8px 10px", borderRadius: 10, background: `${s.color}08` }}>
                <Ic id={s.icon} size={14} color={s.color} />
                <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: s.color }}>{s.label}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Week plan */}
        {program.weekPlan.map((week, wi) => (
          <motion.div key={wi} initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            transition={{ delay: 0.1 + wi * 0.06 }}
            style={{ background: "#FFFFFF", borderRadius: 18, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
              overflow: "hidden", marginBottom: 10 }}>
            {/* Week header */}
            <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10, padding: "12px 16px",
              borderBottom: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}` }}>
              <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 9,
                background: GA(program.area)?.c || T.brand, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>{week.week}</span>
              </div>
              <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Week {week.week}</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{week.focus}</div>
              </div>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{week.actions.length} actions</span>
            </div>
            {/* Actions */}
            {week.actions.map((action, ai) => (
              <div key={ai} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10, padding: "10px 16px",
                borderBottom: ai < week.actions.length - 1 ? `0.5px solid ${T.sep}` : "none" }}>
                <div style={{ width: 6, height: 6, borderRadius: 3, background: GA(program.area)?.c || T.brand, flexShrink: 0 }} />
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 13.5, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>{action.title}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{formatDuration(action.duration)}</div>
                </div>
                <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={() => handleRemoveAction(wi, ai)}
                  style={{ background: "none", border: "none", cursor: "pointer", padding: 4, flexShrink: 0 }}>
                  <Ic id="trash" size={14} color={T.t3} />
                </motion.button>
              </div>
            ))}
          </motion.div>
        ))}

        {/* AI attribution */}
        <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, padding: "8px 0 16px", justifyContent: "center" }}>
          <div style={{ width: 20, height: 20, borderRadius: 6, background: T.grad,
            display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 7, fontWeight: 800, color: "white" }}>M3</span>
          </div>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>AI-generated program. Remove actions you don't need.</span>
        </div>

        {/* Save CTA */}
        <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={handleSave}
          style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
            background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
            display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", gap: 8,
            boxShadow: "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2), 0 2px 6px rgba(108,92,231,0.1), inset 0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.25)" }}>
          <Ic id="check" size={18} color="white" /> Save Journey
        </motion.button>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Step: Saved ── */}
  {step === "saved" && program && (
    <div style={{ flex: 1, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", padding: "40px 20px" }}>
      <motion.div initial={{ scale: 0 }} animate={{ scale: 1 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 20 }}
        style={{ width: 80, height: 80, borderRadius: 40, background: `${T.green}12`,
          display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", marginBottom: 20 }}>
        <Ic id="check" size={36} color={T.green} />
      </motion.div>
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.2 }}>
        <h3 style={{ fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, margin: "0 0 8px", textAlign: "center" }}>
          Journey Created
        </h3>
        <p style={{ fontSize: 15, color: T.t3, margin: "0 0 8px", textAlign: "center", lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
          {editTitle || program.title}
        </p>
        <p style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t3, margin: "0 0 32px", textAlign: "center" }}>
          {program.weeks} weeks · {program.minutesPerDay}m/day · {totalActions} actions
        </p>
      </motion.div>
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.4 }}
        style={{ width: "100%", display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 10 }}>
        <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={onClose}
          style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
            background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
            boxShadow: "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2)" }}>
          Start Journey
        </motion.button>
        <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={onClose}
          style={{ width: "100%", padding: "13px", borderRadius: 14, border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
            background: "#FFFFFF", cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t2 }}>
          Back to Programs
        </motion.button>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  )}
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* ═══ PROGRAM COMMITMENT FLOW ═══ */
function ProgramCommitFlow({ program, onComplete, onCancel }) {
const [step, setStep] = useState(1); // 1=commit, 2=schedule, 3=confirmed
const [days, setDays] = useState([“mon”, “tue”, “wed”, “thu”, “fri”]);
const [time, setTime] = useState(“morning”);
const [reminder, setReminder] = useState(true);
const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(“today”);

const ar = GA(program.a);
const allDays = [
{ id: “mon”, l: “M” }, { id: “tue”, l: “T” }, { id: “wed”, l: “W” },
{ id: “thu”, l: “T” }, { id: “fri”, l: “F” }, { id: “sat”, l: “S” }, { id: “sun”, l: “S” },
];
const times = [
{ id: “morning”, l: “Morning”, sub: “6am – 12pm”, icon: “sun” },
{ id: “afternoon”, l: “Afternoon”, sub: “12pm – 5pm”, icon: “clock” },
{ id: “evening”, l: “Evening”, sub: “5pm – 10pm”, icon: “moon” },
];
const toggleDay = (d) => setDays(prev => prev.includes(d) ? prev.filter(x => x !== d) : […prev, d]);

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: “100%” }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, y: “100%” }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, stiffness: 300, damping: 30 }}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, background: T.meshBg, zIndex: 60, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column” }}>

```
  {/* Header */}
  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "14px 16px",
    background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.55)", backdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)",
    borderBottom: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, flexShrink: 0 }}>
    {step < 3 && (
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.85 }} onClick={step === 1 ? onCancel : () => setStep(step - 1)}
        style={{ width: 34, height: 34, borderRadius: 17, background: T.fill, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
          display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
        <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.text} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round">
          {step === 1 ? <><line x1="18" y1="6" x2="6" y2="18" /><line x1="6" y1="6" x2="18" y2="18" /></> : <polyline points="15 18 9 12 15 6" />}
        </svg>
      </motion.button>
    )}
    <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>{step === 3 ? "You're in!" : "Start Journey"}</div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>Step {Math.min(step, 2)} of 2</div>
    </div>
    {/* Progress dots */}
    <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 4 }}>
      {[1, 2].map(s => (
        <div key={s} style={{ width: s <= step ? 18 : 6, height: 6, borderRadius: 3, background: s <= step ? ar.c : T.fill, transition: "all 0.3s" }} />
      ))}
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Content */}
  <div style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: "auto", padding: "0 0 100px" }}>
    <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
      {/* STEP 1: Commitment overview */}
      {step === 1 && (
        <motion.div key="step1" initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }} transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}>
          <div style={{ padding: "24px 20px 0" }}>
            {/* Program card */}
            <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 16, marginBottom: 24 }}>
              <ProgIcon id={program.id} area={program.a} size={64} />
              <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.3 }}>{program.t}</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3, marginTop: 2 }}>{program.e}</div>
                <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginTop: 6 }}>
                  <Dots d={program.d} />
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{"\u00B7"} {program.w} weeks</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* What you'll commit to */}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 12 }}>What you're committing to</div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 8, marginBottom: 24 }}>
              {[
                { icon: "clock", label: `${program.m} minutes per day`, sub: "Small, focused daily actions" },
                { icon: "calendar", label: `${program.w} weeks total`, sub: "Structured week-by-week progression" },
                { icon: "target", label: `${program.wp?.length || program.w} phases`, sub: "Each building on the last" },
                { icon: "check", label: "Daily check-ins", sub: "Track progress and build streaks" },
              ].map((item, i) => (
                <div key={i} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 14, padding: "14px 16px", borderRadius: 16, background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}` }}>
                  <div style={{ width: 40, height: 40, borderRadius: 12, background: `${ar.c}08`, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
                    <Ic id={item.icon} size={18} color={ar.c} />
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>{item.label}</div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{item.sub}</div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* Week preview */}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 10 }}>Week by week</div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6, marginBottom: 24 }}>
              {(program.wp || []).map((w, i) => (
                <div key={i} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "10px 14px", borderRadius: 14, background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}` }}>
                  <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 9, background: i === 0 ? ar.c : `${ar.c}0C`, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: i === 0 ? "white" : ar.c }}>{i + 1}</span>
                  </div>
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: i === 0 ? T.text : T.t2 }}>{w}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* Start date */}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 10 }}>When do you want to start?</div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginBottom: 16 }}>
              {[{ id: "today", l: "Today", sub: "Jump right in" }, { id: "monday", l: "Next Monday", sub: "Fresh week start" }].map(opt => (
                <motion.button key={opt.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={() => setStartDate(opt.id)}
                  style={{ flex: 1, padding: "14px 12px", borderRadius: 14, border: startDate === opt.id ? `2px solid ${ar.c}` : `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                    background: startDate === opt.id ? `${ar.c}06` : T.sw, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "center" }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: startDate === opt.id ? ar.c : T.text }}>{opt.l}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3, marginTop: 2 }}>{opt.sub}</div>
                </motion.button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      )}

      {/* STEP 2: Schedule setup */}
      {step === 2 && (
        <motion.div key="step2" initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }} transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}>
          <div style={{ padding: "24px 20px 0" }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.3, marginBottom: 4 }}>Set your schedule</div>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 24 }}>Choose when you'll show up for this program</div>

            {/* Active days */}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 10 }}>Which days?</div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, marginBottom: 6 }}>
              {allDays.map((d) => {
                const active = days.includes(d.id);
                return (
                  <motion.button key={d.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.9 }} onClick={() => toggleDay(d.id)}
                    style={{ flex: 1, height: 48, borderRadius: 14, border: active ? `2px solid ${ar.c}` : `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                      background: active ? `${ar.c}08` : T.sw, cursor: "pointer",
                      display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, color: active ? ar.c : T.t3 }}>{d.l}</span>
                  </motion.button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginBottom: 28 }}>
              {[
                { l: "Daily", d: ["mon","tue","wed","thu","fri","sat","sun"] },
                { l: "Weekdays", d: ["mon","tue","wed","thu","fri"] },
                { l: "3x/week", d: ["mon","wed","fri"] },
              ].map(preset => (
                <button key={preset.l} onClick={() => setDays(preset.d)}
                  style={{ padding: "6px 12px", borderRadius: 8, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
                    background: JSON.stringify(days.sort()) === JSON.stringify(preset.d.sort()) ? `${ar.c}12` : T.fill,
                    fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: JSON.stringify(days.sort()) === JSON.stringify(preset.d.sort()) ? ar.c : T.t3 }}>
                  {preset.l}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* Preferred time */}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 10 }}>Best time of day?</div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 8, marginBottom: 28 }}>
              {times.map(t => {
                const active = time === t.id;
                return (
                  <motion.button key={t.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={() => setTime(t.id)}
                    style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 14, padding: "14px 16px", borderRadius: 16,
                      border: active ? `2px solid ${ar.c}` : `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                      background: active ? `${ar.c}06` : T.sw, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "left" }}>
                    <div style={{ width: 40, height: 40, borderRadius: 12, background: active ? `${ar.c}15` : T.fill,
                      display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
                      <Ic id={t.icon} size={18} color={active ? ar.c : T.t3} />
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: active ? ar.c : T.text }}>{t.l}</div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{t.sub}</div>
                    </div>
                    {active && (
                      <div style={{ marginLeft: "auto" }}>
                        <svg width={20} height={20} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={ar.c} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round">
                          <polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" />
                        </svg>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </motion.button>
                );
              })}
            </div>

            {/* Reminder toggle */}
            <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between", padding: "16px", borderRadius: 16, background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}` }}>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12 }}>
                <div style={{ width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: 10, background: `${ar.c}08`, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                  <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={ar.c} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round">
                    <path d="M18 8A6 6 0 006 8c0 7-3 9-3 9h18s-3-2-3-9" /><path d="M13.73 21a2 2 0 01-3.46 0" />
                  </svg>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>Daily reminders</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>Get nudged at your chosen time</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <motion.div whileTap={{ scale: 0.9 }} onClick={() => setReminder(!reminder)}
                style={{ width: 51, height: 31, borderRadius: 16, padding: 2, cursor: "pointer",
                  background: reminder ? ar.c : "rgba(120,120,128,0.16)", transition: "background 0.2s" }}>
                <motion.div animate={{ x: reminder ? 20 : 0 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 500, damping: 30 }}
                  style={{ width: 27, height: 27, borderRadius: 14, background: "white", boxShadow: "0 2px 4px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)" }} />
              </motion.div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      )}

      {/* STEP 3: Confirmation */}
      {step === 3 && (
        <motion.div key="step3" initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }} transition={{ duration: 0.4, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}>
          <div style={{ padding: "48px 20px 0", textAlign: "center" }}>
            {/* Animated check circle */}
            <motion.div initial={{ scale: 0 }} animate={{ scale: 1 }} transition={{ delay: 0.1, type: "spring", stiffness: 200, damping: 15 }}
              style={{ width: 96, height: 96, borderRadius: 48, background: `${ar.c}10`, margin: "0 auto 24px",
                display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
              <motion.div initial={{ scale: 0 }} animate={{ scale: 1 }} transition={{ delay: 0.3, type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 15 }}
                style={{ width: 64, height: 64, borderRadius: 32, background: ar.c,
                  display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                <motion.svg initial={{ pathLength: 0, opacity: 0 }} animate={{ pathLength: 1, opacity: 1 }} transition={{ delay: 0.5, duration: 0.4 }}
                  width={32} height={32} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="white" strokeWidth={3} strokeLinecap="round">
                  <polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" />
                </motion.svg>
              </motion.div>
            </motion.div>

            <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.4 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 800, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.3, marginBottom: 4 }}>You're all set!</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 15, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 32 }}>
                {startDate === "today" ? "Your first day starts now" : "Your journey begins next Monday"}
              </div>
            </motion.div>

            {/* Summary card */}
            <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 15 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.55 }}
              style={{ background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "blur(16px) saturate(180%)", borderRadius: 20, padding: "20px", textAlign: "left", border: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, marginBottom: 24 }}>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 14, marginBottom: 16 }}>
                <ProgIcon id={program.id} area={program.a} size={50} />
                <div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>{program.t}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>{program.e}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr 1fr", gap: 8 }}>
                {[
                  { l: "Duration", v: `${program.w} weeks` },
                  { l: "Schedule", v: `${days.length} days/wk` },
                  { l: "Time", v: time.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + time.slice(1) },
                ].map((s, i) => (
                  <div key={i} style={{ padding: "10px 6px", borderRadius: 12, background: `${ar.c}06`, textAlign: "center" }}>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, color: ar.c }}>{s.v}</div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>{s.l}</div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
              {reminder && (
                <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, marginTop: 12, padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: 12, background: T.fill }}>
                  <svg width={14} height={14} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round">
                    <path d="M18 8A6 6 0 006 8c0 7-3 9-3 9h18s-3-2-3-9" /><path d="M13.73 21a2 2 0 01-3.46 0" />
                  </svg>
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t2 }}>Daily reminders {time === "morning" ? "at 7:00 AM" : time === "afternoon" ? "at 12:30 PM" : "at 6:00 PM"}</span>
                </div>
              )}
            </motion.div>

            {/* Motivational note */}
            <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} transition={{ delay: 0.7 }}
              style={{ padding: "16px", borderRadius: 16, background: `linear-gradient(135deg,${ar.c}08,${ar.c}03)`, border: `0.5px solid ${ar.c}12`, marginBottom: 16 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.6, fontStyle: "italic" }}>
                "The secret of getting ahead is getting started."
              </div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3, marginTop: 4 }}>— Mark Twain</div>
            </motion.div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  </div>

  {/* Bottom CTA */}
  <div style={{ padding: "8px 20px 20px", background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.55)", backdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "saturate(180%) blur(24px)",
    borderTop: "0.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.5)", flexShrink: 0 }}>
    {step === 1 && (
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={() => setStep(2)}
        style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
          background: ar.c, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
          boxShadow: `0 6px 20px ${ar.c}30` }}>
        I'm ready — set my schedule
      </motion.button>
    )}
    {step === 2 && (
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={() => setStep(3)}
        disabled={days.length === 0}
        style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: days.length > 0 ? "pointer" : "default",
          background: days.length > 0 ? T.grad : T.fill, color: days.length > 0 ? "white" : T.t3, fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
          boxShadow: days.length > 0 ? "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2)" : "none", opacity: days.length > 0 ? 1 : 0.6 }}>
        Confirm & start program
      </motion.button>
    )}
    {step === 3 && (
      <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }} onClick={onComplete}
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.6 }}
        style={{ width: "100%", padding: "15px", borderRadius: 14, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
          background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 650,
          boxShadow: "0 6px 20px rgba(108,92,231,0.2)" }}>
        {startDate === "today" ? "Go to Today's Actions" : "Done"}
      </motion.button>
    )}
  </div>
</motion.div>
```

);
}
