/* ═══════════════════════════════════
TAB 3: PROGRESS (Wheel of Life)
═══════════════════════════════════ */

function polarToCart(cx, cy, r, angleDeg) {
const rad = ((angleDeg - 90) * Math.PI) / 180;
return { x: cx + r * Math.cos(rad), y: cy + r * Math.sin(rad) };
}
function scoreLabel(s) { return s <= 3 ? “Needs focus” : s <= 5 ? “Building” : s <= 7 ? “Growing” : s <= 8 ? “Strong” : “Thriving”; }
function scoreTier(s) {
if (s <= 3) return { bg: “#FF2D5512”, color: “#FF2D55” };
if (s <= 5) return { bg: “#FF950012”, color: “#FF9500” };
if (s <= 7) return { bg: “#007AFF12”, color: “#007AFF” };
return { bg: “#34C75912”, color: “#34C759” };
}
const SCORE_TIERS = [
{ range: “1-3”, label: “Needs focus”, c: “#FF2D55” },
{ range: “4-5”, label: “Building”, c: “#FF9500” },
{ range: “6-7”, label: “Growing”, c: “#007AFF” },
{ range: “8-10”, label: “Strong”, c: “#34C759” },
];
function ScoreTierChips() {
return (
<div style={{ display: “flex”, flexWrap: “wrap”, gap: 5 }}>
{SCORE_TIERS.map((s) => (
<div key={s.range} style={{ padding: “3px 9px”, borderRadius: 7, background: `${s.c}10`, fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 650, color: s.c, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 4 }}>
<div style={{ width: 6, height: 6, borderRadius: 3, background: s.c }} />{s.range}: {s.label}
</div>
))}
</div>
);
}

function WheelOfLife({ areas, size = 340, onTapArea, tappedIdx, compareScores, appScores }) {
const cx = size / 2, cy = size / 2, outerR = size / 2 - 48;
const n = areas.length, wedgeAngle = 360 / n, gapDeg = 2;
return (
<svg width={size} height={size} viewBox={`0 0 ${size} ${size}`}>
<defs>
{areas.map((a, i) => (
<radialGradient key={`rg-${i}`} id={`wfg-${i}`} cx=“50%” cy=“50%” r=“55%”>
<stop offset="0%" stopColor={a.c} stopOpacity="0.75" />
<stop offset="100%" stopColor={a.c} stopOpacity="0.45" />
</radialGradient>
))}
<radialGradient id="wfg-empty" cx="50%" cy="50%" r="55%">
<stop offset="0%" stopColor="#E5E5EA" stopOpacity="0.3" />
<stop offset="100%" stopColor="#E5E5EA" stopOpacity="0.12" />
</radialGradient>
</defs>
<circle cx={cx} cy={cy} r={outerR + 1} fill=”#FAFAFA” />
{[2, 4, 6, 8, 10].map((r) => (
<circle key={r} cx={cx} cy={cy} r={(r / 10) * outerR} fill=“none” stroke=“rgba(60,60,67,0.05)” strokeWidth={0.5} />
))}
{areas.map((a, i) => {
const sa = i * wedgeAngle + gapDeg / 2, ea = (i + 1) * wedgeAngle - gapDeg / 2;
const pS = polarToCart(cx, cy, outerR, sa), pE = polarToCart(cx, cy, outerR, ea);
return <path key={`bg-${i}`} d={`M${cx},${cy} L${pS.x},${pS.y} A${outerR},${outerR} 0 0 1 ${pE.x},${pE.y} Z`} fill=“url(#wfg-empty)” />;
})}
{compareScores && areas.map((a, i) => {
const pastScore = compareScores[a.id] || 0;
const sa = i * wedgeAngle + gapDeg / 2, ea = (i + 1) * wedgeAngle - gapDeg / 2;
const r = (pastScore / 10) * outerR;
if (r < 3) return null;
const pS = polarToCart(cx, cy, r, sa), pE = polarToCart(cx, cy, r, ea);
return <path key={`ghost-${i}`} d={`M${cx},${cy} L${pS.x},${pS.y} A${r},${r} 0 0 1 ${pE.x},${pE.y} Z`} fill=“none” stroke={a.c} strokeWidth={1.5} strokeDasharray=“4,3” opacity={0.4} style={{ pointerEvents: “none” }} />;
})}
{/* App score ring — dashed outline showing activity-based score */}
{appScores && areas.map((a, i) => {
const appS = appScores[a.id] || 1;
const sa = i * wedgeAngle + gapDeg / 2, ea = (i + 1) * wedgeAngle - gapDeg / 2;
const r = (appS / 10) * outerR;
if (r < 3) return null;
const pS = polarToCart(cx, cy, r, sa), pE = polarToCart(cx, cy, r, ea);
return <path key={`app-${i}`} d={`M${cx},${cy} L${pS.x},${pS.y} A${r},${r} 0 0 1 ${pE.x},${pE.y} Z`}
fill=“none” stroke={a.c} strokeWidth={2} strokeDasharray=“5,3” opacity={0.55} style={{ pointerEvents: “none” }} />;
})}
{areas.map((a, i) => {
const sa = i * wedgeAngle + gapDeg / 2, ea = (i + 1) * wedgeAngle - gapDeg / 2;
const r = (a.score / 10) * outerR;
if (r < 3) return null;
const pS = polarToCart(cx, cy, r, sa), pE = polarToCart(cx, cy, r, ea);
const isTapped = tappedIdx === i;
return <path key={`fill-${i}`} d={`M${cx},${cy} L${pS.x},${pS.y} A${r},${r} 0 0 1 ${pE.x},${pE.y} Z`} fill={`url(#wfg-${i})`} opacity={tappedIdx !== null && !isTapped ? 0.35 : 1} style={{ transition: “opacity 0.25s”, cursor: “pointer” }} onClick={() => onTapArea?.(i)} />;
})}
{areas.map((_, i) => {
const end = polarToCart(cx, cy, outerR + 1, i * wedgeAngle);
return <line key={`sep-${i}`} x1={cx} y1={cy} x2={end.x} y2={end.y} stroke=“white” strokeWidth={2} style={{ pointerEvents: “none” }} />;
})}
<circle cx={cx} cy={cy} r={outerR + 1} fill=“none” stroke=“rgba(60,60,67,0.06)” strokeWidth={1} />
<circle cx={cx} cy={cy} r={22} fill="white" stroke="rgba(60,60,67,0.08)" strokeWidth={1} />
<text x={cx} y={cy - 3} textAnchor=“middle” dominantBaseline=“central” style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 800, fill: T.text, fontFamily: “-apple-system,sans-serif” }}>
{(areas.reduce((s, a) => s + a.score, 0) / areas.length).toFixed(1)}
</text>
<text x={cx} y={cy + 10} textAnchor=“middle” dominantBaseline=“central” style={{ fontSize: 7.5, fontWeight: 600, fill: T.t3, fontFamily: “-apple-system,sans-serif”, letterSpacing: 0.3 }}>AVG</text>
{areas.map((a, i) => {
const midAngle = (i + 0.5) * wedgeAngle, iconR = outerR + 28;
const ip = polarToCart(cx, cy, iconR, midAngle);
const isTapped = tappedIdx === i;
return (
<g key={`ic-${i}`} style={{ cursor: “pointer” }} onClick={() => onTapArea?.(i)}>
<circle cx={ip.x} cy={ip.y} r={isTapped ? 19 : 16} fill={isTapped ? a.c : “white”} stroke={isTapped ? a.c : “rgba(60,60,67,0.1)”} strokeWidth={isTapped ? 0 : 1} style={{ transition: “all 0.25s” }} />
<svg x={ip.x - 8} y={ip.y - 8} width={16} height={16} viewBox=“0 0 24 24” fill=“none” stroke={isTapped ? “white” : a.c} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap=“round” strokeLinejoin=“round” style={{ pointerEvents: “none” }}>{AREA_ICONS[a.icon]}</svg>
</g>
);
})}
</svg>
);
}

function WheelAreaDetail({ area, compareScore, compareLabel, appScore, onSelectProgram }) {
const tier = scoreTier(area.score);
const change = area.score - area.start;
const compChange = compareScore != null ? area.score - compareScore : null;
const myProgs = getAreaPrograms(area.id);
const availProgs = getAvailablePrograms(area.id);
const STATUS_STYLES = { active: { label: “In Progress”, color: T.green }, queued: { label: “Up Next”, color: T.orange }, completed: { label: “Completed”, color: T.brand } };

// Get all ITEMS in this area — includes primary AND secondary area items
// Items are tagged with a role label (Primary/Secondary) for display
const withRole = (items) => items.map(i => ({
…i,
_role: i.area === area.id ? “primary” : “secondary”,
_weight: areaWeight(i, area.id),
}));
const areaProjects = withRole(ITEMS.filter(i => areaWeight(i, area.id) > 0 && i.status === “active” && i.steps?.length > 0));
const areaHabits   = withRole(ITEMS.filter(i => areaWeight(i, area.id) > 0 && i.status === “active” && i.recurrence));
const areaActions  = withRole(ITEMS.filter(i => areaWeight(i, area.id) > 0 && i.status === “active” && !i.steps?.length && !i.recurrence));
const areaPaused   = ITEMS.filter(i => i.area === area.id && i.status === “paused”);
const areaGoals    = ITEMS.filter(i => i.area === area.id && i.status === “someday”);
// Journeys: check primary + secondary areas
const myProgsWeighted = myProgs.map(p => {
const prog = PRG.find(x => x.id === p.id);
const w = journeyAreaWeight(prog, area.id);
return w > 0 ? { …p, _weight: w, _role: prog?.a === area.id ? “primary” : “secondary” } : null;
}).filter(Boolean);
const activeJourneys = myProgsWeighted.filter(p => p.status === “active”);
const totalContributing = activeJourneys.length + areaProjects.length + areaHabits.length;
const totalItems = myProgsWeighted.length + areaProjects.length + areaHabits.length + areaActions.length;

// Score momentum: projected next score based on active work
const projectedScore = totalContributing > 0
? Math.min(10, area.score + Math.min(2, Math.round(totalContributing * 0.5)))
: null;

// Contribution badge — type pill
const ContribBadge = ({ type }) => {
const cfg = {
journey: { label: “Learning”, color: T.brand },
project: { label: “Executing”, color: T.green },
habit:   { label: “Practising”, color: T.orange },
}[type] || { label: “Active”, color: T.t3 };
return (
<span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 700, padding: “2px 6px”, borderRadius: 5,
background: `${cfg.color}12`, color: cfg.color, letterSpacing: 0.2 }}>
↑ {cfg.label}
</span>
);
};

// Role badge — shows whether this item’s primary or secondary area
const RoleBadge = ({ weight }) => {
if (weight >= 1.0) return null; // primary — no badge needed, it’s the home area
const label = weight >= 0.5 ? “Also improves” : “Minor benefit”;
return (
<span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 600, padding: “2px 6px”, borderRadius: 5,
background: `${T.t3}10`, color: T.t3, letterSpacing: 0.2 }}>
{label}
</span>
);
};

const insight = appScore != null ? appScoreInsight(area.score, appScore) : null;
const insightColors = { aligned: T.green, overconfident: T.orange, undervalued: T.brand };

return (
<div style={{ margin: “0 16px”, padding: “16px”, borderRadius: 18, background: `${area.c}06`, border: `1px solid ${area.c}12` }}>

```
  {/* Header row */}
  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12 }}>
    <div style={{ width: 42, height: 42, borderRadius: 14, background: `${area.c}12`, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
      <AreaIcon area={area} size={20} />
    </div>
    <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8 }}>
        <span style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>{area.n}</span>
        <span style={{ padding: "2px 8px", borderRadius: 6, fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, background: tier.bg, color: tier.color }}>{scoreLabel(area.score)}</span>
      </div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3, marginTop: 2 }}>
        {totalContributing > 0
          ? `${totalContributing} thing${totalContributing !== 1 ? "s" : ""} actively improving your score`
          : "Nothing active yet — score won't improve on its own"}
      </div>
    </div>
    {/* Dual score display */}
    <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, flexShrink: 0 }}>
      <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "6px 10px", borderRadius: 12, background: area.c, color: "white", minWidth: 44 }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 800, lineHeight: 1 }}>{area.score}</div>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 8, fontWeight: 600, opacity: 0.75, marginTop: 1 }}>YOU</div>
      </div>
      {appScore != null && (
        <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "6px 10px", borderRadius: 12, background: `${area.c}12`, border: `1.5px dashed ${area.c}50`, minWidth: 44 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 800, lineHeight: 1, color: area.c }}>{appScore}</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 8, fontWeight: 700, color: area.c, opacity: 0.7, marginTop: 1 }}>APP</div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Insight banner */}
  {insight && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 12, padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: 12,
      background: `${insightColors[insight.type]}08`, border: `0.5px solid ${insightColors[insight.type]}20`,
      display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8 }}>
      <span style={{ fontSize: 14 }}>
        {insight.type === "aligned" ? "✓" : insight.type === "overconfident" ? "🤔" : "💪"}
      </span>
      <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.45, fontWeight: 500 }}>{insight.msg}</span>
    </div>
  )}

  <p style={{ fontSize: 12.5, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.55, margin: "12px 0 0", padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: 12, background: `${area.c}04` }}>{area.desc}</p>

  {/* Score bar with projected marker */}
  <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between", marginBottom: 5 }}>
      <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{compareScore != null ? `${compareLabel}: ${compareScore}/10` : `Started at ${area.start}/10`}</span>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6 }}>
        {projectedScore && projectedScore > area.score && (
          <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 600, color: area.c, opacity: 0.7 }}>
            → {projectedScore} if you keep going
          </span>
        )}
        <span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, color: (compChange ?? change) > 0 ? T.green : (compChange ?? change) < 0 ? T.red : T.t3 }}>
          {(() => { const d = compChange ?? change; return d > 0 ? `+${d}` : d < 0 ? `${d}` : "No change"; })()}
        </span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style={{ position: "relative", height: 6, borderRadius: 3, background: `${area.c}12` }}>
      {/* Baseline marker */}
      <div style={{ position: "absolute", left: `${(compareScore ?? area.start) * 10}%`, top: -2, width: 2, height: 10, borderRadius: 1, background: `${area.c}40` }} />
      {/* Projected marker */}
      {projectedScore && projectedScore > area.score && (
        <div style={{ position: "absolute", left: `${projectedScore * 10}%`, top: -3, width: 2, height: 12, borderRadius: 1,
          background: area.c, opacity: 0.3, borderStyle: "dashed" }} />
      )}
      {/* Current fill */}
      <div style={{ height: "100%", borderRadius: 3, background: area.c, width: `${area.score * 10}%`, transition: "width 0.4s" }} />
    </div>
    <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", marginTop: 3 }}>
      <span style={{ fontSize: 9, color: T.t3 }}>1</span><span style={{ fontSize: 9, color: T.t3 }}>5</span><span style={{ fontSize: 9, color: T.t3 }}>10</span>
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* ── What's improving this score ── */}
  {totalContributing === 0 && totalItems === 0 && availProgs.length === 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14, padding: 16, borderRadius: 14, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}`, textAlign: "center" }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text, marginBottom: 2 }}>Nothing in {area.n} yet</div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 10 }}>Add a goal, habit, or start a journey to move this score</div>
      <button style={{ padding: "8px 18px", borderRadius: 10, border: `1.5px solid ${area.c}`, background: `${area.c}08`, cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 650, color: area.c }}>Browse {area.n} journeys</button>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Journeys (enrolled programs) ── */}
  {myProgsWeighted.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t2, letterSpacing: -0.2, marginBottom: 8 }}>Journeys</div>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
        {myProgsWeighted.map((p) => {
          const st = STATUS_STYLES[p.status];
          return (
            <div key={p.id} onClick={() => onSelectProgram?.(p)} style={{ padding: "12px 14px", borderRadius: 14, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}`, cursor: "pointer" }}>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
                <ProgIcon id={p.id} area={p.a} size={34} />
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginBottom: 2, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>{p.t}</span>
                    {p.status === "active" && <ContribBadge type="journey" />}
                    <RoleBadge weight={p._weight} />
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{p.e}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ padding: "3px 8px", borderRadius: 7, fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 650, background: `${st.color}10`, color: st.color }}>{st.label}</div>
                <svg width={14} height={14} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="9 18 15 12 9 6" /></svg>
              </div>
              {p.status === "active" && (
                <div style={{ marginTop: 8 }}>
                  <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", marginBottom: 4 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3 }}>Week {p.week}, Day {p.day}</span>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, color: area.c }}>{p.pct}%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ height: 4, borderRadius: 2, background: `${area.c}12`, overflow: "hidden" }}>
                    <div style={{ height: "100%", borderRadius: 2, background: area.c, width: `${p.pct}%` }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
              {p.status === "completed" && (
                <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 5, marginTop: 6 }}>
                  <svg width={12} height={12} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.green} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" /></svg>
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.green, fontWeight: 500 }}>Completed all {p.w} weeks</span>
                </div>
              )}
              {p.status === "queued" && <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3, marginTop: 4 }}>Starts after current journey</div>}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Projects ── */}
  {areaProjects.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t2, letterSpacing: -0.2, marginBottom: 8 }}>Projects</div>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
        {areaProjects.map((item) => {
          const doneSteps = item.steps?.filter(s => s.done).length || 0;
          const totalSteps = item.steps?.length || 0;
          const pct = totalSteps > 0 ? Math.round((doneSteps / totalSteps) * 100) : 0;
          return (
            <div key={item.id} style={{ padding: "12px 14px", borderRadius: 14, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}` }}>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
                <div style={{ width: 34, height: 34, borderRadius: 10, background: `${area.c}08`,
                  display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 16 }}>{item.emoji}</span>
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginBottom: 2, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>{item.title}</span>
                    <ContribBadge type="project" />
                    <RoleBadge weight={item._weight} />
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>
                    {item.deadline ? `Due ${new Date(item.deadline).toLocaleDateString("en-US", { month: "short", day: "numeric" })}` :
                     totalSteps > 0 ? `${doneSteps} of ${totalSteps} steps done` : ""}
                  </div>
                </div>
                {totalSteps > 0 && (
                  <div style={{ width: 36, height: 36, position: "relative", flexShrink: 0 }}>
                    <svg width={36} height={36} viewBox="0 0 36 36">
                      <circle cx={18} cy={18} r={14} fill="none" stroke={`${area.c}15`} strokeWidth={3} />
                      <circle cx={18} cy={18} r={14} fill="none" stroke={area.c} strokeWidth={3}
                        strokeDasharray={`${(doneSteps / totalSteps) * 87.96} 87.96`}
                        strokeLinecap="round" transform="rotate(-90 18 18)" />
                    </svg>
                    <span style={{ position: "absolute", inset: 0, display: "flex", alignItems: "center",
                      justifyContent: "center", fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>{pct}%</span>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
              {totalSteps > 0 && (
                <div style={{ marginTop: 8, display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 3 }}>
                  {item.steps.slice(0, 3).map(step => (
                    <div key={step.id} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6 }}>
                      <div style={{ width: 14, height: 14, borderRadius: 7, flexShrink: 0,
                        border: step.done ? `2px solid ${T.green}` : `2px solid ${area.c}30`,
                        background: step.done ? T.green : "transparent",
                        display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                        {step.done && <svg width={7} height={7} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="white" strokeWidth={3.5} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg>}
                      </div>
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: step.done ? T.t3 : T.t2, fontWeight: 500,
                        textDecoration: step.done ? "line-through" : "none" }}>{step.title}</span>
                      {step.today && !step.done && <span style={{ fontSize: 8, fontWeight: 700, color: T.brand, background: `${T.brand}0D`, padding: "1px 5px", borderRadius: 3 }}>TODAY</span>}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                  {item.steps.length > 3 && (
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, paddingLeft: 20 }}>+{item.steps.length - 3} more steps</span>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Habits ── */}
  {areaHabits.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t2, letterSpacing: -0.2, marginBottom: 8 }}>Habits</div>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
        {areaHabits.map((item) => (
          <div key={item.id} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10, padding: "10px 14px", borderRadius: 14, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}` }}>
            <div style={{ width: 34, height: 34, borderRadius: 10, background: `${area.c}08`,
              display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 16 }}>{item.emoji}</span>
            </div>
            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginBottom: 2, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>{item.title}</span>
                <ContribBadge type="habit" />
                <RoleBadge weight={item._weight} />
              </div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{formatRecurrence(item.recurrence)}</div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 4 }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3 }}>{formatDuration(item.habitDuration)}</span>
              <svg width={14} height={14} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.orange} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round" style={{ opacity: 0.5 }}>
                <polyline points="23 4 23 10 17 10" /><path d="M20.49 15a9 9 0 11-2.12-9.36L23 10" />
              </svg>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── To-Do ── */}
  {areaActions.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t2, letterSpacing: -0.2, marginBottom: 8 }}>To-Do</div>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
        {areaActions.map((item) => (
          <div key={item.id} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10, padding: "10px 14px", borderRadius: 14, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}` }}>
            <div style={{ width: 34, height: 34, borderRadius: 10, background: `${area.c}08`,
              display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0 }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 16 }}>{item.emoji}</span>
            </div>
            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>{item.title}</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{formatDuration(item.taskDuration)}</div>
            </div>
            <svg width={14} height={14} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round" style={{ opacity: 0.4 }}>
              <polyline points="9 18 15 12 9 6" />
            </svg>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Goals in this area ── */}
  {areaGoals.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t2, letterSpacing: -0.2, marginBottom: 8 }}>Goals</div>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
        {areaGoals.map((item) => {
          const gp = goalProgress(item);
          const linked = getGoalLinkedItems(item);
          return (
            <div key={item.id} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, padding: "8px 12px", borderRadius: 12, background: "rgba(155,89,182,0.03)", border: `0.5px solid rgba(155,89,182,0.1)`, width: "100%" }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize: 14, flexShrink: 0 }}>{item.emoji}</span>
              <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>{item.title}</span>
                {linked.length > 0 && (
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>{linked.length} linked · {Math.round(gp * 100)}%</div>
                )}
              </div>
              {linked.length > 0 && (
                <div style={{ width: 28, height: 3, borderRadius: 2, background: `${area.c}15`, overflow: "hidden", flexShrink: 0 }}>
                  <div style={{ height: "100%", borderRadius: 2, background: area.c, width: `${Math.round(gp * 100)}%` }} />
                </div>
              )}
              <Ic id="target" size={12} color="#9B59B6" />
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Paused items ── */}
  {areaPaused.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t2, letterSpacing: -0.2, marginBottom: 8 }}>Paused</div>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: 6, opacity: 0.55 }}>
        {areaPaused.map((item) => (
          <div key={item.id} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, padding: "6px 12px", borderRadius: 10, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}` }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 14 }}>{item.emoji}</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 500, color: T.t2 }}>{item.title}</span>
            <svg width={10} height={10} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round">
              <rect x="6" y="4" width="4" height="16" /><rect x="14" y="4" width="4" height="16" />
            </svg>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Available journeys ── */}
  {availProgs.length > 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t2, letterSpacing: -0.2, marginBottom: 8 }}>Available Journeys</div>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 5 }}>
        {availProgs.slice(0, 3).map((p) => (
          <div key={p.id} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10, padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: 12, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}`, cursor: "pointer" }}>
            <ProgIcon id={p.id} area={p.a} size={30} />
            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>{p.t}</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3 }}>{p.e} · {p.w}w</div>
            </div>
            <Dots d={p.d} />
          </div>
        ))}
        {availProgs.length > 3 && <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: area.c, fontWeight: 600, textAlign: "center", padding: "4px 0", cursor: "pointer" }}>+{availProgs.length - 3} more journeys</div>}
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Empty state ── */}
  {totalItems === 0 && availProgs.length === 0 && (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 14, padding: 16, borderRadius: 14, background: T.glass, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}`, textAlign: "center" }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text, marginBottom: 2 }}>Nothing in {area.n} yet</div>
      <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 10 }}>Add a goal, habit, or start a journey</div>
      <button style={{ padding: "8px 18px", borderRadius: 10, border: `1.5px solid ${area.c}`, background: `${area.c}08`, cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 650, color: area.c }}>Browse {area.n} journeys</button>
    </div>
  )}
</div>
```

);
}

function WheelProgramDetail({ program, onBack }) {
const [expandedWeek, setExpandedWeek] = useState(program.week || 1);
const prg = PRG.find(p => p.id === program.id) || {};
const ar = GA(prg.a);
const st = { active: { label: “In Progress”, color: T.green }, queued: { label: “Up Next”, color: T.orange }, completed: { label: “Completed”, color: T.brand } }[program.status];
const completedDays = program.weeks.reduce((sum, w) => sum + w.days.filter(d => d.done).length, 0);
const totalDays = prg.w * 7;

return (
<div style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: “auto”, paddingBottom: 120, WebkitOverflowScrolling: “touch” }}>
<div style={{ padding: “12px 16px 0” }}>
<button onClick={onBack} style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 4, background: “none”, border: “none”, cursor: “pointer”, padding: “4px 0”, marginBottom: 8 }}>
<svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.brand} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="15 18 9 12 15 6" /></svg>
<span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.brand }}>{ar?.n || “Back”}</span>
</button>
</div>
<div style={{ padding: “0 16px 12px” }}>
<div style={{ background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: T.glassBlur, WebkitBackdropFilter: T.glassBlur, borderRadius: 22, padding: 20, boxShadow: `${T.cardShadow}, ${T.cardHighlight}`, border: T.cardBorder }}>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 14 }}>
<ProgIcon id={program.id} area={prg.a} size={50} />
<div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
<div style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.3 }}>{prg.t}</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3, marginTop: 2 }}>{prg.e} · {prg.w} weeks · {prg.d}</div>
</div>
</div>
<div style={{ marginTop: 16, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 10 }}>
<div style={{ padding: “4px 10px”, borderRadius: 8, fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, background: `${st.color}10`, color: st.color }}>{st.label}</div>
{program.status === “active” && <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>Week {program.week}, Day {program.day}</span>}
{program.status === “completed” && <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.green, fontWeight: 600 }}>All {prg.w} weeks completed</span>}
</div>
{program.status !== “queued” && (
<div style={{ marginTop: 12 }}>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, justifyContent: “space-between”, marginBottom: 4 }}>
<span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>{completedDays} of {totalDays} days</span>
<span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, color: ar?.c }}>{program.pct}%</span>
</div>
<div style={{ height: 6, borderRadius: 3, background: `${ar?.c}12`, overflow: “hidden” }}>
<div style={{ height: “100%”, borderRadius: 3, background: ar?.c, width: `${program.pct}%` }} />
</div>
</div>
)}
</div>
</div>
<div style={{ padding: “0 16px” }}>
<div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 10 }}>Program Weeks</div>
{program.weeks.length === 0 ? (
<div style={{ background: T.glass, backdropFilter: “blur(16px)”, WebkitBackdropFilter: “blur(16px)”, borderRadius: 18, padding: “24px 20px”, textAlign: “center”, boxShadow: T.cardShadow, border: T.cardBorder }}>
<div style={{ fontSize: 28, marginBottom: 8 }}>{”\uD83D\uDCCB”}</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>Program content loading</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3, marginTop: 4 }}>{program.status === “queued” ? “Full content available when this journey becomes active.” : “Detailed weekly content will appear here.”}</div>
</div>
) : (
<div style={{ display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, gap: 10 }}>
{program.weeks.map((wk) => {
const isExpanded = expandedWeek === wk.w, isCurrent = wk.w === program.week;
const wkDone = wk.days.filter(d => d.done).length, wkTotal = wk.days.length;
const wkPct = Math.round((wkDone / wkTotal) * 100), allDone = wkDone === wkTotal;
return (
<div key={wk.w} style={{ background: T.glass, backdropFilter: “blur(16px) saturate(180%)”, WebkitBackdropFilter: “blur(16px) saturate(180%)”, borderRadius: 20, overflow: “hidden”, border: isCurrent ? `1.5px solid ${ar?.c}30` : `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, boxShadow: isCurrent ? `0 2px 12px ${ar?.c}10` : “0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.04)” }}>
<button onClick={() => setExpandedWeek(isExpanded ? null : wk.w)} style={{ width: “100%”, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, padding: “14px 16px”, background: “none”, border: “none”, cursor: “pointer”, gap: 12 }}>
<div style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, background: allDone ? `${T.green}12` : isCurrent ? `${ar?.c}12` : T.fill, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, flexShrink: 0 }}>
{allDone ? <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.green} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" /></svg>
: <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 800, color: isCurrent ? ar?.c : T.t3 }}>{wk.w}</span>}
</div>
<div style={{ flex: 1, textAlign: “left” }}>
<div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Week {wk.w}: {wk.title}{isCurrent && <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, color: ar?.c, marginLeft: 6 }}>CURRENT</span>}</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>{wkDone}/{wkTotal} days · {wkPct}%</div>
</div>
<svg width={14} height={14} viewBox=“0 0 24 24” fill=“none” stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap=“round” style={{ transform: isExpanded ? “rotate(180deg)” : “rotate(0deg)”, transition: “transform 0.2s”, flexShrink: 0 }}><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9" /></svg>
</button>
<div style={{ height: 3, background: `${ar?.c}08`, margin: “0 16px” }}>
<div style={{ height: “100%”, background: allDone ? T.green : ar?.c, width: `${wkPct}%`, borderRadius: 2 }} />
</div>
{isExpanded && (
<div style={{ padding: “12px 16px 16px” }}>
{wk.days.map((day, di) => {
const isToday = isCurrent && day.d === program.day;
return (
<div key={di} style={{ padding: “12px 14px”, borderRadius: 14, marginBottom: 8, background: isToday ? `${ar?.c}05` : day.done ? `${T.green}04` : “transparent”, border: isToday ? `1px solid ${ar?.c}15` : day.done ? `0.5px solid ${T.green}10` : `0.5px solid ${T.sep}` }}>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 10, marginBottom: 6 }}>
<div style={{ width: 22, height: 22, borderRadius: 11, background: day.done ? T.green : isToday ? ar?.c : T.fill, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”, flexShrink: 0 }}>
{day.done ? <svg width={12} height={12} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="white" strokeWidth={3} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" /></svg>
: <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, color: isToday ? “white” : T.t3 }}>{day.d}</span>}
</div>
<div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
<div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: day.done ? T.t3 : T.text, textDecoration: day.done ? “line-through” : “none” }}>{day.title}</div>
{isToday && <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700, color: ar?.c }}>TODAY</span>}
</div>
</div>
<div style={{ paddingLeft: 32 }}>
{day.actions.map((action, ai) => (
<div key={ai} style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “flex-start”, gap: 8, marginBottom: 4 }}>
<div style={{ width: 16, height: 16, borderRadius: 4, flexShrink: 0, marginTop: 1, border: day.done ? `1.5px solid ${T.green}` : `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`, background: day.done ? `${T.green}12` : “white”, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center” }}>
{day.done && <svg width={10} height={10} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.green} strokeWidth={3} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" /></svg>}
</div>
<span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: day.done ? T.t3 : T.t2, lineHeight: 1.4, textDecoration: day.done ? “line-through” : “none” }}>{action}</span>
</div>
))}
</div>
</div>
);
})}
</div>
)}
</div>
);
})}
{Array.from({ length: prg.w - program.weeks.length }, (_, i) => {
const wNum = program.weeks.length + i + 1;
return (
<div key={`locked-${wNum}`} style={{ background: T.glass, backdropFilter: “blur(16px)”, WebkitBackdropFilter: “blur(16px)”, borderRadius: 20, padding: “14px 16px”, border: `0.5px solid ${T.glassBorder}`, opacity: 0.5, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 12 }}>
<div style={{ width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 10, background: T.fill, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center” }}>
<svg width={14} height={14} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round"><rect x="3" y="11" width="18" height="11" rx="2"/><path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0110 0v4"/></svg>
</div>
<div><div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3 }}>Week {wNum}</div><div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3 }}>Unlocks as you progress</div></div>
</div>
);
})}
</div>
)}
</div>
</div>
);
}

/* Inline assignees display + picker trigger */
function InlineAssignees({ assignees = [], onToggle, size = 22, max = 4, accentColor }) {
const [showPicker, setShowPicker] = useState(false);
const people = assignees.map(id => PEOPLE.find(p => p.id === id)).filter(Boolean);
const color = accentColor || T.brand;

return (
<>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 2 }}
onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); setShowPicker(true); }}>
{people.slice(0, max).map((p, i) => (
<div key={p.id} style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size / 2,
background: `${p.color}18`, border: `1.5px solid white`,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”,
fontSize: size * 0.38, fontWeight: 700, color: p.color,
marginLeft: i > 0 ? -size * 0.3 : 0, zIndex: max - i,
cursor: “pointer”, position: “relative” }}>
{p.avatar}
</div>
))}
{people.length > max && (
<div style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size / 2,
background: T.fill, border: `1.5px solid white`,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”,
fontSize: size * 0.32, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t3,
marginLeft: -size * 0.3, cursor: “pointer” }}>
+{people.length - max}
</div>
)}
{/* Add button when empty or as append */}
<div style={{ width: size, height: size, borderRadius: size / 2,
background: “transparent”, border: `1.5px dashed ${color}35`,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, justifyContent: “center”,
cursor: “pointer”, marginLeft: people.length > 0 ? -size * 0.3 : 0 }}>
<svg width={size * 0.4} height={size * 0.4} viewBox=“0 0 24 24” fill=“none”
stroke={color} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap=“round”>
<line x1="12" y1="5" x2="12" y2="19" /><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12" />
</svg>
</div>
</div>

```
  <AnimatePresence>
    {showPicker && (
      <PeoplePicker
        selected={assignees}
        onToggle={onToggle}
        onClose={() => setShowPicker(false)}
      />
    )}
  </AnimatePresence>
</>
```

);
}

function AreaPicker({ selected, onSelect, onClose }) {
const allAreas = Object.entries(ITEM_AREAS).map(([id, a]) => ({ id, …a }));
return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
style={{ position: “fixed”, inset: 0, zIndex: 55, background: “rgba(0,0,0,0.3)”, display: “flex”, alignItems: “flex-end”, justifyContent: “center” }}
onClick={onClose}>
<motion.div initial={{ y: 200 }} animate={{ y: 0 }} exit={{ y: 200 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, damping: 28, stiffness: 300 }}
onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
style={{
width: “100%”, maxWidth: 430, background: “rgba(255,255,255,0.96)”, backdropFilter: “blur(40px)”, WebkitBackdropFilter: “blur(40px)”,
borderRadius: “24px 24px 0 0”, padding: “20px 20px 32px”,
boxShadow: “0 -8px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)”,
}}>
<div style={{ width: 36, height: 4, borderRadius: 2, background: T.sep, margin: “0 auto 16px” }} />
<div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 14 }}>Choose area</div>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, flexWrap: “wrap”, gap: 6 }}>
{allAreas.map(a => (
<button key={a.id} onClick={() => { onSelect(a.id); onClose(); }}
style={{
padding: “8px 14px”, borderRadius: 10, cursor: “pointer”,
border: selected === a.id ? `1.5px solid ${a.c}40` : “1.5px solid transparent”,
background: selected === a.id ? `${a.c}10` : T.fill,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 6,
}}>
<span style={{ fontSize: 12 }}>{a.e}</span>
<span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: selected === a.id ? a.c : T.text }}>{a.n}</span>
</button>
))}
</div>
</motion.div>
</motion.div>
);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
GOAL DETAIL PAGE — tap-into from Plan
═══════════════════════════════════ */
function GoalDetailPage({ goalId, onBack, onOpenItem }) {
const { items, updateItem, removeItem } = useAppState();
const goal = items.find(i => i.id === goalId);
if (!goal) return <div style={{ padding: 40, textAlign: “center”, color: T.t3 }}>Goal not found</div>;

const [editingTitle, setEditingTitle]   = useState(false);
const [titleDraft, setTitleDraft]       = useState(goal.title);
const [editingWhy, setEditingWhy]       = useState(false);
const [whyDraft, setWhyDraft]           = useState(goal.why || “”);
const [editingDesc, setEditingDesc]     = useState(false);
const [descDraft, setDescDraft]         = useState(goal.description || “”);
const [showAreaPicker, setShowAreaPicker]   = useState(false);
const [showCollabPicker, setShowCollabPicker] = useState(false);
const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel]       = useState(false);

const gp = goalProgress(goal);
const linked = getGoalLinkedItems(goal);
const ai = ITEM_AREAS[goal.area];
const ac = ai?.c || “#9B59B6”;
const collaborators = goal.collaborators || [];

const toggleCollaborator = (pid) => {
const next = collaborators.includes(pid)
? collaborators.filter(x => x !== pid)
: […collaborators, pid];
updateItem(goal.id, { collaborators: next });
};

return (
<div style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: “auto”, paddingBottom: 30 }}>
<AnimatePresence>
{showAreaPicker && <AreaPicker selected={goal.area} onSelect={(a) => updateItem(goal.id, { area: a })} onClose={() => setShowAreaPicker(false)} />}
{showCollabPicker && (
<PeoplePicker
title=“Working on this goal with…”
selected={collaborators}
onToggle={toggleCollaborator}
onClose={() => setShowCollabPicker(false)} />
)}
</AnimatePresence>

```
  {confirmDel && (
    <div style={{ position: "fixed", inset: 0, zIndex: 50, background: "rgba(0,0,0,0.3)", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }} onClick={() => setConfirmDel(false)}>
      <div style={{ background: "white", borderRadius: 20, padding: "24px 20px", width: 280, textAlign: "center", boxShadow: "0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.2)" }} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 6 }}>Delete this goal?</div>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 18, lineHeight: 1.4 }}>Linked projects won't be deleted.</div>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8 }}>
          <button onClick={() => setConfirmDel(false)} style={{ flex: 1, padding: "10px 0", borderRadius: 10, border: `1.5px solid ${T.sep}`, background: "white", cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Cancel</button>
          <button onClick={() => { removeItem(goal.id); onBack(); }} style={{ flex: 1, padding: "10px 0", borderRadius: 10, border: "none", background: T.red, cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: "white" }}>Delete</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )}

  {/* Back */}
  <div style={{ padding: "12px 16px 0" }}>
    <button onClick={onBack} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 4, background: "none", border: "none", cursor: "pointer", padding: "4px 0" }}>
      <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.brand} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="15 18 9 12 15 6" /></svg>
      <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.brand }}>Plan</span>
    </button>
  </div>

  {/* Hero */}
  <div style={{ padding: "8px 16px 16px" }}>
    <div style={{ background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: T.glassBlur, WebkitBackdropFilter: T.glassBlur, borderRadius: 22, padding: 20, boxShadow: `${T.cardShadow}, ${T.cardHighlight}`, border: T.cardBorder }}>
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 16 }}>
        <div style={{ position: "relative", width: 64, height: 64, flexShrink: 0 }}>
          <ProgressRing progress={gp} size={64} sw={5} color={ac} />
          <div style={{ position: "absolute", inset: 0, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 28 }}>{goal.emoji}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
          {editingTitle ? (
            <input autoFocus value={titleDraft} onChange={(e) => setTitleDraft(e.target.value)}
              onBlur={() => { if (titleDraft.trim()) updateItem(goal.id, { title: titleDraft.trim() }); setEditingTitle(false); }}
              onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === "Enter") { if (titleDraft.trim()) updateItem(goal.id, { title: titleDraft.trim() }); setEditingTitle(false); } }}
              style={{ fontSize: 19, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, border: "none", borderBottom: `2px solid ${T.brand}`, background: "transparent", outline: "none", width: "100%", padding: "2px 0", fontFamily: "inherit", letterSpacing: -0.3 }} />
          ) : (
            <div onClick={() => { setTitleDraft(goal.title); setEditingTitle(true); }} style={{ fontSize: 19, fontWeight: 750, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.3, cursor: "pointer" }}>
              {goal.title}
              <Ic id="edit" size={11} color={T.t3} />
            </div>
          )}
          <button onClick={() => setShowAreaPicker(true)} style={{ display: "inline-flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 4, marginTop: 6, background: `${ac}08`, border: `0.5px solid ${ac}15`, borderRadius: 8, padding: "4px 10px", cursor: "pointer" }}>
            <div style={{ width: 7, height: 7, borderRadius: 4, background: ac }} />
            <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: ac, fontWeight: 600 }}>{ai?.n || goal.area}</span>
            <svg width={8} height={8} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round"><polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9" /></svg>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* ── Why field ── */}
      <div style={{ marginTop: 16, padding: "12px 14px", borderRadius: 14,
        background: `${ac}06`, border: `1px solid ${ac}12` }}>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginBottom: editingWhy ? 8 : goal.why ? 6 : 0 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, color: ac, letterSpacing: 0.2, textTransform: "uppercase" }}>
            Why this matters
          </span>
          {!editingWhy && (
            <button onClick={() => { setWhyDraft(goal.why || ""); setEditingWhy(true); }}
              style={{ fontSize: 10, color: ac, background: "none", border: "none",
                cursor: "pointer", opacity: 0.6, padding: 0, marginLeft: "auto" }}>
              {goal.why ? "✏️ Edit" : "+ Add"}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
        {editingWhy ? (
          <div>
            <textarea autoFocus value={whyDraft}
              onChange={e => setWhyDraft(e.target.value)}
              onBlur={() => {
                updateItem(goal.id, { why: whyDraft.trim() || undefined });
                setEditingWhy(false);
              }}
              onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === "Escape") { setWhyDraft(goal.why || ""); setEditingWhy(false); } }}
              placeholder="In one sentence — why do you want this?"
              rows={2}
              style={{ width: "100%", fontSize: 14, fontStyle: "italic", color: T.text,
                background: "white", border: `1.5px solid ${ac}30`, borderRadius: 10,
                padding: "8px 10px", outline: "none", fontFamily: "inherit",
                resize: "none", lineHeight: 1.5, boxSizing: "border-box" }} />
            <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, marginTop: 3 }}>Esc or click away to save</div>
          </div>
        ) : goal.why ? (
          <div onClick={() => { setWhyDraft(goal.why); setEditingWhy(true); }}
            style={{ fontSize: 14, fontStyle: "italic", color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.5,
              cursor: "pointer" }}>
            "{goal.why}"
          </div>
        ) : (
          <button onClick={() => { setWhyDraft(""); setEditingWhy(true); }}
            style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3, fontStyle: "italic", background: "none",
              border: "none", cursor: "pointer", padding: 0 }}>
            Tap to add your why…
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* ── Description ── */}
      <div style={{ marginTop: 10, paddingTop: 10, borderTop: `1px solid ${T.sep}` }}>
        {editingDesc ? (
          <div>
            <textarea autoFocus value={descDraft}
              onChange={e => setDescDraft(e.target.value)}
              onBlur={() => {
                updateItem(goal.id, { description: descDraft.trim() || undefined });
                setEditingDesc(false);
              }}
              onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === "Escape") { setDescDraft(goal.description || ""); setEditingDesc(false); } }}
              placeholder="Add details — target, constraints, what success looks like…"
              rows={3}
              style={{ width: "100%", fontSize: 13, color: T.text, background: `${ac}04`,
                border: `1.5px solid ${ac}20`, borderRadius: 10, padding: "8px 10px",
                outline: "none", fontFamily: "inherit", resize: "none",
                lineHeight: 1.5, boxSizing: "border-box" }} />
            <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, marginTop: 3 }}>Esc or click away to save</div>
          </div>
        ) : goal.description ? (
          <div onClick={() => { setDescDraft(goal.description); setEditingDesc(true); }}
            style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.55, cursor: "pointer" }}>
            {goal.description}
            <span style={{ opacity: 0.3, marginLeft: 5, fontSize: 11 }}>✏️</span>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <button onClick={() => { setDescDraft(""); setEditingDesc(true); }}
            style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, background: "none",
              border: "none", cursor: "pointer", padding: "2px 0" }}>
            <svg width={13} height={13} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round">
              <path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v16a2 2 0 002 2h12a2 2 0 002-2V8z"/>
              <polyline points="14 2 14 8 20 8"/><line x1="16" y1="13" x2="8" y2="13"/>
            </svg>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3 }}>Add description…</span>
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Stats row */}
      <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginTop: 14 }}>
        <div style={{ flex: 1, padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: 12, background: `${ac}06`, textAlign: "center" }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 800, color: ac }}>{Math.round(gp * 100)}%</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>Progress</div>
        </div>
        <div style={{ flex: 1, padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: 12, background: T.fill, textAlign: "center" }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 800, color: T.text }}>{linked.length}</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3, marginTop: 1 }}>Linked</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Collaborators */}
      <div style={{ marginTop: 14, paddingTop: 14, borderTop: `1px solid ${T.sep}` }}>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between", marginBottom: 10 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, color: T.t3, textTransform: "uppercase", letterSpacing: 0.3 }}>
            Working on this with
          </div>
          <button onClick={() => setShowCollabPicker(true)}
            style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 650, color: ac, background: `${ac}08`,
              border: "none", borderRadius: 7, padding: "4px 10px", cursor: "pointer" }}>
            + Edit
          </button>
        </div>
        {collaborators.length > 0 ? (
          <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
            {collaborators.map(pid => {
              const p = PEOPLE.find(pp => pp.id === pid);
              if (!p) return null;
              return (
                <div key={pid} style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 7,
                  padding: "6px 12px 6px 6px", borderRadius: 20,
                  background: `${p.color}08`, border: `1.5px solid ${p.color}20` }}>
                  <div style={{ width: 26, height: 26, borderRadius: 13,
                    background: `${p.color}18`, border: `1.5px solid ${p.color}30`,
                    display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center",
                    fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, color: p.color }}>{p.avatar}</div>
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text }}>{p.name}</span>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        ) : (
          <button onClick={() => setShowCollabPicker(true)}
            style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 8, padding: "10px 14px",
              width: "100%", borderRadius: 12, border: `1.5px dashed ${ac}25`,
              background: "transparent", cursor: "pointer" }}>
            <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 14, background: `${ac}08`,
              border: `1.5px dashed ${ac}30`, display: "flex", alignItems: "center",
              justifyContent: "center" }}>
              <svg width={12} height={12} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={ac} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round">
                <line x1="12" y1="5" x2="12" y2="19" /><line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12" />
              </svg>
            </div>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3, fontWeight: 500 }}>
              Add friends to work on this goal together
            </span>
          </button>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Linked items */}
  <div style={{ padding: "0 16px" }}>
    <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 10 }}>Linked Projects & Journeys</div>
    {linked.length === 0 && (
      <div style={{ padding: "24px 16px", borderRadius: 16, border: `1.5px dashed ${ac}20`, background: `${ac}03`, textAlign: "center" }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3, marginTop: 4 }}>No items linked yet</div>
      </div>
    )}
    <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", gap: 6 }}>
      {linked.map(li => {
        const kc = KIND_CONFIG[li.kind] || {};
        const liColor = ITEM_AREAS[li.area]?.c || kc.color || T.t3;
        const liPct = Math.round((li.progress || 0) * 100);
        const hasSteps = li.steps?.length > 0;
        return (
          <motion.button key={li.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }}
            onClick={() => onOpenItem(li)}
            style={{
              width: "100%", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12,
              padding: "14px", borderRadius: 16, border: T.cardBorder, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "left",
              background: T.cardGlass, backdropFilter: "blur(16px)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "blur(16px)",
              boxShadow: "0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.03)",
            }}>
            <div style={{ width: 40, height: 40, borderRadius: 12, background: `linear-gradient(135deg, ${liColor}0C, ${liColor}18)`, border: `0.5px solid ${liColor}20`, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
              <SmartIcon icon={kc.icon || "folder"} size={18} color={liColor} />
            </div>
            <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>{li.title}</div>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, marginTop: 3 }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 600, color: kc.color, background: `${kc.color}0D`, padding: "1px 6px", borderRadius: 4 }}>{kc.label}</span>
                {hasSteps && <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3 }}>{li.steps.filter(s => s.done).length}/{li.steps.length} tasks</span>}
                {li.kind === "journey" && <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: T.t3 }}>Week {li.committed?.week || 0}/{li.prog?.w || 0}</span>}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ position: "relative", width: 36, height: 36, flexShrink: 0 }}>
              <ProgressRing progress={li.progress || 0} size={36} sw={3} color={liColor} />
              <div style={{ position: "absolute", inset: 0, display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center" }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 800, color: liColor }}>{liPct}%</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <svg width={10} height={10} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round" style={{ opacity: 0.3 }}><polyline points="9 18 15 12 9 6" /></svg>
          </motion.button>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  </div>

  {/* Delete */}
  <div style={{ padding: "20px 16px 0" }}>
    <button onClick={() => setConfirmDel(true)} style={{ width: "100%", padding: "12px 14px", borderRadius: 12, border: `1.5px solid ${T.red}20`, background: "transparent", cursor: "pointer", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", gap: 6 }}>
      <SmartIcon icon="trash" size={14} color={T.red} /><span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.red }}>Delete Goal</span>
    </button>
  </div>
</div>
```

);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
PROJECT EDIT PAGE — full edit: tasks, people, dates, delete
═══════════════════════════════════ */
function ProjectEditPage({ itemId, onBack, backLabel }) {
const { items, updateItem, removeItem, toggleStep, toggleSubtask,
addStep, removeStep, updateStep, addSubtask, removeSubtask,
pauseItem, resumeItem, completeItem } = useAppState();

const item = items.find(i => i.id === itemId);
if (!item) return <div style={{ padding: 40, textAlign: “center”, color: T.t3 }}>Item not found</div>;

const ai   = ITEM_AREAS[item.area];
const ac   = ai?.c || T.brand;
const steps = item.steps || [];
const pct   = Math.round(projectProgress(item) * 100);
const kind  = itemKind(item);

// ── Page state ──
const [editingTitle, setEditingTitle]       = useState(false);
const [titleDraft, setTitleDraft]           = useState(item.title);
const [editingDesc, setEditingDesc]         = useState(false);
const [descDraft, setDescDraft]             = useState(item.description || “”);
const [expandedTask, setExpandedTask]       = useState(null);
const [newTaskText, setNewTaskText]         = useState(””);
const [addingSubFor, setAddingSubFor]       = useState(null);
const [newSubText, setNewSubText]           = useState(””);
const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel]           = useState(null);
const [showAreaPicker, setShowAreaPicker]   = useState(false);
const [showCollabPicker, setShowCollabPicker] = useState(false);
const [editingStepDesc, setEditingStepDesc] = useState(null); // stepId
const [stepDescDraft, setStepDescDraft]     = useState(””);
const [showDepPicker, setShowDepPicker]     = useState(null); // stepId — for choosing blockedBy
const taskInputRef = useRef(null);
const subInputRef  = useRef(null);
// AI assist
const [aiTasksLoading, setAiTasksLoading] = useState(false);
const [aiSubLoading, setAiSubLoading]     = useState(null); // stepId
const [aiTaskBanner, setAiTaskBanner]     = useState(null); // “success” | “error”

const collaborators = item.collaborators || [];
const doneCount  = steps.filter(s => s.done).length;
const totalCount = steps.length;
const blockedCount = steps.filter(s => s.status === “blocked”).length;

// ── Helpers ──
const toggleCollaborator = (pid) => {
const next = collaborators.includes(pid) ? collaborators.filter(x => x !== pid) : […collaborators, pid];
updateItem(item.id, { collaborators: next });
};
const toggleStepAssignee = (stepId, pid) => {
const step = steps.find(s => s.id === stepId); if (!step) return;
const cur = step.assignees || [];
updateStep(item.id, stepId, { assignees: cur.includes(pid) ? cur.filter(x => x !== pid) : […cur, pid] });
};
const toggleSubAssignee = (stepId, subtaskId, pid) => {
const step = steps.find(s => s.id === stepId); if (!step) return;
updateStep(item.id, stepId, { subtasks: (step.subtasks || []).map(st => {
if (st.id !== subtaskId) return st;
const cur = st.assignees || [];
return { …st, assignees: cur.includes(pid) ? cur.filter(x => x !== pid) : […cur, pid] };
})});
};
const toggleDep = (stepId, depId) => {
const step = steps.find(s => s.id === stepId); if (!step) return;
const cur = step.blockedBy || [];
updateStep(item.id, stepId, { blockedBy: cur.includes(depId) ? cur.filter(x => x !== depId) : […cur, depId] });
};
const cycleStatus = (step) => {
const order = [“todo”,“doing”,“blocked”,“done”];
const next = order[(order.indexOf(step.status || “todo”) + 1) % order.length];
updateStep(item.id, step.id, { status: next, done: next === “done” });
};
const cyclePriority = (step) => {
const order = [“normal”,“high”,“urgent”,“low”];
const next = order[(order.indexOf(step.priority || “normal”) + 1) % order.length];
updateStep(item.id, step.id, { priority: next });
};
const cycleEffort = (step) => {
const order = [“quick”,“medium”,“deep”];
const next = order[(order.indexOf(step.effort || “quick”) + 1) % order.length];
updateStep(item.id, step.id, { effort: next });
};
const doAddTask = () => {
if (!newTaskText.trim()) return;
addStep(item.id, { id: `s-${Date.now()}`, title: newTaskText.trim(), done: false, status: “todo”, priority: “normal”, effort: “medium”, assignees: [], blockedBy: [] });
setNewTaskText(””); setTimeout(() => taskInputRef.current?.focus(), 30);
};
const doAddSubtask = (stepId) => {
if (!newSubText.trim()) return;
addSubtask(item.id, stepId, { id: `st-${Date.now()}`, title: newSubText.trim(), done: false, assignees: [] });
setNewSubText(””); setTimeout(() => subInputRef.current?.focus(), 30);
};

// ── AI task generation ──
async function handleAiTasks() {
if (aiTasksLoading) return;
setAiTasksLoading(true);
setAiTaskBanner(null);
try {
const existing = steps.map(s => s.title).join(”, “);
const prompt = existing
? “Project: "” + item.title + “"\nExisting tasks: “ + existing + “\nGenerate 3-5 MORE concrete tasks that are missing. Reply JSON only, no markdown:\n{"tasks":["task 1","task 2"…]}”
: “Project: "” + item.title + “"\nDescription: "” + (item.description || “”) + “"\nGenerate 5-7 concrete, actionable tasks to complete this project. Reply JSON only, no markdown:\n{"tasks":["task 1","task 2"…]}”;
const raw = await aiAssist(prompt);
const clean = raw.replace(/`json|`/g, “”).trim();
const parsed = JSON.parse(clean);
if (parsed.tasks?.length) {
parsed.tasks.forEach(t => {
const uid = “s-” + Date.now() + “-” + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6);
addStep(item.id, { id: uid, title: t, done: false, status: “todo”, priority: “normal”, effort: “medium”, assignees: [], blockedBy: [] });
});
setAiTaskBanner(“success”);
setTimeout(() => setAiTaskBanner(null), 3000);
}
} catch(e) { setAiTaskBanner(“error”); setTimeout(() => setAiTaskBanner(null), 3000); }
setAiTasksLoading(false);
}

async function handleAiSubtasks(stepId) {
if (aiSubLoading) return;
setAiSubLoading(stepId);
try {
const step = steps.find(s => s.id === stepId);
const prompt = “Break down this task into 3-4 subtasks:\n"” + (step ? step.title : “”) + “"\nProject context: "” + item.title + “"\nReply JSON only, no markdown:\n{"subtasks":["subtask 1","subtask 2"…]}”;
const raw = await aiAssist(prompt);
const clean = raw.replace(/`json|`/g, “”).trim();
const parsed = JSON.parse(clean);
if (parsed.subtasks?.length) {
parsed.subtasks.forEach(t => {
const uid = “st-” + Date.now() + “-” + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6);
addSubtask(item.id, stepId, { id: uid, title: t, done: false, assignees: [] });
});
}
} catch(e) {}
setAiSubLoading(null);
}

// ── Dependency picker sheet ──
const DepPicker = ({ stepId, onClose }) => {
const step = steps.find(s => s.id === stepId);
const blockedBy = step?.blockedBy || [];
const available = steps.filter(s => s.id !== stepId);
return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
style={{ position: “fixed”, inset: 0, zIndex: 60, background: “rgba(0,0,0,0.3)”,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “flex-end”, justifyContent: “center” }}
onClick={onClose}>
<motion.div initial={{ y: 250 }} animate={{ y: 0 }} exit={{ y: 250 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, damping: 28, stiffness: 300 }}
onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
style={{ width: “100%”, maxWidth: 430, background: “rgba(255,255,255,0.97)”,
backdropFilter: “blur(40px)”, WebkitBackdropFilter: “blur(40px)”,
borderRadius: “24px 24px 0 0”, padding: “16px 20px 36px”,
boxShadow: “0 -8px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.12)” }}>
<div style={{ width: 36, height: 4, borderRadius: 2, background: T.sep, margin: “0 auto 14px” }} />
<div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, marginBottom: 4 }}>Blocked by…</div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 14 }}>
“{step?.title}” can’t start until these are done
</div>
{available.length === 0 ? (
<div style={{ padding: “20px 0”, textAlign: “center”, color: T.t3, fontSize: 13 }}>
No other tasks to depend on
</div>
) : (
<div style={{ display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, gap: 4 }}>
{available.map(s => {
const isSel = blockedBy.includes(s.id);
const ss = STEP_STATUS[s.status || “todo”];
return (
<motion.button key={s.id} whileTap={{ scale: 0.98 }}
onClick={() => toggleDep(stepId, s.id)}
style={{ display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 12, padding: “10px 14px”,
borderRadius: 12, border: isSel ? `1.5px solid ${ac}30` : “1.5px solid transparent”,

})}
</div>

<button onClick={onClose}

</motion.div>
);
};

{showDepPicker && <DepPicker stepId={showDepPicker} onClose={() => setShowDepPicker(null)} />}

                background: "white", cursor: "pointer", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 650, color: T.text }}>Cancel</button>

              else if (typeof confirmDel === "string") removeStep(item.id, confirmDel);

                    {/* ── Attribute chips row ── */}
                    <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, marginBottom: 12, paddingLeft: 34, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>

                      </button>
                    </div>

                    <div style={{ marginLeft: 34, marginBottom: 10 }}>
                      {editingStepDesc === step.id ? (

                          <textarea autoFocus value={stepDescDraft}
                            onChange={e => setStepDescDraft(e.target.value)}
                            onBlur={() => { updateStep(item.id, step.id, { description: stepDescDraft.trim() || undefined }); setEditingStepDesc(null); }}

                            rows={2}
                            style={{ width: "100%", fontSize: 12, color: T.text, background: "white",
                              border: `1.5px solid ${ac}20`, borderRadius: 8, padding: "7px 9px",
                              outline: "none", fontFamily: "inherit", resize: "none",

                        <div onClick={() => { setStepDescDraft(step.description); setEditingStepDesc(step.id); }}
                          style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.t2, lineHeight: 1.5, cursor: "pointer",
