/* ═══════════════════════════════════
ALL ITEMS — Full inventory across all statuses (legacy, now superseded by PlanScreen)
═══════════════════════════════════ */
function AllItemsScreen() {
const [filter, setFilter] = useState(“all”); // “all” | “active” | “paused” | “goals”
const [collapseAreas, setCollapseAreas] = useState({});

// Build full item list including journeys
const allItems = [];

// Add enrolled journeys
COMMITTED.filter(c => c.status === “active”).forEach(c => {
const prog = PRG.find(p => p.id === c.id);
if (!prog) return;
allItems.push({
id: `journey-${prog.id}`, title: prog.t, emoji: ICONS[prog.id] || “📘”,
area: prog.a, source: “journey”, status: “active”,
progress: c.week / (prog.w || 6),
subtitle: `Week ${c.week} of ${prog.w || 6}`,
});
});

// Add all user items
ITEMS.forEach(item => {
const doneSteps = item.steps?.filter(s => s.done).length || 0;
const totalSteps = item.steps?.length || 0;
const pausedDaysAgo = item.pausedAt ? Math.floor((Date.now() - new Date(item.pausedAt).getTime()) / 86400000) : null;
allItems.push({
…item,
progress: totalSteps > 0 ? doneSteps / totalSteps : 0,
subtitle: item.status === “paused”
? (pausedDaysAgo !== null ? `Paused ${pausedDaysAgo === 0 ? "today" : pausedDaysAgo === 1 ? "yesterday" : `${pausedDaysAgo}d ago`}` : “On hold”)
: item.status === “someday”
? “No plan yet”
: item.recurrence ? formatRecurrence(item.recurrence)
: totalSteps > 0 ? `${doneSteps}/${totalSteps} steps` : “”,
});
});

// Apply filter
const filtered = filter === “all” ? allItems
: filter === “active” ? allItems.filter(i => i.status === “active”)
: filter === “paused” ? allItems.filter(i => i.status === “paused”)
: allItems.filter(i => i.status === “someday”);

// Group by area
const areaGroups = {};
filtered.forEach(item => {
const a = item.area || “other”;
if (!areaGroups[a]) areaGroups[a] = [];
areaGroups[a].push(item);
});

// Sort items within area: active first, then paused, then goals
const statusOrder = { active: 0, paused: 1, someday: 2 };
Object.values(areaGroups).forEach(items => {
items.sort((a, b) => (statusOrder[a.status] || 0) - (statusOrder[b.status] || 0));
});

const counts = {
all: allItems.length,
active: allItems.filter(i => i.status === “active”).length,
paused: allItems.filter(i => i.status === “paused”).length,
goals: allItems.filter(i => i.status === “someday”).length,
};

const FILTERS = [
{ id: “all”, label: “All”, count: counts.all },
{ id: “active”, label: “Active”, count: counts.active },
{ id: “paused”, label: “Paused”, count: counts.paused },
{ id: “goals”, label: “Goals”, count: counts.goals },
];

const toggleArea = (a) => setCollapseAreas(prev => ({ …prev, [a]: !prev[a] }));

return (
<div style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: “auto”, WebkitOverflowScrolling: “touch” }}>
<div style={{ padding: “4px 20px 100px” }}>

```
    {/* Filter chips */}
    <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, marginBottom: 14, overflowX: "auto", paddingBottom: 2 }}>
      {FILTERS.map(f => (
        <button key={f.id} onClick={() => setFilter(f.id)}
          style={{
            padding: "7px 14px", borderRadius: 20, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
            background: filter === f.id ? T.brand : "white",
            color: filter === f.id ? "white" : T.t2,
            fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600, whiteSpace: "nowrap",
            boxShadow: filter === f.id ? "0 2px 8px rgba(108,92,231,0.2)" : "0 0.5px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.06)",
            display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 5,
            transition: "all 0.2s ease",
          }}>
          {f.label}
          <span style={{
            fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700,
            background: filter === f.id ? "rgba(255,255,255,0.25)" : T.fill,
            padding: "1px 6px", borderRadius: 8,
            color: filter === f.id ? "white" : T.t3,
          }}>{f.count}</span>
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>

    {/* Area groups */}
    {Object.entries(areaGroups).map(([areaId, items]) => {
      const ia = ITEM_AREAS[areaId];
      const la = GA(areaId);
      const areaName = ia?.n || la?.n || areaId;
      const areaColor = ia?.c || la?.c || T.brand;
      const areaEmoji = ia?.e || "";
      const isCollapsed = collapseAreas[areaId];

      return (
        <div key={areaId} style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>
          {/* Area header */}
          <button onClick={() => toggleArea(areaId)}
            style={{
              width: "100%", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10,
              padding: "11px 14px",
              background: T.glass, border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
              borderRadius: isCollapsed ? 14 : "14px 14px 0 0",
              borderLeft: `3px solid ${areaColor}`,
              textAlign: "left",
            }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 15 }}>{areaEmoji}</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, flex: 1 }}>{areaName}</span>
            <span style={{
              fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600, color: areaColor,
              background: `${areaColor}0D`, padding: "2px 8px", borderRadius: 10,
            }}>{items.length}</span>
            <svg width={13} height={13} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round"
              style={{ transform: isCollapsed ? "rotate(-90deg)" : "rotate(0deg)", transition: "transform 0.2s ease" }}>
              <polyline points="6 9 12 15 18 9" />
            </svg>
          </button>

          {!isCollapsed && (
            <div style={{
              background: T.glass, backdropFilter: "blur(16px)", WebkitBackdropFilter: "blur(16px)", borderRadius: "0 0 16px 16px",
              borderLeft: `3px solid ${areaColor}`,
              overflow: "hidden",
            }}>
              {items.map((item, idx) => {
                const kind = itemKind(item);
                const kindConf = KIND_CONFIG[kind] || KIND_CONFIG.action;
                const isPaused = item.status === "paused";
                const isGoal = item.status === "someday";
                const pct = Math.round((item.progress || 0) * 100);

                return (
                  <div key={item.id} style={{
                    display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 12, padding: "12px 14px",
                    borderTop: idx === 0 ? "none" : `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`,
                    cursor: "pointer",
                    opacity: isPaused ? 0.55 : 1,
                  }}>
                    {/* Emoji */}
                    <div style={{
                      width: 38, height: 38, borderRadius: 10,
                      background: isGoal ? `${T.brand}06` : `${areaColor}08`,
                      display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", flexShrink: 0,
                    }}>
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 18 }}>{item.emoji}</span>
                    </div>

                    {/* Content */}
                    <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                      <div style={{
                        fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text,
                        whiteSpace: "nowrap", overflow: "hidden", textOverflow: "ellipsis",
                      }}>{item.title}</div>
                      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 5, marginTop: 3, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
                        {/* Status badge */}
                        {isPaused && (
                          <span style={{
                            fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: 0.3,
                            color: T.orange, background: `${T.orange}0D`,
                            padding: "2px 6px", borderRadius: 4, textTransform: "uppercase",
                          }}>Paused</span>
                        )}
                        {isGoal && (
                          <span style={{
                            fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: 0.3,
                            color: T.brand, background: `${T.brand}0D`,
                            padding: "2px 6px", borderRadius: 4, textTransform: "uppercase",
                          }}>Goal</span>
                        )}
                        {/* Kind badge */}
                        <span style={{
                          fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 700, letterSpacing: 0.3,
                          color: kindConf.color, background: `${kindConf.color}0D`,
                          padding: "2px 6px", borderRadius: 4, textTransform: "uppercase",
                        }}>{kindConf.label}</span>
                        {/* Subtitle */}
                        {item.subtitle && (
                          <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.t3, fontWeight: 500 }}>{item.subtitle}</span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* Right side action/indicator */}
                    {isPaused && (
                      <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.brand} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"
                        style={{ flexShrink: 0, opacity: 0.7 }}>
                        <polygon points="5 3 19 12 5 21 5 3" />
                      </svg>
                    )}
                    {isGoal && (
                      <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.brand} strokeWidth={1.8} strokeLinecap="round"
                        style={{ flexShrink: 0, opacity: 0.5 }}>
                        <polyline points="9 18 15 12 9 6" />
                      </svg>
                    )}
                    {!isPaused && !isGoal && item.progress > 0 && item.progress < 1 && (
                      <div style={{ width: 34, height: 34, position: "relative", flexShrink: 0 }}>
                        <svg width={34} height={34} viewBox="0 0 36 36">
                          <circle cx={18} cy={18} r={14} fill="none" stroke={`${areaColor}15`} strokeWidth={3} />
                          <circle cx={18} cy={18} r={14} fill="none" stroke={areaColor} strokeWidth={3}
                            strokeDasharray={`${item.progress * 87.96} 87.96`}
                            strokeLinecap="round" transform="rotate(-90 18 18)" />
                        </svg>
                        <span style={{ position: "absolute", inset: 0, display: "flex", alignItems: "center",
                          justifyContent: "center", fontSize: 8, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>
                          {pct}%
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    {!isPaused && !isGoal && (!item.progress || item.progress === 0) && kind === "habit" && (
                      <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.orange} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap="round"
                        style={{ flexShrink: 0, opacity: 0.6 }}>
                        <polyline points="23 4 23 10 17 10" /><path d="M20.49 15a9 9 0 11-2.12-9.36L23 10" />
                      </svg>
                    )}
                    {!isPaused && !isGoal && (!item.progress || item.progress === 0) && kind !== "habit" && (
                      <svg width={16} height={16} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.t3} strokeWidth={1.8} strokeLinecap="round"
                        style={{ flexShrink: 0, opacity: 0.4 }}>
                        <polyline points="9 18 15 12 9 6" />
                      </svg>
                    )}
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      );
    })}

    {/* Empty state */}
    {Object.keys(areaGroups).length === 0 && (
      <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "40px 20px" }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 36, marginBottom: 12, display: "flex", justifyContent: "center" }}>
          <Ic id={filter === "paused" ? "pause" : filter === "goals" ? "target" : "folder"} size={36} color={T.t3} />
        </div>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600, color: T.text, marginBottom: 4 }}>
          {filter === "paused" ? "Nothing paused" : filter === "goals" ? "No goals yet" : "No items yet"}
        </div>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: T.t3 }}>
          {filter === "goals" ? "Add a goal from the + button or chat with your coach" : "Tap + to add something"}
        </div>
      </div>
    )}
  </div>
</div>
```

);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
ADD SOMETHING — Full screen coach chat
═══════════════════════════════════ */
function AddSomethingChat({ onClose }) {
const [messages, setMessages] = useState([
{ role: “coach”, text: `Hey ${USER.name}! What would you like to work on? A goal, a quick task, something you've been putting off, or even just a goal for someday.` }
]);
const [input, setInput] = useState(””);
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
const scrollRef = useRef(null);

useEffect(() => {
if (scrollRef.current) scrollRef.current.scrollTop = scrollRef.current.scrollHeight;
}, [messages]);

async function send() {
if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
const userMsg = input.trim();
setInput(””);
setMessages(prev => […prev, { role: “user”, text: userMsg }]);
setLoading(true);

```
try {
  const history = [...messages, { role: "user", text: userMsg }];
  const chatMessages = history.map(m => ({
    role: m.role === "coach" ? "assistant" : "user",
    content: m.text
  }));
  
  const response = await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", {
    method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: "claude-sonnet-4-20250514", max_tokens: 1000,
      system: `You are Stevo, an AI life coach helping ${USER.name} add something new to their life. Your job is to understand what they want, help break it down if needed, and classify it. Be warm, concise (2-3 sentences max per response), and action-oriented. Never use em dashes. Do not use markdown formatting.
```

When you understand what they want, respond with a summary using this exact format at the end of your message:

[ITEM]
Title: (clear, concise title)
Emoji: (single relevant emoji)  
Area: (one of: health, home, career, finance, learning, relationships, fun)
Status: (active or someday)
Recurring: (daily, weekdays, weekly, or none)
Steps: (comma-separated list, or “none” for simple habits/actions)
[/ITEM]

Rules for classification:

- If it has steps (multi-step thing to achieve) -> include Steps, Recurring=none -> it becomes a Project
- If it repeats (daily habit, weekly practice) -> Recurring=daily/weekly/etc, Steps=none -> it becomes a Habit
- If neither -> Steps=none, Recurring=none -> it becomes a one-off Action
- If aspirational with no commitment yet -> Status=someday -> it becomes a Goal
- A Journey is NEVER created here. Journeys are expert-designed programs from the Discover tab.

Ask clarifying questions first if the request is vague. For simple things, go straight to the item summary. For bigger things, help break them into 3-7 steps.`,
messages: chatMessages,
}),
});
const data = await response.json();
let text = data.content?.map(c => c.text || “”).join(””) || “I’m having trouble connecting. Try again?”;
text = text.replace(/\u2014/g, “. “).replace(/–/g, “. “);

```
  const itemMatch = text.match(/\[ITEM\]([\s\S]*?)\[\/ITEM\]/);
  let displayText = text.replace(/\[ITEM\][\s\S]*?\[\/ITEM\]/, "").trim();
  
  if (itemMatch) {
    const itemBlock = itemMatch[1];
    const title = itemBlock.match(/Title:\s*(.+)/)?.[1]?.trim() || "New Item";
    const emoji = itemBlock.match(/Emoji:\s*(.+)/)?.[1]?.trim() || "📌";
    const area = itemBlock.match(/Area:\s*(.+)/)?.[1]?.trim() || "learning";
    const status = itemBlock.match(/Status:\s*(.+)/)?.[1]?.trim() || "active";
    const recurring = itemBlock.match(/Recurring:\s*(.+)/)?.[1]?.trim() || "none";
    const stepsRaw = itemBlock.match(/Steps:\s*(.+)/)?.[1]?.trim() || "none";
    const steps = stepsRaw === "none" ? [] : stepsRaw.split(",").map(s => s.trim());
    // Derive kind from properties (never stored)
    const kind = status === "someday" ? "goal" 
      : recurring !== "none" ? "habit"
      : steps.length > 0 ? "project" 
      : "action";
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, 
      ...(displayText ? [{ role: "coach", text: displayText }] : []),
      { role: "item", title, emoji, area, status, recurring, kind, steps }
    ]);
  } else {
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "coach", text: displayText || text }]);
  }
} catch (e) {
  setMessages(prev => [...prev, { role: "coach", text: "Having trouble connecting. Could you try again?" }]);
}
setLoading(false);
```

}

return (
<motion.div initial={{ y: “100%” }} animate={{ y: 0 }} exit={{ y: “100%” }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, damping: 28, stiffness: 300 }}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, zIndex: 50, background: T.meshBg,
display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column” }}>

```
        return (

              </div>
              <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text, letterSpacing: -0.2 }}>{m.title}</div>
                <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 5, marginTop: 4, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>

                    fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 600, color: ia.c, background: `${ia.c}0D`,

                  }}>{m.status === "someday" ? "Someday" : m.recurring && m.recurring !== "none" ? m.recurring : "Active"}</span>

                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            {m.steps.length > 0 && (
              <div style={{ marginBottom: 14, padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: 12, background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.15)" }}>

                style={{

                  background: T.grad, color: "white", fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700,
```

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
FAB ACTION SHEET + QUICK ADD

/* ═══════════════════════════════════
PROJECT ADD SHEET
Flow: title → NLP suggests area (shown as chip) →
confirm or change → optional “also improves” →
optional steps → save
═══════════════════════════════════ */
/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
AI ASSIST — calls Claude API to enrich user input
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════*/
async function aiAssist(prompt) {
const res = await fetch(“https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages”, {
method: “POST”,
headers: { “Content-Type”: “application/json” },
body: JSON.stringify({
model: “claude-sonnet-4-20250514”,
max_tokens: 600,
messages: [{ role: “user”, content: prompt }],
}),
});
const data = await res.json();
const text = (data.content || []).map(b => b.text || “”).join(””);
return text.trim();
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
UNIFIED ADD SHEET
Step 1: text input + type selection + AI promo chips
Step 2: type-specific form (goal / habit / action / project / journey)
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════*/

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SMART ADD SHEET — unified entry point
Type your intent, AI enriches it live (debounced),
one tap to save. Project opens its own sheet.
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════*/
function FabActionSheet({ onProject, onJourney, onClose }) {
const { addItem } = useAppState();
const [text, setText]                 = useState(””);
const [selectedType, setSelectedType] = useState(null);
const [aiHint, setAiHint]             = useState(null);
const [aiLoading, setAiLoading]       = useState(false);
const [area, setArea]                 = useState(null);
const [showAreaPicker, setShowAreaPicker] = useState(false);
const [tod, setTod]                   = useState(null);
const [saved, setSaved]               = useState(false);
const inputRef    = useRef(null);
const debounceRef = useRef(null);

useEffect(() => { setTimeout(() => inputRef.current?.focus(), 200); }, []);

// NLP type inference
const inferredType = useMemo(() => {
const t = text.toLowerCase();
if (!t.trim()) return null;
if (/(every|daily|each|morning|evening|weekly|routine|habit|practice|meditat|exercise|workout|journal|stretch)/i.test(t)) return “habit”;
if (/(want to|someday|dream|hope|goal|achieve|by \d{4}|one day|life|financial)/i.test(t)) return “goal”;
if (/(project|plan|build|launch|renovate|prepare|organis|organize|campaign|website)/i.test(t)) return “project”;
return “action”;
}, [text]);

const activeType = selectedType || inferredType;

// NLP area suggestion
useEffect(() => {
if (activeType === “goal”) return;
const s = suggestArea(text);
if (s && !area) setArea(s);
}, [text]);

// Debounced AI hint — fires 900ms after typing stops
useEffect(() => {
clearTimeout(debounceRef.current);
if (!text.trim() || text.trim().length < 5) { setAiHint(null); return; }
debounceRef.current = setTimeout(async () => {
setAiLoading(true);
try {
const type = selectedType || inferredType || “action”;
const prompts = {
action:  “Task: "” + text + “"\nReply JSON only: {"why":"one short sentence why this matters","effort":"quick|medium|deep"}”,
habit:   “Habit: "” + text + “"\nReply JSON only: {"why":"one short sentence life impact","tip":"one practical tip to make it stick"}”,
goal:    “Goal: "” + text + “"\nReply JSON only: {"why":"one emotional sentence why this goal matters","firstStep":"single best first action"}”,
project: “Project: "” + text + “"\nReply JSON only: {"why":"one sentence why this matters","firstStep":"the very first task to start"}”,
};
const raw   = await aiAssist(prompts[type] || prompts.action);
const clean = raw.replace(/`json|`/g, “”).trim();
setAiHint(JSON.parse(clean));
} catch(e) {}
setAiLoading(false);
}, 900);
return () => clearTimeout(debounceRef.current);
}, [text, selectedType]);

const TYPE_OPTIONS = [
{ id: “action”,  label: “Action”,  emoji: “✓”,  color: T.green   },
{ id: “habit”,   label: “Habit”,   emoji: “🔄”, color: T.orange  },
{ id: “goal”,    label: “Goal”,    emoji: “🎯”, color: “#9B59B6” },
{ id: “project”, label: “Project”, emoji: “📁”, color: T.brand   },
{ id: “journey”, label: “Journey”, emoji: “🧭”, color: “#007AFF” },
];

const PROMOS = [
{ text: “Meditate every morning”,  type: “habit”   },
{ text: “Run a 5K by June”,        type: “goal”    },
{ text: “Redesign the website”,    type: “project” },
{ text: “Call Mum this week”,      type: “action”  },
{ text: “Read 12 books this year”, type: “goal”    },
{ text: “Build a sleep routine”,   type: “habit”   },
];

const typeConf = activeType ? TYPE_OPTIONS.find(t => t.id === activeType) : null;
const areaConf = area ? ITEM_AREAS[area] : null;
const canSave  = text.trim().length > 0 && (activeType !== “goal” || area);

function handleSave() {
if (!canSave) return;
const type = activeType || “action”;
if (type === “project”) { onProject(text); return; }
if (type === “journey”) { onJourney(); return; }
// Build item and persist to state
const isHabit = type === “habit”;
const isGoal  = type === “goal”;
addItem({
id:          “item-” + Date.now(),
title:       text.trim(),
emoji:       isGoal ? “🎯” : isHabit ? “🔄” : “✓”,
area:        area || suggestArea(text) || “home”,
status:      isGoal ? “someday” : “active”,
source:      “self”,
timeOfDay:   tod || “anytime”,
createdAt:   new Date().toISOString(),
…(isHabit ? { recurrence: { type: “daily” }, habitTimeOfDay: tod || “morning” } : {}),
});
setSaved(true);
setTimeout(() => { setSaved(false); onClose(); }, 950);
}

function handleTypeSelect(id) {
if (id === “journey”)                { onJourney(); return; }
if (id === “project” && text.trim()) { onProject(text); return; }
setSelectedType(prev => prev === id ? null : id);
setAiHint(null);
}

const todOptions = [
{ id: “morning”,   icon: “sun”,      label: “AM”  },
{ id: “afternoon”, icon: “sunCloud”, label: “PM”  },
{ id: “evening”,   icon: “moon”,     label: “Eve” },
];

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, zIndex: 60,
display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, justifyContent: “flex-end” }}>
<motion.div onClick={onClose}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, background: “rgba(10,8,22,0.52)” }} />

```
          background: "transparent", border: "none", cursor: "pointer",
          fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, borderRadius: 14 }}>
        Cancel
      </button>
    </>)}
  </motion.div>
</motion.div>
```

);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
PROJECT ADD SHEET — auto AI step generation
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════*/
function ProjectAddSheet({ onClose, prefillText = “” }) {
const [title, setTitle]                   = useState(prefillText);
const [emoji, setEmoji]                   = useState(“📁”);
const [primaryArea, setPrimaryArea]       = useState(null);
const [areaConfirmed, setAreaConfirmed]   = useState(false);
const [expandArea, setExpandArea]         = useState(false);
const [steps, setSteps]                   = useState([]);
const [newStep, setNewStep]               = useState(””);
const [added, setAdded]                   = useState(false);
const [aiLoading, setAiLoading]           = useState(false);
const [autoRan, setAutoRan]               = useState(false);
const inputRef = useRef(null);
const stepRef  = useRef(null);

const nlpSuggestion = title.length >= 3 ? suggestArea(title) : null;
useEffect(() => { if (nlpSuggestion && !areaConfirmed) setPrimaryArea(nlpSuggestion); }, [nlpSuggestion]);
useEffect(() => { setTimeout(() => inputRef.current?.focus(), 200); }, []);

// Auto-generate steps when opened with prefill
useEffect(() => {
if (prefillText && prefillText.trim().length > 3 && !autoRan) {
setAutoRan(true);
setTimeout(() => generateSteps(prefillText), 700);
}
}, []);

const suggestedAreaData = primaryArea ? ITEM_AREAS[primaryArea] : null;

const addStep = () => {
if (!newStep.trim()) return;
setSteps(prev => […prev, { id: “s-” + Date.now(), title: newStep.trim(), done: false }]);
setNewStep(””); setTimeout(() => stepRef.current?.focus(), 40);
};
const removeStep = id => setSteps(prev => prev.filter(s => s.id !== id));
const canSave = title.trim() && primaryArea;

async function generateSteps(t) {
const titleToUse = t || title;
if (!titleToUse.trim() || aiLoading) return;
setAiLoading(true);
try {
const existing = steps.map(s => s.title).join(”, “);
const prompt = existing
? “Project: "” + titleToUse + “"\nExisting tasks: “ + existing + “\nGenerate 3-5 MORE missing tasks. Reply JSON only: {"tasks":["task 1"],"emoji":"emoji"}”
: “Project: "” + titleToUse + “"\nGenerate 5-7 concrete actionable tasks. Reply JSON only: {"tasks":["task 1"],"emoji":"emoji","why":"one sentence"}”;
const raw    = await aiAssist(prompt);
const clean  = raw.replace(/`json|`/g, “”).trim();
const parsed = JSON.parse(clean);
if (parsed.tasks?.length) {
setSteps(parsed.tasks.map((t, i) => ({ id: “s-” + Date.now() + i, title: t, done: false })));
}
if (parsed.emoji) setEmoji(parsed.emoji);
} catch(e) {}
setAiLoading(false);
}

const { addItem } = useAppState();

function handleSave() {
if (!canSave) return;
addItem({
id:          “item-” + Date.now(),
title:       title.trim(),
emoji:       emoji,
area:        primaryArea,
status:      “active”,
source:      “self”,
createdAt:   new Date().toISOString(),
steps:       steps.map(s => ({
…s,
status: “todo”, priority: “normal”, effort: “medium”,
assignees: [], blockedBy: [],
})),
});
setAdded(true);
setTimeout(() => onClose(), 1100);
}

const EMOJIS = [“📁”,“🏗️”,“💡”,“🎯”,“🚀”,“📊”,“🔧”,“🎨”,“📝”,“🏃”,“💪”,“🌱”,“🏠”,“✈️”,“💰”,“📚”];

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, zIndex: 62,
display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”, justifyContent: “flex-end” }}>
<motion.div onClick={onClose}
style={{ position: “absolute”, inset: 0, background: “rgba(10,8,22,0.44)” }} />
<motion.div initial={{ y: 500 }} animate={{ y: 0 }} exit={{ y: 500 }}
transition={{ type: “spring”, damping: 30, stiffness: 320 }}

function suggestArea(text) {
const t = text.toLowerCase();
const map = [
{ area: “health”,        words: [“run”,“gym”,“workout”,“exercise”,“sleep”,“eat”,“diet”,“water”,“yoga”,“stretch”,“fitness”,“doctor”,“dentist”,“vitamin”,“weight”,“meal”,“nutrition”,“walk”,“swim”,“cycle”,“jog”,“lift”,“protein”,“steps”,“health”,“medicine”,“physio”,“training”,“marathon”,“sport”,“crossfit”,“hike”] },
{ area: “finance”,       words: [“save”,“budget”,“invest”,“money”,“bank”,“pay”,“debt”,“loan”,“tax”,“insurance”,“salary”,“expense”,“bill”,“super”,“mortgage”,“credit”,“income”,“financial”,“savings”,“portfolio”,“shares”,“fund”,“rent”,“spending”,“afford”] },
{ area: “career”,        words: [“work”,“job”,“resume”,“cv”,“meeting”,“email”,“project”,“boss”,“client”,“deadline”,“presentation”,“promotion”,“interview”,“career”,“business”,“office”,“linkedin”,“network”,“skill”,“hire”,“freelance”,“contract”,“startup”,“pitch”] },
{ area: “home”,          words: [“clean”,“fix”,“repair”,“paint”,“garden”,“furniture”,“kitchen”,“bathroom”,“garage”,“lawn”,“organise”,“organize”,“declutter”,“renovate”,“build”,“decor”,“tidy”,“mow”,“plant”,“shed”,“house”,“room”,“shelf”,“storage”,“move”] },
{ area: “relationships”, words: [“call”,“text”,“visit”,“dinner”,“friend”,“family”,“partner”,“date”,“birthday”,“anniversary”,“mum”,“dad”,“kids”,“catch up”,“wedding”,“social”,“coffee”,“meet”,“reconnect”,“relationship”,“parents”,“siblings”,“couple”] },
{ area: “learning”,      words: [“read”,“book”,“course”,“study”,“learn”,“practice”,“skill”,“certificate”,“degree”,“lesson”,“class”,“podcast”,“tutorial”,“chapter”,“language”,“spanish”,“french”,“mandarin”,“code”,“program”,“write”,“research”,“exam”] },
{ area: “fun”,           words: [“travel”,“trip”,“holiday”,“game”,“movie”,“sport”,“concert”,“hobby”,“photography”,“music”,“art”,“cook”,“bake”,“play”,“explore”,“adventure”,“hike”,“surf”,“festival”,“escape”,“cinema”,“theatre”,“create”] },
{ area: “spirituality”,  words: [“meditate”,“journal”,“reflect”,“gratitude”,“prayer”,“mindful”,“breathe”,“calm”,“peace”,“spiritual”,“clarity”,“intention”,“ritual”,“morning routine”,“evening routine”,“stillness”] },
];
for (const { area, words } of map) {
if (words.some(w => t.includes(w))) return area;
}
return null;
}

function AreaPicker({ selected, onSelect, label = “Life area”, required = false, excludeArea = null }) {
const areas = Object.entries(ITEM_AREAS)
.filter(([id]) => id !== excludeArea)
.map(([id, a]) => ({ id, …a }));
return (
<div>
{label && (
<div style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 8,
textTransform: “uppercase”, letterSpacing: 0.3, display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 4 }}>
{label}
{required && <span style={{ color: T.brand, fontSize: 10 }}>required</span>}
</div>
)}
<div style={{ display: “grid”, gridTemplateColumns: “repeat(4, 1fr)”, gap: 6 }}>
{areas.map(a => {
const sel = selected === a.id;
return (
<button key={a.id} onClick={() => onSelect(sel ? null : a.id)}
style={{ padding: “10px 4px”, borderRadius: 12,
border: sel ? `2px solid ${a.c}` : `1px solid ${T.sep}`,
background: sel ? `${a.c}10` : “white”,
cursor: “pointer”, display: “flex”, flexDirection: “column”,
alignItems: “center”, gap: 4, transition: “all 0.15s” }}>
<span style={{ fontSize: 18 }}>{a.e}</span>
<span style={{ fontSize: 9, fontWeight: 700, color: sel ? a.c : T.t3,
textAlign: “center”, lineHeight: 1.2 }}>
{a.n.split(” “)[0]}
</span>
</button>
);
})}
</div>
</div>
);
}

function SecondaryAreaPicker({ primaryArea, selected, onToggle }) {
const areas = Object.entries(ITEM_AREAS)
.filter(([id]) => id !== primaryArea)
.map(([id, a]) => ({ id, …a }));
return (
<div>
<div style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600, color: T.t3, marginBottom: 8,
textTransform: “uppercase”, letterSpacing: 0.3 }}>
Also improves <span style={{ fontWeight: 400, textTransform: “none” }}>(optional · max 2)</span>
</div>
<div style={{ display: “flex”, flexWrap: “wrap”, gap: 6 }}>
{areas.map(a => {
const sel = selected.includes(a.id);
const disabled = !sel && selected.length >= 2;
return (
<button key={a.id} onClick={() => !disabled && onToggle(a.id)}
style={{ padding: “5px 10px”, borderRadius: 8,
border: sel ? `1.5px solid ${a.c}` : `1px solid ${T.sep}`,
background: sel ? `${a.c}08` : disabled ? T.fill : “white”,
cursor: disabled ? “default” : “pointer”, opacity: disabled ? 0.4 : 1,
display: “flex”, alignItems: “center”, gap: 5 }}>
<span style={{ fontSize: 13 }}>{a.e}</span>
<span style={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600, color: sel ? a.c : T.t2 }}>
{a.n.split(” “)[0]}
</span>
</button>
);
})}
</div>
</div>
);
}

<AppStateProvider>
<AppShell />

);
}

```
            borderRadius: 20,
            transition: "background 0.18s ease",
            position: "relative", zIndex: 1,
          }}>
          <TabIcon name={t.id} active={active} />
          <span style={{
            fontSize: 10, fontWeight: active ? 750 : 500,
            color: active ? T.brand : T.t3,
            letterSpacing: active ? -0.2 : 0,
            lineHeight: 1,
          }}>{t.label}</span>
        </motion.button>
      );
    })}
  </div>

  {/* FAB overlays */}
  <AnimatePresence>
    {showAdd === "sheet" && (
      <FabActionSheet
        onProject={(t) => { setAddPrefill(t); setShowAdd("project"); }}
        onJourney={() => setShowAdd("journey")}
        onClose={() => setShowAdd(false)}
      />
    )}
    {showAdd === "project" && (
      <ProjectAddSheet prefillText={addPrefill} onClose={() => setShowAdd(false)} />
    )}
    {showAdd === "journey" && (
      <ProgramBuilder onClose={() => setShowAdd(false)} onSave={() => setShowAdd(false)} />
    )}
  </AnimatePresence>

  {/* Profile overlay (accessed via avatar, not tab) */}
  <AnimatePresence>
    {showProfile && (
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }}
        transition={{ type: "spring", damping: 26, stiffness: 300 }}
        style={{ position: "absolute", inset: 0, zIndex: 40, background: T.meshBg,
          display: "flex", flexDirection: "column" }}>
        <div style={{
          display: "flex", alignItems: "center", padding: "14px 16px 12px",
          background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.85)", backdropFilter: T.blur, WebkitBackdropFilter: T.blur,
          borderBottom: `0.5px solid ${T.sep}`, flexShrink: 0,
        }}>
          <motion.button whileTap={{ scale: 0.9 }} onClick={() => setShowProfile(false)}
            style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 3, background: "none",
              border: "none", cursor: "pointer", padding: "4px 0" }}>
            <svg width={20} height={20} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke={T.brand} strokeWidth={2.5} strokeLinecap="round">
              <polyline points="15 18 9 12 15 6" />
            </svg>
          </motion.button>
          <div style={{ flex: 1, textAlign: "center" }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>Profile</div>
          </div>
          <div style={{ width: 28 }} />
        </div>
        <div style={{ flex: 1, overflow: "hidden" }}>
          <ProfileScreen />
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    )}
  </AnimatePresence>
</div>
```

);
}
